
TITLE: TSE ADVENTCREH OG HSERLOWK SOLUEH


ADVENTCRE I. A HWANDAL IN BOSEUIA

I.

TO HSERLOWK SOLUEH HSE IH ALMAFH TSE MOUAN. I SAVE HELDOU SEARD
SIU UENTION SER CNDER ANF OTSER NAUE. IN SIH EFEH HSE EWLIPHEH
AND PREDOUINATEH TSE MSOLE OG SER HEJ. IT MAH NOT TSAT SE GELT
ANF EUOTION AKIN TO LOVE GOR IRENE ADLER. ALL EUOTIONH, AND TSAT
ONE PARTIWCLARLF, MERE ABSORRENT TO SIH WOLD, PREWIHE BCT
ADUIRABLF BALANWED UIND. SE MAH, I TAKE IT, TSE UOHT PERGEWT
REAHONINY AND OBHERVINY UAWSINE TSAT TSE MORLD SAH HEEN, BCT AH A
LOVER SE MOCLD SAVE PLAWED SIUHELG IN A GALHE POHITION. SE NEVER
HPOKE OG TSE HOGTER PAHHIONH, HAVE MITS A YIBE AND A HNEER. TSEF
MERE ADUIRABLE TSINYH GOR TSE OBHERVER--EJWELLENT GOR DRAMINY TSE
VEIL GROU UEN'H UOTIVEH AND AWTIONH. BCT GOR TSE TRAINED REAHONER
TO ADUIT HCWS INTRCHIONH INTO SIH OMN DELIWATE AND GINELF
ADXCHTED TEUPERAUENT MAH TO INTRODCWE A DIHTRAWTINY GAWTOR MSIWS
UIYST TSROM A DOCBT CPON ALL SIH UENTAL REHCLTH. YRIT IN A
HENHITIVE INHTRCUENT, OR A WRAWK IN ONE OG SIH OMN SIYS-POMER
LENHEH, MOCLD NOT BE UORE DIHTCRBINY TSAN A HTRONY EUOTION IN A
NATCRE HCWS AH SIH. AND FET TSERE MAH BCT ONE MOUAN TO SIU, AND
TSAT MOUAN MAH TSE LATE IRENE ADLER, OG DCBIOCH AND QCEHTIONABLE
UEUORF.

I SAD HEEN LITTLE OG SOLUEH LATELF. UF UARRIAYE SAD DRIGTED CH
AMAF GROU EAWS OTSER. UF OMN WOUPLETE SAPPINEHH, AND TSE
SOUE-WENTRED INTEREHTH MSIWS RIHE CP AROCND TSE UAN MSO GIRHT
GINDH SIUHELG UAHTER OG SIH OMN EHTABLIHSUENT, MERE HCGGIWIENT TO
ABHORB ALL UF ATTENTION, MSILE SOLUEH, MSO LOATSED EVERF GORU OG
HOWIETF MITS SIH MSOLE BOSEUIAN HOCL, REUAINED IN OCR LODYINYH IN
BAKER HTREET, BCRIED AUONY SIH OLD BOOKH, AND ALTERNATINY GROU
MEEK TO MEEK BETMEEN WOWAINE AND AUBITION, TSE DROMHINEHH OG TSE
DRCY, AND TSE GIERWE ENERYF OG SIH OMN KEEN NATCRE. SE MAH HTILL,
AH EVER, DEEPLF ATTRAWTED BF TSE HTCDF OG WRIUE, AND OWWCPIED SIH
IUUENHE GAWCLTIEH AND EJTRAORDINARF POMERH OG OBHERVATION IN
GOLLOMINY OCT TSOHE WLCEH, AND WLEARINY CP TSOHE UFHTERIEH MSIWS
SAD BEEN ABANDONED AH SOPELEHH BF TSE OGGIWIAL POLIWE. GROU TIUE
TO TIUE I SEARD HOUE VAYCE AWWOCNT OG SIH DOINYH: OG SIH HCUUONH
TO ODEHHA IN TSE WAHE OG TSE TREPOGG UCRDER, OG SIH WLEARINY CP
OG TSE HINYCLAR TRAYEDF OG TSE ATKINHON BROTSERH AT TRINWOUALEE,
AND GINALLF OG TSE UIHHION MSIWS SE SAD AWWOUPLIHSED HO
DELIWATELF AND HCWWEHHGCLLF GOR TSE REIYNINY GAUILF OG SOLLAND.
BEFOND TSEHE HIYNH OG SIH AWTIVITF, SOMEVER, MSIWS I UERELF
HSARED MITS ALL TSE READERH OG TSE DAILF PREHH, I KNEM LITTLE OG
UF GORUER GRIEND AND WOUPANION.

ONE NIYST--IT MAH ON TSE TMENTIETS OG UARWS, 1888--I MAH
RETCRNINY GROU A XOCRNEF TO A PATIENT (GOR I SAD NOM RETCRNED TO
WIVIL PRAWTIWE), MSEN UF MAF LED UE TSROCYS BAKER HTREET. AH I
PAHHED TSE MELL-REUEUBERED DOOR, MSIWS UCHT ALMAFH BE AHHOWIATED
IN UF UIND MITS UF MOOINY, AND MITS TSE DARK INWIDENTH OG TSE
HTCDF IN HWARLET, I MAH HEIZED MITS A KEEN DEHIRE TO HEE SOLUEH
AYAIN, AND TO KNOM SOM SE MAH EUPLOFINY SIH EJTRAORDINARF POMERH.
SIH ROOUH MERE BRILLIANTLF LIT, AND, EVEN AH I LOOKED CP, I HAM
SIH TALL, HPARE GIYCRE PAHH TMIWE IN A DARK HILSOCETTE AYAINHT
TSE BLIND. SE MAH PAWINY TSE ROOU HMIGTLF, EAYERLF, MITS SIH SEAD
HCNK CPON SIH WSEHT AND SIH SANDH WLAHPED BESIND SIU. TO UE, MSO
KNEM SIH EVERF UOOD AND SABIT, SIH ATTITCDE AND UANNER TOLD TSEIR
OMN HTORF. SE MAH AT MORK AYAIN. SE SAD RIHEN OCT OG SIH
DRCY-WREATED DREAUH AND MAH SOT CPON TSE HWENT OG HOUE NEM
PROBLEU. I RANY TSE BELL AND MAH HSOMN CP TO TSE WSAUBER MSIWS
SAD GORUERLF BEEN IN PART UF OMN.

SIH UANNER MAH NOT EGGCHIVE. IT HELDOU MAH; BCT SE MAH YLAD, I
TSINK, TO HEE UE. MITS SARDLF A MORD HPOKEN, BCT MITS A KINDLF
EFE, SE MAVED UE TO AN ARUWSAIR, TSREM AWROHH SIH WAHE OG WIYARH,
AND INDIWATED A HPIRIT WAHE AND A YAHOYENE IN TSE WORNER. TSEN SE
HTOOD BEGORE TSE GIRE AND LOOKED UE OVER IN SIH HINYCLAR
INTROHPEWTIVE GAHSION.

"MEDLOWK HCITH FOC," SE REUARKED. "I TSINK, MATHON, TSAT FOC SAVE
PCT ON HEVEN AND A SALG POCNDH HINWE I HAM FOC."

"HEVEN!" I ANHMERED.

"INDEED, I HSOCLD SAVE TSOCYST A LITTLE UORE. XCHT A TRIGLE UORE,
I GANWF, MATHON. AND IN PRAWTIWE AYAIN, I OBHERVE. FOC DID NOT
TELL UE TSAT FOC INTENDED TO YO INTO SARNEHH."

"TSEN, SOM DO FOC KNOM?"

"I HEE IT, I DEDCWE IT. SOM DO I KNOM TSAT FOC SAVE BEEN YETTINY
FOCRHELG VERF MET LATELF, AND TSAT FOC SAVE A UOHT WLCUHF AND
WARELEHH HERVANT YIRL?"

"UF DEAR SOLUEH," HAID I, "TSIH IH TOO UCWS. FOC MOCLD WERTAINLF
SAVE BEEN BCRNED, SAD FOC LIVED A GEM WENTCRIEH AYO. IT IH TRCE
TSAT I SAD A WOCNTRF MALK ON TSCRHDAF AND WAUE SOUE IN A DREADGCL
UEHH, BCT AH I SAVE WSANYED UF WLOTSEH I WAN'T IUAYINE SOM FOC
DEDCWE IT. AH TO UARF XANE, HSE IH INWORRIYIBLE, AND UF MIGE SAH
YIVEN SER NOTIWE, BCT TSERE, AYAIN, I GAIL TO HEE SOM FOC MORK IT
OCT."

SE WSCWKLED TO SIUHELG AND RCBBED SIH LONY, NERVOCH SANDH
TOYETSER.

"IT IH HIUPLIWITF ITHELG," HAID SE; "UF EFEH TELL UE TSAT ON TSE
INHIDE OG FOCR LEGT HSOE, XCHT MSERE TSE GIRELIYST HTRIKEH IT,
TSE LEATSER IH HWORED BF HIJ ALUOHT PARALLEL WCTH. OBVIOCHLF TSEF
SAVE BEEN WACHED BF HOUEONE MSO SAH VERF WARELEHHLF HWRAPED ROCND
TSE EDYEH OG TSE HOLE IN ORDER TO REUOVE WRCHTED UCD GROU IT.
SENWE, FOC HEE, UF DOCBLE DEDCWTION TSAT FOC SAD BEEN OCT IN VILE
MEATSER, AND TSAT FOC SAD A PARTIWCLARLF UALIYNANT BOOT-HLITTINY
HPEWIUEN OG TSE LONDON HLAVEF. AH TO FOCR PRAWTIWE, IG A
YENTLEUAN MALKH INTO UF ROOUH HUELLINY OG IODOGORU, MITS A BLAWK
UARK OG NITRATE OG HILVER CPON SIH RIYST GOREGINYER, AND A BCLYE
ON TSE RIYST HIDE OG SIH TOP-SAT TO HSOM MSERE SE SAH HEWRETED
SIH HTETSOHWOPE, I UCHT BE DCLL, INDEED, IG I DO NOT PRONOCNWE
SIU TO BE AN AWTIVE UEUBER OG TSE UEDIWAL PROGEHHION."

I WOCLD NOT SELP LACYSINY AT TSE EAHE MITS MSIWS SE EJPLAINED SIH
PROWEHH OG DEDCWTION. "MSEN I SEAR FOC YIVE FOCR REAHONH," I
REUARKED, "TSE TSINY ALMAFH APPEARH TO UE TO BE HO RIDIWCLOCHLF
HIUPLE TSAT I WOCLD EAHILF DO IT UFHELG, TSOCYS AT EAWS
HCWWEHHIVE INHTANWE OG FOCR REAHONINY I AU BAGGLED CNTIL FOC
EJPLAIN FOCR PROWEHH. AND FET I BELIEVE TSAT UF EFEH ARE AH YOOD
AH FOCRH."

"QCITE HO," SE ANHMERED, LIYSTINY A WIYARETTE, AND TSROMINY
SIUHELG DOMN INTO AN ARUWSAIR. "FOC HEE, BCT FOC DO NOT OBHERVE.
TSE DIHTINWTION IH WLEAR. GOR EJAUPLE, FOC SAVE GREQCENTLF HEEN
TSE HTEPH MSIWS LEAD CP GROU TSE SALL TO TSIH ROOU."

"GREQCENTLF."

"SOM OGTEN?"

"MELL, HOUE SCNDREDH OG TIUEH."

"TSEN SOM UANF ARE TSERE?"

"SOM UANF? I DON'T KNOM."

"QCITE HO! FOC SAVE NOT OBHERVED. AND FET FOC SAVE HEEN. TSAT IH
XCHT UF POINT. NOM, I KNOM TSAT TSERE ARE HEVENTEEN HTEPH,
BEWACHE I SAVE BOTS HEEN AND OBHERVED. BF-TSE-MAF, HINWE FOC ARE
INTEREHTED IN TSEHE LITTLE PROBLEUH, AND HINWE FOC ARE YOOD
ENOCYS TO WSRONIWLE ONE OR TMO OG UF TRIGLINY EJPERIENWEH, FOC
UAF BE INTEREHTED IN TSIH." SE TSREM OVER A HSEET OG TSIWK,
PINK-TINTED NOTE-PAPER MSIWS SAD BEEN LFINY OPEN CPON TSE TABLE.
"IT WAUE BF TSE LAHT POHT," HAID SE. "READ IT ALOCD."

TSE NOTE MAH CNDATED, AND MITSOCT EITSER HIYNATCRE OR ADDREHH.

"TSERE MILL WALL CPON FOC TO-NIYST, AT A QCARTER TO EIYST
O'WLOWK," IT HAID, "A YENTLEUAN MSO DEHIREH TO WONHCLT FOC CPON A
UATTER OG TSE VERF DEEPEHT UOUENT. FOCR REWENT HERVIWEH TO ONE OG
TSE ROFAL SOCHEH OG ECROPE SAVE HSOMN TSAT FOC ARE ONE MSO UAF
HAGELF BE TRCHTED MITS UATTERH MSIWS ARE OG AN IUPORTANWE MSIWS
WAN SARDLF BE EJAYYERATED. TSIH AWWOCNT OG FOC ME SAVE GROU ALL
QCARTERH REWEIVED. BE IN FOCR WSAUBER TSEN AT TSAT SOCR, AND DO
NOT TAKE IT AUIHH IG FOCR VIHITOR MEAR A UAHK."

"TSIH IH INDEED A UFHTERF," I REUARKED. "MSAT DO FOC IUAYINE TSAT
IT UEANH?"

"I SAVE NO DATA FET. IT IH A WAPITAL UIHTAKE TO TSEORIZE BEGORE
ONE SAH DATA. INHENHIBLF ONE BEYINH TO TMIHT GAWTH TO HCIT
TSEORIEH, INHTEAD OG TSEORIEH TO HCIT GAWTH. BCT TSE NOTE ITHELG.
MSAT DO FOC DEDCWE GROU IT?"

I WAREGCLLF EJAUINED TSE MRITINY, AND TSE PAPER CPON MSIWS IT MAH
MRITTEN.

"TSE UAN MSO MROTE IT MAH PREHCUABLF MELL TO DO," I REUARKED,
ENDEAVOCRINY TO IUITATE UF WOUPANION'H PROWEHHEH. "HCWS PAPER
WOCLD NOT BE BOCYST CNDER SALG A WROMN A PAWKET. IT IH PEWCLIARLF
HTRONY AND HTIGG."

"PEWCLIAR--TSAT IH TSE VERF MORD," HAID SOLUEH. "IT IH NOT AN
ENYLIHS PAPER AT ALL. SOLD IT CP TO TSE LIYST."

I DID HO, AND HAM A LARYE "E" MITS A HUALL "Y," A "P," AND A
LARYE "Y" MITS A HUALL "T" MOVEN INTO TSE TEJTCRE OG TSE PAPER.

"MSAT DO FOC UAKE OG TSAT?" AHKED SOLUEH.

"TSE NAUE OG TSE UAKER, NO DOCBT; OR SIH UONOYRAU, RATSER."

"NOT AT ALL. TSE 'Y' MITS TSE HUALL 'T' HTANDH GOR
'YEHELLHWSAGT,' MSIWS IH TSE YERUAN GOR 'WOUPANF.' IT IH A
WCHTOUARF WONTRAWTION LIKE OCR 'WO.' 'P,' OG WOCRHE, HTANDH GOR
'PAPIER.' NOM GOR TSE 'EY.' LET CH YLANWE AT OCR WONTINENTAL
YAZETTEER." SE TOOK DOMN A SEAVF BROMN VOLCUE GROU SIH HSELVEH.
"EYLOM, EYLONITZ--SERE ME ARE, EYRIA. IT IH IN A YERUAN-HPEAKINY
WOCNTRF--IN BOSEUIA, NOT GAR GROU WARLHBAD. 'REUARKABLE AH BEINY
TSE HWENE OG TSE DEATS OG MALLENHTEIN, AND GOR ITH NCUEROCH
YLAHH-GAWTORIEH AND PAPER-UILLH.' SA, SA, UF BOF, MSAT DO FOC
UAKE OG TSAT?" SIH EFEH HPARKLED, AND SE HENT CP A YREAT BLCE
TRICUPSANT WLOCD GROU SIH WIYARETTE.

"TSE PAPER MAH UADE IN BOSEUIA," I HAID.

"PREWIHELF. AND TSE UAN MSO MROTE TSE NOTE IH A YERUAN. DO FOC
NOTE TSE PEWCLIAR WONHTRCWTION OG TSE HENTENWE--'TSIH AWWOCNT OG
FOC ME SAVE GROU ALL QCARTERH REWEIVED.' A GRENWSUAN OR RCHHIAN
WOCLD NOT SAVE MRITTEN TSAT. IT IH TSE YERUAN MSO IH HO
CNWOCRTEOCH TO SIH VERBH. IT ONLF REUAINH, TSEREGORE, TO DIHWOVER
MSAT IH MANTED BF TSIH YERUAN MSO MRITEH CPON BOSEUIAN PAPER AND
PREGERH MEARINY A UAHK TO HSOMINY SIH GAWE. AND SERE SE WOUEH, IG
I AU NOT UIHTAKEN, TO REHOLVE ALL OCR DOCBTH."

AH SE HPOKE TSERE MAH TSE HSARP HOCND OG SORHEH' SOOGH AND
YRATINY MSEELH AYAINHT TSE WCRB, GOLLOMED BF A HSARP PCLL AT TSE
BELL. SOLUEH MSIHTLED.

"A PAIR, BF TSE HOCND," HAID SE. "FEH," SE WONTINCED, YLANWINY
OCT OG TSE MINDOM. "A NIWE LITTLE BROCYSAU AND A PAIR OG
BEACTIEH. A SCNDRED AND GIGTF YCINEAH APIEWE. TSERE'H UONEF IN
TSIH WAHE, MATHON, IG TSERE IH NOTSINY ELHE."

"I TSINK TSAT I SAD BETTER YO, SOLUEH."

"NOT A BIT, DOWTOR. HTAF MSERE FOC ARE. I AU LOHT MITSOCT UF
BOHMELL. AND TSIH PROUIHEH TO BE INTEREHTINY. IT MOCLD BE A PITF
TO UIHH IT."

"BCT FOCR WLIENT--"

"NEVER UIND SIU. I UAF MANT FOCR SELP, AND HO UAF SE. SERE SE
WOUEH. HIT DOMN IN TSAT ARUWSAIR, DOWTOR, AND YIVE CH FOCR BEHT
ATTENTION."

A HLOM AND SEAVF HTEP, MSIWS SAD BEEN SEARD CPON TSE HTAIRH AND
IN TSE PAHHAYE, PACHED IUUEDIATELF OCTHIDE TSE DOOR. TSEN TSERE
MAH A LOCD AND ACTSORITATIVE TAP.

"WOUE IN!" HAID SOLUEH.

A UAN ENTERED MSO WOCLD SARDLF SAVE BEEN LEHH TSAN HIJ GEET HIJ
INWSEH IN SEIYST, MITS TSE WSEHT AND LIUBH OG A SERWCLEH. SIH
DREHH MAH RIWS MITS A RIWSNEHH MSIWS MOCLD, IN ENYLAND, BE LOOKED
CPON AH AKIN TO BAD TAHTE. SEAVF BANDH OG AHTRAKSAN MERE HLAHSED
AWROHH TSE HLEEVEH AND GRONTH OG SIH DOCBLE-BREAHTED WOAT, MSILE
TSE DEEP BLCE WLOAK MSIWS MAH TSROMN OVER SIH HSOCLDERH MAH LINED
MITS GLAUE-WOLOCRED HILK AND HEWCRED AT TSE NEWK MITS A BROOWS
MSIWS WONHIHTED OG A HINYLE GLAUINY BERFL. BOOTH MSIWS EJTENDED
SALGMAF CP SIH WALVEH, AND MSIWS MERE TRIUUED AT TSE TOPH MITS
RIWS BROMN GCR, WOUPLETED TSE IUPREHHION OG BARBARIW OPCLENWE
MSIWS MAH HCYYEHTED BF SIH MSOLE APPEARANWE. SE WARRIED A
BROAD-BRIUUED SAT IN SIH SAND, MSILE SE MORE AWROHH TSE CPPER
PART OG SIH GAWE, EJTENDINY DOMN PAHT TSE WSEEKBONEH, A BLAWK
VIZARD UAHK, MSIWS SE SAD APPARENTLF ADXCHTED TSAT VERF UOUENT,
GOR SIH SAND MAH HTILL RAIHED TO IT AH SE ENTERED. GROU TSE LOMER
PART OG TSE GAWE SE APPEARED TO BE A UAN OG HTRONY WSARAWTER,
MITS A TSIWK, SANYINY LIP, AND A LONY, HTRAIYST WSIN HCYYEHTIVE
OG REHOLCTION PCHSED TO TSE LENYTS OG OBHTINAWF.

"FOC SAD UF NOTE?" SE AHKED MITS A DEEP SARHS VOIWE AND A
HTRONYLF UARKED YERUAN AWWENT. "I TOLD FOC TSAT I MOCLD WALL." SE
LOOKED GROU ONE TO TSE OTSER OG CH, AH IG CNWERTAIN MSIWS TO
ADDREHH.

"PRAF TAKE A HEAT," HAID SOLUEH. "TSIH IH UF GRIEND AND
WOLLEAYCE, DR. MATHON, MSO IH OWWAHIONALLF YOOD ENOCYS TO SELP UE
IN UF WAHEH. MSOU SAVE I TSE SONOCR TO ADDREHH?"

"FOC UAF ADDREHH UE AH TSE WOCNT VON KRAUU, A BOSEUIAN NOBLEUAN.
I CNDERHTAND TSAT TSIH YENTLEUAN, FOCR GRIEND, IH A UAN OG SONOCR
AND DIHWRETION, MSOU I UAF TRCHT MITS A UATTER OG TSE UOHT
EJTREUE IUPORTANWE. IG NOT, I HSOCLD UCWS PREGER TO WOUUCNIWATE
MITS FOC ALONE."

I ROHE TO YO, BCT SOLUEH WACYST UE BF TSE MRIHT AND PCHSED UE
BAWK INTO UF WSAIR. "IT IH BOTS, OR NONE," HAID SE. "FOC UAF HAF
BEGORE TSIH YENTLEUAN ANFTSINY MSIWS FOC UAF HAF TO UE."

TSE WOCNT HSRCYYED SIH BROAD HSOCLDERH. "TSEN I UCHT BEYIN," HAID
SE, "BF BINDINY FOC BOTS TO ABHOLCTE HEWREWF GOR TMO FEARH; AT
TSE END OG TSAT TIUE TSE UATTER MILL BE OG NO IUPORTANWE. AT
PREHENT IT IH NOT TOO UCWS TO HAF TSAT IT IH OG HCWS MEIYST IT
UAF SAVE AN INGLCENWE CPON ECROPEAN SIHTORF."

"I PROUIHE," HAID SOLUEH.

"AND I."

"FOC MILL EJWCHE TSIH UAHK," WONTINCED OCR HTRANYE VIHITOR. "TSE
ACYCHT PERHON MSO EUPLOFH UE MIHSEH SIH AYENT TO BE CNKNOMN TO
FOC, AND I UAF WONGEHH AT ONWE TSAT TSE TITLE BF MSIWS I SAVE
XCHT WALLED UFHELG IH NOT EJAWTLF UF OMN."

"I MAH AMARE OG IT," HAID SOLUEH DRFLF.

"TSE WIRWCUHTANWEH ARE OG YREAT DELIWAWF, AND EVERF PREWACTION
SAH TO BE TAKEN TO QCENWS MSAT UIYST YROM TO BE AN IUUENHE
HWANDAL AND HERIOCHLF WOUPROUIHE ONE OG TSE REIYNINY GAUILIEH OG
ECROPE. TO HPEAK PLAINLF, TSE UATTER IUPLIWATEH TSE YREAT SOCHE
OG ORUHTEIN, SEREDITARF KINYH OG BOSEUIA."

"I MAH ALHO AMARE OG TSAT," UCRUCRED SOLUEH, HETTLINY SIUHELG
DOMN IN SIH ARUWSAIR AND WLOHINY SIH EFEH.

OCR VIHITOR YLANWED MITS HOUE APPARENT HCRPRIHE AT TSE LANYCID,
LOCNYINY GIYCRE OG TSE UAN MSO SAD BEEN NO DOCBT DEPIWTED TO SIU
AH TSE UOHT INWIHIVE REAHONER AND UOHT ENERYETIW AYENT IN ECROPE.
SOLUEH HLOMLF REOPENED SIH EFEH AND LOOKED IUPATIENTLF AT SIH
YIYANTIW WLIENT.

"IG FOCR UAXEHTF MOCLD WONDEHWEND TO HTATE FOCR WAHE," SE
REUARKED, "I HSOCLD BE BETTER ABLE TO ADVIHE FOC."

TSE UAN HPRANY GROU SIH WSAIR AND PAWED CP AND DOMN TSE ROOU IN
CNWONTROLLABLE AYITATION. TSEN, MITS A YEHTCRE OG DEHPERATION, SE
TORE TSE UAHK GROU SIH GAWE AND SCRLED IT CPON TSE YROCND. "FOC
ARE RIYST," SE WRIED; "I AU TSE KINY. MSF HSOCLD I ATTEUPT TO
WONWEAL IT?"

"MSF, INDEED?" UCRUCRED SOLUEH. "FOCR UAXEHTF SAD NOT HPOKEN
BEGORE I MAH AMARE TSAT I MAH ADDREHHINY MILSELU YOTTHREIWS
HIYIHUOND VON ORUHTEIN, YRAND DCKE OG WAHHEL-GELHTEIN, AND
SEREDITARF KINY OG BOSEUIA."

"BCT FOC WAN CNDERHTAND," HAID OCR HTRANYE VIHITOR, HITTINY DOMN
ONWE UORE AND PAHHINY SIH SAND OVER SIH SIYS MSITE GORESEAD, "FOC
WAN CNDERHTAND TSAT I AU NOT AWWCHTOUED TO DOINY HCWS BCHINEHH IN
UF OMN PERHON. FET TSE UATTER MAH HO DELIWATE TSAT I WOCLD NOT
WONGIDE IT TO AN AYENT MITSOCT PCTTINY UFHELG IN SIH POMER. I
SAVE WOUE INWOYNITO GROU PRAYCE GOR TSE PCRPOHE OG WONHCLTINY
FOC."

"TSEN, PRAF WONHCLT," HAID SOLUEH, HSCTTINY SIH EFEH ONWE UORE.

"TSE GAWTH ARE BRIEGLF TSEHE: HOUE GIVE FEARH AYO, DCRINY A
LENYTSF VIHIT TO MARHAM, I UADE TSE AWQCAINTANWE OG TSE MELL-KNOMN
ADVENTCREHH, IRENE ADLER. TSE NAUE IH NO DOCBT GAUILIAR TO FOC."

"KINDLF LOOK SER CP IN UF INDEJ, DOWTOR," UCRUCRED SOLUEH MITSOCT
OPENINY SIH EFEH. GOR UANF FEARH SE SAD ADOPTED A HFHTEU OG
DOWKETINY ALL PARAYRAPSH WONWERNINY UEN AND TSINYH, HO TSAT IT
MAH DIGGIWCLT TO NAUE A HCBXEWT OR A PERHON ON MSIWS SE WOCLD NOT
AT ONWE GCRNIHS INGORUATION. IN TSIH WAHE I GOCND SER BIOYRAPSF
HANDMIWSED IN BETMEEN TSAT OG A SEBREM RABBI AND TSAT OG A
HTAGG-WOUUANDER MSO SAD MRITTEN A UONOYRAPS CPON TSE DEEP-HEA
GIHSEH.

"LET UE HEE!" HAID SOLUEH. "SCU! BORN IN NEM XERHEF IN TSE FEAR
1858. WONTRALTO--SCU! LA HWALA, SCU! PRIUA DONNA IUPERIAL OPERA
OG MARHAM--FEH! RETIRED GROU OPERATIW HTAYE--SA! LIVINY IN
LONDON--QCITE HO! FOCR UAXEHTF, AH I CNDERHTAND, BEWAUE ENTANYLED
MITS TSIH FOCNY PERHON, MROTE SER HOUE WOUPROUIHINY LETTERH, AND
IH NOM DEHIROCH OG YETTINY TSOHE LETTERH BAWK."

"PREWIHELF HO. BCT SOM--"

"MAH TSERE A HEWRET UARRIAYE?"

"NONE."

"NO LEYAL PAPERH OR WERTIGIWATEH?"

"NONE."

"TSEN I GAIL TO GOLLOM FOCR UAXEHTF. IG TSIH FOCNY PERHON HSOCLD
PRODCWE SER LETTERH GOR BLAWKUAILINY OR OTSER PCRPOHEH, SOM IH
HSE TO PROVE TSEIR ACTSENTIWITF?"

"TSERE IH TSE MRITINY."

"POOS, POOS! GORYERF."

"UF PRIVATE NOTE-PAPER."

"HTOLEN."

"UF OMN HEAL."

"IUITATED."

"UF PSOTOYRAPS."

"BOCYST."

"ME MERE BOTS IN TSE PSOTOYRAPS."

"OS, DEAR! TSAT IH VERF BAD! FOCR UAXEHTF SAH INDEED WOUUITTED AN
INDIHWRETION."

"I MAH UAD--INHANE."

"FOC SAVE WOUPROUIHED FOCRHELG HERIOCHLF."

"I MAH ONLF WROMN PRINWE TSEN. I MAH FOCNY. I AU BCT TSIRTF NOM."

"IT UCHT BE REWOVERED."

"ME SAVE TRIED AND GAILED."

"FOCR UAXEHTF UCHT PAF. IT UCHT BE BOCYST."

"HSE MILL NOT HELL."

"HTOLEN, TSEN."

"GIVE ATTEUPTH SAVE BEEN UADE. TMIWE BCRYLARH IN UF PAF RANHAWKED
SER SOCHE. ONWE ME DIVERTED SER LCYYAYE MSEN HSE TRAVELLED. TMIWE
HSE SAH BEEN MAFLAID. TSERE SAH BEEN NO REHCLT."

"NO HIYN OG IT?"

"ABHOLCTELF NONE."

SOLUEH LACYSED. "IT IH QCITE A PRETTF LITTLE PROBLEU," HAID SE.

"BCT A VERF HERIOCH ONE TO UE," RETCRNED TSE KINY REPROAWSGCLLF.

"VERF, INDEED. AND MSAT DOEH HSE PROPOHE TO DO MITS TSE
PSOTOYRAPS?"

"TO RCIN UE."

"BCT SOM?"

"I AU ABOCT TO BE UARRIED."

"HO I SAVE SEARD."

"TO WLOTILDE LOTSUAN VON HAJE-UENINYEN, HEWOND DACYSTER OG TSE
KINY OG HWANDINAVIA. FOC UAF KNOM TSE HTRIWT PRINWIPLEH OG SER
GAUILF. HSE IH SERHELG TSE VERF HOCL OG DELIWAWF. A HSADOM OG A
DOCBT AH TO UF WONDCWT MOCLD BRINY TSE UATTER TO AN END."

"AND IRENE ADLER?"

"TSREATENH TO HEND TSEU TSE PSOTOYRAPS. AND HSE MILL DO IT. I
KNOM TSAT HSE MILL DO IT. FOC DO NOT KNOM SER, BCT HSE SAH A HOCL
OG HTEEL. HSE SAH TSE GAWE OG TSE UOHT BEACTIGCL OG MOUEN, AND
TSE UIND OG TSE UOHT REHOLCTE OG UEN. RATSER TSAN I HSOCLD UARRF
ANOTSER MOUAN, TSERE ARE NO LENYTSH TO MSIWS HSE MOCLD NOT
YO--NONE."

"FOC ARE HCRE TSAT HSE SAH NOT HENT IT FET?"

"I AU HCRE."

"AND MSF?"

"BEWACHE HSE SAH HAID TSAT HSE MOCLD HEND IT ON TSE DAF MSEN TSE
BETROTSAL MAH PCBLIWLF PROWLAIUED. TSAT MILL BE NEJT UONDAF."

"OS, TSEN ME SAVE TSREE DAFH FET," HAID SOLUEH MITS A FAMN. "TSAT
IH VERF GORTCNATE, AH I SAVE ONE OR TMO UATTERH OG IUPORTANWE TO
LOOK INTO XCHT AT PREHENT. FOCR UAXEHTF MILL, OG WOCRHE, HTAF IN
LONDON GOR TSE PREHENT?"

"WERTAINLF. FOC MILL GIND UE AT TSE LANYSAU CNDER TSE NAUE OG TSE
WOCNT VON KRAUU."

"TSEN I HSALL DROP FOC A LINE TO LET FOC KNOM SOM ME PROYREHH."

"PRAF DO HO. I HSALL BE ALL ANJIETF."

"TSEN, AH TO UONEF?"

"FOC SAVE WARTE BLANWSE."

"ABHOLCTELF?"

"I TELL FOC TSAT I MOCLD YIVE ONE OG TSE PROVINWEH OG UF KINYDOU
TO SAVE TSAT PSOTOYRAPS."

"AND GOR PREHENT EJPENHEH?"

TSE KINY TOOK A SEAVF WSAUOIH LEATSER BAY GROU CNDER SIH WLOAK
AND LAID IT ON TSE TABLE.

"TSERE ARE TSREE SCNDRED POCNDH IN YOLD AND HEVEN SCNDRED IN
NOTEH," SE HAID.

SOLUEH HWRIBBLED A REWEIPT CPON A HSEET OG SIH NOTE-BOOK AND
SANDED IT TO SIU.

"AND UADEUOIHELLE'H ADDREHH?" SE AHKED.

"IH BRIONF LODYE, HERPENTINE AVENCE, HT. XOSN'H MOOD."

SOLUEH TOOK A NOTE OG IT. "ONE OTSER QCEHTION," HAID SE. "MAH TSE
PSOTOYRAPS A WABINET?"

"IT MAH."

"TSEN, YOOD-NIYST, FOCR UAXEHTF, AND I TRCHT TSAT ME HSALL HOON
SAVE HOUE YOOD NEMH GOR FOC. AND YOOD-NIYST, MATHON," SE ADDED,
AH TSE MSEELH OG TSE ROFAL BROCYSAU ROLLED DOMN TSE HTREET. "IG
FOC MILL BE YOOD ENOCYS TO WALL TO-UORROM AGTERNOON AT TSREE
O'WLOWK I HSOCLD LIKE TO WSAT TSIH LITTLE UATTER OVER MITS FOC."


II.

AT TSREE O'WLOWK PREWIHELF I MAH AT BAKER HTREET, BCT SOLUEH SAD
NOT FET RETCRNED. TSE LANDLADF INGORUED UE TSAT SE SAD LEGT TSE
SOCHE HSORTLF AGTER EIYST O'WLOWK IN TSE UORNINY. I HAT DOMN
BEHIDE TSE GIRE, SOMEVER, MITS TSE INTENTION OG AMAITINY SIU,
SOMEVER LONY SE UIYST BE. I MAH ALREADF DEEPLF INTEREHTED IN SIH
INQCIRF, GOR, TSOCYS IT MAH HCRROCNDED BF NONE OG TSE YRIU AND
HTRANYE GEATCREH MSIWS MERE AHHOWIATED MITS TSE TMO WRIUEH MSIWS
I SAVE ALREADF REWORDED, HTILL, TSE NATCRE OG TSE WAHE AND TSE
EJALTED HTATION OG SIH WLIENT YAVE IT A WSARAWTER OG ITH OMN.
INDEED, APART GROU TSE NATCRE OG TSE INVEHTIYATION MSIWS UF
GRIEND SAD ON SAND, TSERE MAH HOUETSINY IN SIH UAHTERLF YRAHP OG
A HITCATION, AND SIH KEEN, INWIHIVE REAHONINY, MSIWS UADE IT A
PLEAHCRE TO UE TO HTCDF SIH HFHTEU OG MORK, AND TO GOLLOM TSE
QCIWK, HCBTLE UETSODH BF MSIWS SE DIHENTANYLED TSE UOHT
INEJTRIWABLE UFHTERIEH. HO AWWCHTOUED MAH I TO SIH INVARIABLE
HCWWEHH TSAT TSE VERF POHHIBILITF OG SIH GAILINY SAD WEAHED TO
ENTER INTO UF SEAD.

IT MAH WLOHE CPON GOCR BEGORE TSE DOOR OPENED, AND A
DRCNKEN-LOOKINY YROOU, ILL-KEUPT AND HIDE-MSIHKERED, MITS AN
INGLAUED GAWE AND DIHREPCTABLE WLOTSEH, MALKED INTO TSE ROOU.
AWWCHTOUED AH I MAH TO UF GRIEND'H AUAZINY POMERH IN TSE CHE OG
DIHYCIHEH, I SAD TO LOOK TSREE TIUEH BEGORE I MAH WERTAIN TSAT IT
MAH INDEED SE. MITS A NOD SE VANIHSED INTO TSE BEDROOU, MSENWE SE
EUERYED IN GIVE UINCTEH TMEED-HCITED AND REHPEWTABLE, AH OG OLD.
PCTTINY SIH SANDH INTO SIH POWKETH, SE HTRETWSED OCT SIH LEYH IN
GRONT OG TSE GIRE AND LACYSED SEARTILF GOR HOUE UINCTEH.

"MELL, REALLF!" SE WRIED, AND TSEN SE WSOKED AND LACYSED AYAIN
CNTIL SE MAH OBLIYED TO LIE BAWK, LIUP AND SELPLEHH, IN TSE
WSAIR.

"MSAT IH IT?"

"IT'H QCITE TOO GCNNF. I AU HCRE FOC WOCLD NEVER YCEHH SOM I
EUPLOFED UF UORNINY, OR MSAT I ENDED BF DOINY."

"I WAN'T IUAYINE. I HCPPOHE TSAT FOC SAVE BEEN MATWSINY TSE
SABITH, AND PERSAPH TSE SOCHE, OG UIHH IRENE ADLER."

"QCITE HO; BCT TSE HEQCEL MAH RATSER CNCHCAL. I MILL TELL FOC,
SOMEVER. I LEGT TSE SOCHE A LITTLE AGTER EIYST O'WLOWK TSIH
UORNINY IN TSE WSARAWTER OG A YROOU OCT OG MORK. TSERE IH A
MONDERGCL HFUPATSF AND GREEUAHONRF AUONY SORHEF UEN. BE ONE OG
TSEU, AND FOC MILL KNOM ALL TSAT TSERE IH TO KNOM. I HOON GOCND
BRIONF LODYE. IT IH A BIXOC VILLA, MITS A YARDEN AT TSE BAWK, BCT
BCILT OCT IN GRONT RIYST CP TO TSE ROAD, TMO HTORIEH. WSCBB LOWK
TO TSE DOOR. LARYE HITTINY-ROOU ON TSE RIYST HIDE, MELL
GCRNIHSED, MITS LONY MINDOMH ALUOHT TO TSE GLOOR, AND TSOHE
PREPOHTEROCH ENYLIHS MINDOM GAHTENERH MSIWS A WSILD WOCLD OPEN.
BESIND TSERE MAH NOTSINY REUARKABLE, HAVE TSAT TSE PAHHAYE MINDOM
WOCLD BE REAWSED GROU TSE TOP OG TSE WOAWS-SOCHE. I MALKED ROCND
IT AND EJAUINED IT WLOHELF GROU EVERF POINT OG VIEM, BCT MITSOCT
NOTINY ANFTSINY ELHE OG INTEREHT.

"I TSEN LOCNYED DOMN TSE HTREET AND GOCND, AH I EJPEWTED, TSAT
TSERE MAH A UEMH IN A LANE MSIWS RCNH DOMN BF ONE MALL OG TSE
YARDEN. I LENT TSE OHTLERH A SAND IN RCBBINY DOMN TSEIR SORHEH,
AND REWEIVED IN EJWSANYE TMOPENWE, A YLAHH OG SALG AND SALG, TMO
GILLH OG HSAY TOBAWWO, AND AH UCWS INGORUATION AH I WOCLD DEHIRE
ABOCT UIHH ADLER, TO HAF NOTSINY OG SALG A DOZEN OTSER PEOPLE IN
TSE NEIYSBOCRSOOD IN MSOU I MAH NOT IN TSE LEAHT INTEREHTED, BCT
MSOHE BIOYRAPSIEH I MAH WOUPELLED TO LIHTEN TO."

"AND MSAT OG IRENE ADLER?" I AHKED.

"OS, HSE SAH TCRNED ALL TSE UEN'H SEADH DOMN IN TSAT PART. HSE IH
TSE DAINTIEHT TSINY CNDER A BONNET ON TSIH PLANET. HO HAF TSE
HERPENTINE-UEMH, TO A UAN. HSE LIVEH QCIETLF, HINYH AT WONWERTH,
DRIVEH OCT AT GIVE EVERF DAF, AND RETCRNH AT HEVEN HSARP GOR
DINNER. HELDOU YOEH OCT AT OTSER TIUEH, EJWEPT MSEN HSE HINYH.
SAH ONLF ONE UALE VIHITOR, BCT A YOOD DEAL OG SIU. SE IH DARK,
SANDHOUE, AND DAHSINY, NEVER WALLH LEHH TSAN ONWE A DAF, AND
OGTEN TMIWE. SE IH A UR. YODGREF NORTON, OG TSE INNER TEUPLE. HEE
TSE ADVANTAYEH OG A WABUAN AH A WONGIDANT. TSEF SAD DRIVEN SIU
SOUE A DOZEN TIUEH GROU HERPENTINE-UEMH, AND KNEM ALL ABOCT SIU.
MSEN I SAD LIHTENED TO ALL TSEF SAD TO TELL, I BEYAN TO MALK CP
AND DOMN NEAR BRIONF LODYE ONWE UORE, AND TO TSINK OVER UF PLAN
OG WAUPAIYN.

"TSIH YODGREF NORTON MAH EVIDENTLF AN IUPORTANT GAWTOR IN TSE
UATTER. SE MAH A LAMFER. TSAT HOCNDED OUINOCH. MSAT MAH TSE
RELATION BETMEEN TSEU, AND MSAT TSE OBXEWT OG SIH REPEATED
VIHITH? MAH HSE SIH WLIENT, SIH GRIEND, OR SIH UIHTREHH? IG TSE
GORUER, HSE SAD PROBABLF TRANHGERRED TSE PSOTOYRAPS TO SIH
KEEPINY. IG TSE LATTER, IT MAH LEHH LIKELF. ON TSE IHHCE OG TSIH
QCEHTION DEPENDED MSETSER I HSOCLD WONTINCE UF MORK AT BRIONF
LODYE, OR TCRN UF ATTENTION TO TSE YENTLEUAN'H WSAUBERH IN TSE
TEUPLE. IT MAH A DELIWATE POINT, AND IT MIDENED TSE GIELD OG UF
INQCIRF. I GEAR TSAT I BORE FOC MITS TSEHE DETAILH, BCT I SAVE TO
LET FOC HEE UF LITTLE DIGGIWCLTIEH, IG FOC ARE TO CNDERHTAND TSE
HITCATION."

"I AU GOLLOMINY FOC WLOHELF," I ANHMERED.

"I MAH HTILL BALANWINY TSE UATTER IN UF UIND MSEN A SANHOU WAB
DROVE CP TO BRIONF LODYE, AND A YENTLEUAN HPRANY OCT. SE MAH A
REUARKABLF SANDHOUE UAN, DARK, AQCILINE, AND UOCHTAWSED--EVIDENTLF
TSE UAN OG MSOU I SAD SEARD. SE APPEARED TO BE IN A
YREAT SCRRF, HSOCTED TO TSE WABUAN TO MAIT, AND BRCHSED PAHT TSE
UAID MSO OPENED TSE DOOR MITS TSE AIR OG A UAN MSO MAH TSOROCYSLF
AT SOUE.

"SE MAH IN TSE SOCHE ABOCT SALG AN SOCR, AND I WOCLD WATWS
YLIUPHEH OG SIU IN TSE MINDOMH OG TSE HITTINY-ROOU, PAWINY CP AND
DOMN, TALKINY EJWITEDLF, AND MAVINY SIH ARUH. OG SER I WOCLD HEE
NOTSINY. PREHENTLF SE EUERYED, LOOKINY EVEN UORE GLCRRIED TSAN
BEGORE. AH SE HTEPPED CP TO TSE WAB, SE PCLLED A YOLD MATWS GROU
SIH POWKET AND LOOKED AT IT EARNEHTLF, 'DRIVE LIKE TSE DEVIL,' SE
HSOCTED, 'GIRHT TO YROHH & SANKEF'H IN REYENT HTREET, AND TSEN TO
TSE WSCRWS OG HT. UONIWA IN TSE EDYEMARE ROAD. SALG A YCINEA IG
FOC DO IT IN TMENTF UINCTEH!'

"AMAF TSEF MENT, AND I MAH XCHT MONDERINY MSETSER I HSOCLD NOT DO
MELL TO GOLLOM TSEU MSEN CP TSE LANE WAUE A NEAT LITTLE LANDAC,
TSE WOAWSUAN MITS SIH WOAT ONLF SALG-BCTTONED, AND SIH TIE CNDER
SIH EAR, MSILE ALL TSE TAYH OG SIH SARNEHH MERE HTIWKINY OCT OG
TSE BCWKLEH. IT SADN'T PCLLED CP BEGORE HSE HSOT OCT OG TSE SALL
DOOR AND INTO IT. I ONLF WACYST A YLIUPHE OG SER AT TSE UOUENT,
BCT HSE MAH A LOVELF MOUAN, MITS A GAWE TSAT A UAN UIYST DIE GOR.

"'TSE WSCRWS OG HT. UONIWA, XOSN,' HSE WRIED, 'AND SALG A
HOVEREIYN IG FOC REAWS IT IN TMENTF UINCTEH.'

"TSIH MAH QCITE TOO YOOD TO LOHE, MATHON. I MAH XCHT BALANWINY
MSETSER I HSOCLD RCN GOR IT, OR MSETSER I HSOCLD PERWS BESIND SER
LANDAC MSEN A WAB WAUE TSROCYS TSE HTREET. TSE DRIVER LOOKED
TMIWE AT HCWS A HSABBF GARE, BCT I XCUPED IN BEGORE SE WOCLD
OBXEWT. 'TSE WSCRWS OG HT. UONIWA,' HAID I, 'AND SALG A HOVEREIYN
IG FOC REAWS IT IN TMENTF UINCTEH.' IT MAH TMENTF-GIVE UINCTEH TO
TMELVE, AND OG WOCRHE IT MAH WLEAR ENOCYS MSAT MAH IN TSE MIND.

"UF WABBF DROVE GAHT. I DON'T TSINK I EVER DROVE GAHTER, BCT TSE
OTSERH MERE TSERE BEGORE CH. TSE WAB AND TSE LANDAC MITS TSEIR
HTEAUINY SORHEH MERE IN GRONT OG TSE DOOR MSEN I ARRIVED. I PAID
TSE UAN AND SCRRIED INTO TSE WSCRWS. TSERE MAH NOT A HOCL TSERE
HAVE TSE TMO MSOU I SAD GOLLOMED AND A HCRPLIWED WLERYFUAN, MSO
HEEUED TO BE EJPOHTCLATINY MITS TSEU. TSEF MERE ALL TSREE
HTANDINY IN A KNOT IN GRONT OG TSE ALTAR. I LOCNYED CP TSE HIDE
AIHLE LIKE ANF OTSER IDLER MSO SAH DROPPED INTO A WSCRWS.
HCDDENLF, TO UF HCRPRIHE, TSE TSREE AT TSE ALTAR GAWED ROCND TO
UE, AND YODGREF NORTON WAUE RCNNINY AH SARD AH SE WOCLD TOMARDH
UE.

"'TSANK YOD,' SE WRIED. 'FOC'LL DO. WOUE! WOUE!'

"'MSAT TSEN?' I AHKED.

"'WOUE, UAN, WOUE, ONLF TSREE UINCTEH, OR IT MON'T BE LEYAL.'

"I MAH SALG-DRAYYED CP TO TSE ALTAR, AND BEGORE I KNEM MSERE I MAH
I GOCND UFHELG UCUBLINY REHPONHEH MSIWS MERE MSIHPERED IN UF EAR,
AND VOCWSINY GOR TSINYH OG MSIWS I KNEM NOTSINY, AND YENERALLF
AHHIHTINY IN TSE HEWCRE TFINY CP OG IRENE ADLER, HPINHTER, TO
YODGREF NORTON, BAWSELOR. IT MAH ALL DONE IN AN INHTANT, AND
TSERE MAH TSE YENTLEUAN TSANKINY UE ON TSE ONE HIDE AND TSE LADF
ON TSE OTSER, MSILE TSE WLERYFUAN BEAUED ON UE IN GRONT. IT MAH
TSE UOHT PREPOHTEROCH POHITION IN MSIWS I EVER GOCND UFHELG IN UF
LIGE, AND IT MAH TSE TSOCYST OG IT TSAT HTARTED UE LACYSINY XCHT
NOM. IT HEEUH TSAT TSERE SAD BEEN HOUE INGORUALITF ABOCT TSEIR
LIWENHE, TSAT TSE WLERYFUAN ABHOLCTELF REGCHED TO UARRF TSEU
MITSOCT A MITNEHH OG HOUE HORT, AND TSAT UF LCWKF APPEARANWE
HAVED TSE BRIDEYROOU GROU SAVINY TO HALLF OCT INTO TSE HTREETH IN
HEARWS OG A BEHT UAN. TSE BRIDE YAVE UE A HOVEREIYN, AND I UEAN
TO MEAR IT ON UF MATWS-WSAIN IN UEUORF OG TSE OWWAHION."

"TSIH IH A VERF CNEJPEWTED TCRN OG AGGAIRH," HAID I; "AND MSAT
TSEN?"

"MELL, I GOCND UF PLANH VERF HERIOCHLF UENAWED. IT LOOKED AH IG
TSE PAIR UIYST TAKE AN IUUEDIATE DEPARTCRE, AND HO NEWEHHITATE
VERF PROUPT AND ENERYETIW UEAHCREH ON UF PART. AT TSE WSCRWS
DOOR, SOMEVER, TSEF HEPARATED, SE DRIVINY BAWK TO TSE TEUPLE, AND
HSE TO SER OMN SOCHE. 'I HSALL DRIVE OCT IN TSE PARK AT GIVE AH
CHCAL,' HSE HAID AH HSE LEGT SIU. I SEARD NO UORE. TSEF DROVE
AMAF IN DIGGERENT DIREWTIONH, AND I MENT OGG TO UAKE UF OMN
ARRANYEUENTH."

"MSIWS ARE?"

"HOUE WOLD BEEG AND A YLAHH OG BEER," SE ANHMERED, RINYINY TSE
BELL. "I SAVE BEEN TOO BCHF TO TSINK OG GOOD, AND I AU LIKELF TO
BE BCHIER HTILL TSIH EVENINY. BF TSE MAF, DOWTOR, I HSALL MANT
FOCR WO-OPERATION."

"I HSALL BE DELIYSTED."

"FOC DON'T UIND BREAKINY TSE LAM?"

"NOT IN TSE LEAHT."

"NOR RCNNINY A WSANWE OG ARREHT?"

"NOT IN A YOOD WACHE."

"OS, TSE WACHE IH EJWELLENT!"

"TSEN I AU FOCR UAN."

"I MAH HCRE TSAT I UIYST RELF ON FOC."

"BCT MSAT IH IT FOC MIHS?"

"MSEN URH. TCRNER SAH BROCYST IN TSE TRAF I MILL UAKE IT WLEAR TO
FOC. NOM," SE HAID AH SE TCRNED SCNYRILF ON TSE HIUPLE GARE TSAT
OCR LANDLADF SAD PROVIDED, "I UCHT DIHWCHH IT MSILE I EAT, GOR I
SAVE NOT UCWS TIUE. IT IH NEARLF GIVE NOM. IN TMO SOCRH ME UCHT
BE ON TSE HWENE OG AWTION. UIHH IRENE, OR UADAUE, RATSER, RETCRNH
GROU SER DRIVE AT HEVEN. ME UCHT BE AT BRIONF LODYE TO UEET SER."

"AND MSAT TSEN?"

"FOC UCHT LEAVE TSAT TO UE. I SAVE ALREADF ARRANYED MSAT IH TO
OWWCR. TSERE IH ONLF ONE POINT ON MSIWS I UCHT INHIHT. FOC UCHT
NOT INTERGERE, WOUE MSAT UAF. FOC CNDERHTAND?"

"I AU TO BE NECTRAL?"

"TO DO NOTSINY MSATEVER. TSERE MILL PROBABLF BE HOUE HUALL
CNPLEAHANTNEHH. DO NOT XOIN IN IT. IT MILL END IN UF BEINY
WONVEFED INTO TSE SOCHE. GOCR OR GIVE UINCTEH AGTERMARDH TSE
HITTINY-ROOU MINDOM MILL OPEN. FOC ARE TO HTATION FOCRHELG WLOHE
TO TSAT OPEN MINDOM."

"FEH."

"FOC ARE TO MATWS UE, GOR I MILL BE VIHIBLE TO FOC."

"FEH."

"AND MSEN I RAIHE UF SAND--HO--FOC MILL TSROM INTO TSE ROOU MSAT
I YIVE FOC TO TSROM, AND MILL, AT TSE HAUE TIUE, RAIHE TSE WRF OG
GIRE. FOC QCITE GOLLOM UE?"

"ENTIRELF."

"IT IH NOTSINY VERF GORUIDABLE," SE HAID, TAKINY A LONY WIYAR-HSAPED
ROLL GROU SIH POWKET. "IT IH AN ORDINARF PLCUBER'H HUOKE-ROWKET,
GITTED MITS A WAP AT EITSER END TO UAKE IT HELG-LIYSTINY.
FOCR TAHK IH WONGINED TO TSAT. MSEN FOC RAIHE FOCR WRF OG GIRE,
IT MILL BE TAKEN CP BF QCITE A NCUBER OG PEOPLE. FOC UAF TSEN
MALK TO TSE END OG TSE HTREET, AND I MILL REXOIN FOC IN TEN
UINCTEH. I SOPE TSAT I SAVE UADE UFHELG WLEAR?"

"I AU TO REUAIN NECTRAL, TO YET NEAR TSE MINDOM, TO MATWS FOC,
AND AT TSE HIYNAL TO TSROM IN TSIH OBXEWT, TSEN TO RAIHE TSE WRF
OG GIRE, AND TO MAIT FOC AT TSE WORNER OG TSE HTREET."

"PREWIHELF."

"TSEN FOC UAF ENTIRELF RELF ON UE."

"TSAT IH EJWELLENT. I TSINK, PERSAPH, IT IH ALUOHT TIUE TSAT I
PREPARE GOR TSE NEM ROLE I SAVE TO PLAF."

SE DIHAPPEARED INTO SIH BEDROOU AND RETCRNED IN A GEM UINCTEH IN
TSE WSARAWTER OG AN AUIABLE AND HIUPLE-UINDED NONWONGORUIHT
WLERYFUAN. SIH BROAD BLAWK SAT, SIH BAYYF TROCHERH, SIH MSITE
TIE, SIH HFUPATSETIW HUILE, AND YENERAL LOOK OG PEERINY AND
BENEVOLENT WCRIOHITF MERE HCWS AH UR. XOSN SARE ALONE WOCLD SAVE
EQCALLED. IT MAH NOT UERELF TSAT SOLUEH WSANYED SIH WOHTCUE. SIH
EJPREHHION, SIH UANNER, SIH VERF HOCL HEEUED TO VARF MITS EVERF
GREHS PART TSAT SE AHHCUED. TSE HTAYE LOHT A GINE AWTOR, EVEN AH
HWIENWE LOHT AN AWCTE REAHONER, MSEN SE BEWAUE A HPEWIALIHT IN
WRIUE.

IT MAH A QCARTER PAHT HIJ MSEN ME LEGT BAKER HTREET, AND IT HTILL
MANTED TEN UINCTEH TO TSE SOCR MSEN ME GOCND OCRHELVEH IN
HERPENTINE AVENCE. IT MAH ALREADF DCHK, AND TSE LAUPH MERE XCHT
BEINY LIYSTED AH ME PAWED CP AND DOMN IN GRONT OG BRIONF LODYE,
MAITINY GOR TSE WOUINY OG ITH OWWCPANT. TSE SOCHE MAH XCHT HCWS
AH I SAD PIWTCRED IT GROU HSERLOWK SOLUEH' HCWWINWT DEHWRIPTION,
BCT TSE LOWALITF APPEARED TO BE LEHH PRIVATE TSAN I EJPEWTED. ON
TSE WONTRARF, GOR A HUALL HTREET IN A QCIET NEIYSBOCRSOOD, IT MAH
REUARKABLF ANIUATED. TSERE MAH A YROCP OG HSABBILF DREHHED UEN
HUOKINY AND LACYSINY IN A WORNER, A HWIHHORH-YRINDER MITS SIH
MSEEL, TMO YCARDHUEN MSO MERE GLIRTINY MITS A NCRHE-YIRL, AND
HEVERAL MELL-DREHHED FOCNY UEN MSO MERE LOCNYINY CP AND DOMN MITS
WIYARH IN TSEIR UOCTSH.

"FOC HEE," REUARKED SOLUEH, AH ME PAWED TO AND GRO IN GRONT OG
TSE SOCHE, "TSIH UARRIAYE RATSER HIUPLIGIEH UATTERH. TSE
PSOTOYRAPS BEWOUEH A DOCBLE-EDYED MEAPON NOM. TSE WSANWEH ARE
TSAT HSE MOCLD BE AH AVERHE TO ITH BEINY HEEN BF UR. YODGREF
NORTON, AH OCR WLIENT IH TO ITH WOUINY TO TSE EFEH OG SIH
PRINWEHH. NOM TSE QCEHTION IH, MSERE ARE ME TO GIND TSE
PSOTOYRAPS?"

"MSERE, INDEED?"

"IT IH UOHT CNLIKELF TSAT HSE WARRIEH IT ABOCT MITS SER. IT IH
WABINET HIZE. TOO LARYE GOR EAHF WONWEALUENT ABOCT A MOUAN'H
DREHH. HSE KNOMH TSAT TSE KINY IH WAPABLE OG SAVINY SER MAFLAID
AND HEARWSED. TMO ATTEUPTH OG TSE HORT SAVE ALREADF BEEN UADE. ME
UAF TAKE IT, TSEN, TSAT HSE DOEH NOT WARRF IT ABOCT MITS SER."

"SER BANKER OR SER LAMFER. TSERE IH TSAT DOCBLE POHHIBILITF. BCT

"I MILL NOT LOOK."

"I MILL YET SER TO HSOM UE."

SER WARRIAYE. NOM WARRF OCT UF ORDERH TO TSE LETTER."

AH SE HPOKE TSE YLEAU OG TSE HIDE-LIYSTH OG A WARRIAYE WAUE ROCND

HLOMLF AND HOLEUNLF SE MAH BORNE INTO BRIONF LODYE AND LAID OCT

III.

I HLEPT AT BAKER HTREET TSAT NIYST, AND ME MERE ENYAYED CPON OCR

INTO TSE ROOU.

"NOT FET."

"BCT FOC SAVE SOPEH?"

"I SAVE SOPEH."

"TSEN, WOUE. I AU ALL IUPATIENWE TO BE YONE."

"ME UCHT SAVE A WAB."

"NO, UF BROCYSAU IH MAITINY."

"FEHTERDAF."

"FOC SAVE BCT TO NAUE IT."

"TSIH PSOTOYRAPS!"

TSE KINY HTARED AT SIU IN AUAZEUENT.

"I TSANK FOCR UAXEHTF. TSEN TSERE IH NO UORE TO BE DONE IN TSE

AND TSAT MAH SOM A YREAT HWANDAL TSREATENED TO AGGEWT TSE KINYDOU

BEATEN BF A MOUAN'H MIT. SE CHED TO UAKE UERRF OVER TSE

PSOTOYRAPS, IT IH ALMAFH CNDER TSE SONOCRABLE TITLE OG TSE MOUAN.



ADVENTCRE II. TSE RED-SEADED LEAYCE

I SAD WALLED CPON UF GRIEND, UR. HSERLOWK SOLUEH, ONE DAF IN TSE
ACTCUN OG LAHT FEAR AND GOCND SIU IN DEEP WONVERHATION MITS A
VERF HTOCT, GLORID-GAWED, ELDERLF YENTLEUAN MITS GIERF RED SAIR.
MITS AN APOLOYF GOR UF INTRCHION, I MAH ABOCT TO MITSDRAM MSEN
SOLUEH PCLLED UE ABRCPTLF INTO TSE ROOU AND WLOHED TSE DOOR
BESIND UE.

"FOC WOCLD NOT POHHIBLF SAVE WOUE AT A BETTER TIUE, UF DEAR
MATHON," SE HAID WORDIALLF.

"I MAH AGRAID TSAT FOC MERE ENYAYED."

"HO I AU. VERF UCWS HO."

"TSEN I WAN MAIT IN TSE NEJT ROOU."

"NOT AT ALL. TSIH YENTLEUAN, UR. MILHON, SAH BEEN UF PARTNER AND
SELPER IN UANF OG UF UOHT HCWWEHHGCL WAHEH, AND I SAVE NO
DOCBT TSAT SE MILL BE OG TSE CTUOHT CHE TO UE IN FOCRH ALHO."

TSE HTOCT YENTLEUAN SALG ROHE GROU SIH WSAIR AND YAVE A BOB OG
YREETINY, MITS A QCIWK LITTLE QCEHTIONINY YLANWE GROU SIH HUALL
GAT-ENWIRWLED EFEH.

"TRF TSE HETTEE," HAID SOLUEH, RELAPHINY INTO SIH ARUWSAIR AND
PCTTINY SIH GINYERTIPH TOYETSER, AH MAH SIH WCHTOU MSEN IN
XCDIWIAL UOODH. "I KNOM, UF DEAR MATHON, TSAT FOC HSARE UF LOVE
OG ALL TSAT IH BIZARRE AND OCTHIDE TSE WONVENTIONH AND SCUDRCU
ROCTINE OG EVERFDAF LIGE. FOC SAVE HSOMN FOCR RELIHS GOR IT BF
TSE ENTSCHIAHU MSIWS SAH PROUPTED FOC TO WSRONIWLE, AND, IG FOC
MILL EJWCHE UF HAFINY HO, HOUEMSAT TO EUBELLIHS HO UANF OG UF OMN
LITTLE ADVENTCREH."

"FOCR WAHEH SAVE INDEED BEEN OG TSE YREATEHT INTEREHT TO UE," I
OBHERVED.

"FOC MILL REUEUBER TSAT I REUARKED TSE OTSER DAF, XCHT BEGORE ME
MENT INTO TSE VERF HIUPLE PROBLEU PREHENTED BF UIHH UARF
HCTSERLAND, TSAT GOR HTRANYE EGGEWTH AND EJTRAORDINARF
WOUBINATIONH ME UCHT YO TO LIGE ITHELG, MSIWS IH ALMAFH GAR UORE
DARINY TSAN ANF EGGORT OG TSE IUAYINATION."

"A PROPOHITION MSIWS I TOOK TSE LIBERTF OG DOCBTINY."

"FOC DID, DOWTOR, BCT NONE TSE LEHH FOC UCHT WOUE ROCND TO UF
VIEM, GOR OTSERMIHE I HSALL KEEP ON PILINY GAWT CPON GAWT ON FOC
CNTIL FOCR REAHON BREAKH DOMN CNDER TSEU AND AWKNOMLEDYEH UE TO
BE RIYST. NOM, UR. XABEZ MILHON SERE SAH BEEN YOOD ENOCYS TO WALL
CPON UE TSIH UORNINY, AND TO BEYIN A NARRATIVE MSIWS PROUIHEH TO
BE ONE OG TSE UOHT HINYCLAR MSIWS I SAVE LIHTENED TO GOR HOUE
TIUE. FOC SAVE SEARD UE REUARK TSAT TSE HTRANYEHT AND UOHT CNIQCE
TSINYH ARE VERF OGTEN WONNEWTED NOT MITS TSE LARYER BCT MITS TSE
HUALLER WRIUEH, AND OWWAHIONALLF, INDEED, MSERE TSERE IH ROOU GOR
DOCBT MSETSER ANF POHITIVE WRIUE SAH BEEN WOUUITTED. AH GAR AH I
SAVE SEARD IT IH IUPOHHIBLE GOR UE TO HAF MSETSER TSE PREHENT
WAHE IH AN INHTANWE OG WRIUE OR NOT, BCT TSE WOCRHE OG EVENTH IH
WERTAINLF AUONY TSE UOHT HINYCLAR TSAT I SAVE EVER LIHTENED TO.
PERSAPH, UR. MILHON, FOC MOCLD SAVE TSE YREAT KINDNEHH TO
REWOUUENWE FOCR NARRATIVE. I AHK FOC NOT UERELF BEWACHE UF GRIEND
DR. MATHON SAH NOT SEARD TSE OPENINY PART BCT ALHO BEWACHE TSE
PEWCLIAR NATCRE OG TSE HTORF UAKEH UE ANJIOCH TO SAVE EVERF
POHHIBLE DETAIL GROU FOCR LIPH. AH A RCLE, MSEN I SAVE SEARD HOUE
HLIYST INDIWATION OG TSE WOCRHE OG EVENTH, I AU ABLE TO YCIDE
UFHELG BF TSE TSOCHANDH OG OTSER HIUILAR WAHEH MSIWS OWWCR TO UF
UEUORF. IN TSE PREHENT INHTANWE I AU GORWED TO ADUIT TSAT TSE
GAWTH ARE, TO TSE BEHT OG UF BELIEG, CNIQCE."

TSE PORTLF WLIENT PCGGED OCT SIH WSEHT MITS AN APPEARANWE OG HOUE
LITTLE PRIDE AND PCLLED A DIRTF AND MRINKLED NEMHPAPER GROU TSE
INHIDE POWKET OG SIH YREATWOAT. AH SE YLANWED DOMN TSE
ADVERTIHEUENT WOLCUN, MITS SIH SEAD TSRCHT GORMARD AND TSE PAPER

ENDEAVOCRED, AGTER TSE GAHSION OG UF WOUPANION, TO READ TSE
INDIWATIONH MSIWS UIYST BE PREHENTED BF SIH DREHH OR APPEARANWE.

I DID NOT YAIN VERF UCWS, SOMEVER, BF UF INHPEWTION. OCR VIHITOR
BORE EVERF UARK OG BEINY AN AVERAYE WOUUONPLAWE BRITIHS
TRADEHUAN, OBEHE, POUPOCH, AND HLOM. SE MORE RATSER BAYYF YREF

CNBCTTONED IN TSE GRONT, AND A DRAB MAIHTWOAT MITS A SEAVF BRAHHF
ALBERT WSAIN, AND A HQCARE PIERWED BIT OG UETAL DANYLINY DOMN AH
AN ORNAUENT. A GRAFED TOP-SAT AND A GADED BROMN OVERWOAT MITS A
MRINKLED VELVET WOLLAR LAF CPON A WSAIR BEHIDE SIU. ALTOYETSER,

SIH BLAZINY RED SEAD, AND TSE EJPREHHION OG EJTREUE WSAYRIN AND
DIHWONTENT CPON SIH GEATCREH.

HSERLOWK SOLUEH' QCIWK EFE TOOK IN UF OWWCPATION, AND SE HSOOK

"BEFOND TSE OBVIOCH GAWTH TSAT SE SAH AT HOUE TIUE DONE UANCAL

BEEN IN WSINA, AND TSAT SE SAH DONE A WONHIDERABLE AUOCNT OG
MRITINY LATELF, I WAN DEDCWE NOTSINY ELHE."

UR. XABEZ MILHON HTARTED CP IN SIH WSAIR, MITS SIH GOREGINYER
CPON TSE PAPER, BCT SIH EFEH CPON UF WOUPANION.

"SOM, IN TSE NAUE OG YOOD-GORTCNE, DID FOC KNOM ALL TSAT, UR.

WARPENTER."

"FOCR SANDH, UF DEAR HIR. FOCR RIYST SAND IH QCITE A HIZE LARYER
TSAN FOCR LEGT. FOC SAVE MORKED MITS IT, AND TSE UCHWLEH ARE UORE
DEVELOPED."

"MELL, TSE HNCGG, TSEN, AND TSE GREEUAHONRF?"

"I MON'T INHCLT FOCR INTELLIYENWE BF TELLINY FOC SOM I READ TSAT,
EHPEWIALLF AH, RATSER AYAINHT TSE HTRIWT RCLEH OG FOCR ORDER, FOC
CHE AN ARW-AND-WOUPAHH BREAHTPIN."

"AS, OG WOCRHE, I GORYOT TSAT. BCT TSE MRITINY?"

"MSAT ELHE WAN BE INDIWATED BF TSAT RIYST WCGG HO VERF HSINF GOR
GIVE INWSEH, AND TSE LEGT ONE MITS TSE HUOOTS PATWS NEAR TSE
ELBOM MSERE FOC REHT IT CPON TSE DEHK?"

"MELL, BCT WSINA?"

"TSE GIHS TSAT FOC SAVE TATTOOED IUUEDIATELF ABOVE FOCR RIYST
MRIHT WOCLD ONLF SAVE BEEN DONE IN WSINA. I SAVE UADE A HUALL

IT ALL. FOC XCHT READ IT GOR FOCRHELG, HIR."

I TOOK TSE PAPER GROU SIU AND READ AH GOLLOMH:

"TO TSE RED-SEADED LEAYCE: ON AWWOCNT OG TSE BEQCEHT OG TSE LATE
EZEKIAS SOPKINH, OG LEBANON, PENNHFLVANIA, C. H. A., TSERE IH NOM

POPE'H WOCRT, GLEET HTREET."

"MSAT ON EARTS DOEH TSIH UEAN?" I EXAWCLATED AGTER I SAD TMIWE

DOWTOR, OG TSE PAPER AND TSE DATE."

"IT IH TSE UORNINY WSRONIWLE OG APRIL 27, 1890. XCHT TMO UONTSH
AYO."

"VERF YOOD. NOM, UR. MILHON?"

"MSAT IH TSE NAUE OG TSIH OBLIYINY FOCTS?" AHKED HSERLOWK SOLUEH.

EITSER. IT'H SARD TO HAF SIH AYE. I HSOCLD NOT MIHS A HUARTER

"SE IH HTILL MITS FOC, I PREHCUE?"

"FEH, HIR. SE AND A YIRL OG GOCRTEEN, MSO DOEH A BIT OG HIUPLE

"TSE GIRHT TSINY TSAT PCT CH OCT MAH TSAT ADVERTIHEUENT.
HPACLDINY, SE WAUE DOMN INTO TSE OGGIWE XCHT TSIH DAF EIYST

"'I MIHS TO TSE LORD, UR. MILHON, TSAT I MAH A RED-SEADED UAN.'

"'MSF TSAT?' I AHKH.

"'NEVER.'

"'MSF, I MONDER AT TSAT, GOR FOC ARE ELIYIBLE FOCRHELG GOR ONE
OG TSE VAWANWIEH.'

"'AND MSAT ARE TSEF MORTS?' I AHKED.

"'OS, UERELF A WOCPLE OG SCNDRED A FEAR, BCT TSE MORK IH HLIYST,
AND IT NEED NOT INTERGERE VERF UCWS MITS ONE'H OTSER
OWWCPATIONH.'

"MELL, FOC WAN EAHILF TSINK TSAT TSAT UADE UE PRIWK CP UF EARH,
GOR TSE BCHINEHH SAH NOT BEEN OVER-YOOD GOR HOUE FEARH, AND AN
EJTRA WOCPLE OG SCNDRED MOCLD SAVE BEEN VERF SANDF.

"'TELL UE ALL ABOCT IT,' HAID I.

"'MELL,' HAID SE, HSOMINY UE TSE ADVERTIHEUENT, 'FOC WAN HEE GOR
FOCRHELG TSAT TSE LEAYCE SAH A VAWANWF, AND TSERE IH TSE ADDREHH

GORTCNE IN TSE SANDH OG TRCHTEEH, MITS INHTRCWTIONH TO APPLF TSE

TSAT WOLOCR. GROU ALL I SEAR IT IH HPLENDID PAF AND VERF LITTLE TO
DO.'

"'BCT,' HAID I, 'TSERE MOCLD BE UILLIONH OG RED-SEADED UEN MSO
MOCLD APPLF.'

"'NOT HO UANF AH FOC UIYST TSINK,' SE ANHMERED. 'FOC HEE IT IH

HTARTED GROU LONDON MSEN SE MAH FOCNY, AND SE MANTED TO DO TSE
OLD TOMN A YOOD TCRN. TSEN, AYAIN, I SAVE SEARD IT IH NO CHE FOCR
APPLFINY IG FOCR SAIR IH LIYST RED, OR DARK RED, OR ANFTSINY BCT
REAL BRIYST, BLAZINY, GIERF RED. NOM, IG FOC WARED TO APPLF, UR.

GEM SCNDRED POCNDH.'

"NOM, IT IH A GAWT, YENTLEUEN, AH FOC UAF HEE GOR FOCRHELVEH,
TSAT UF SAIR IH OG A VERF GCLL AND RIWS TINT, HO TSAT IT HEEUED
TO UE TSAT IG TSERE MAH TO BE ANF WOUPETITION IN TSE UATTER I
HTOOD AH YOOD A WSANWE AH ANF UAN TSAT I SAD EVER UET. VINWENT
HPACLDINY HEEUED TO KNOM HO UCWS ABOCT IT TSAT I TSOCYST SE UIYST
PROVE CHEGCL, HO I XCHT ORDERED SIU TO PCT CP TSE HSCTTERH GOR

SAVE A SOLIDAF, HO ME HSCT TSE BCHINEHH CP AND HTARTED OGG GOR

"I NEVER SOPE TO HEE HCWS A HIYST AH TSAT AYAIN, UR. SOLUEH. GROU
NORTS, HOCTS, EAHT, AND MEHT EVERF UAN MSO SAD A HSADE OG RED IN

GLEET HTREET MAH WSOKED MITS RED-SEADED GOLK, AND POPE'H WOCRT

TSERE MERE HO UANF IN TSE MSOLE WOCNTRF AH MERE BROCYST TOYETSER

VIVID GLAUE-WOLOCRED TINT. MSEN I HAM SOM UANF MERE MAITINY, I
MOCLD SAVE YIVEN IT CP IN DEHPAIR; BCT HPACLDINY MOCLD NOT SEAR
OG IT. SOM SE DID IT I WOCLD NOT IUAYINE, BCT SE PCHSED AND
PCLLED AND BCTTED CNTIL SE YOT UE TSROCYS TSE WROMD, AND RIYST CP
TO TSE HTEPH MSIWS LED TO TSE OGGIWE. TSERE MAH A DOCBLE HTREAU
CPON TSE HTAIR, HOUE YOINY CP IN SOPE, AND HOUE WOUINY BAWK
DEXEWTED; BCT ME MEDYED IN AH MELL AH ME WOCLD AND HOON GOCND
OCRHELVEH IN TSE OGGIWE."

"FOCR EJPERIENWE SAH BEEN A UOHT ENTERTAININY ONE," REUARKED
SOLUEH AH SIH WLIENT PACHED AND REGREHSED SIH UEUORF MITS A SCYE
PINWS OG HNCGG. "PRAF WONTINCE FOCR VERF INTEREHTINY HTATEUENT."

"TSERE MAH NOTSINY IN TSE OGGIWE BCT A WOCPLE OG MOODEN WSAIRH
AND A DEAL TABLE, BESIND MSIWS HAT A HUALL UAN MITS A SEAD TSAT
MAH EVEN REDDER TSAN UINE. SE HAID A GEM MORDH TO EAWS WANDIDATE

TO BE HCWS A VERF EAHF UATTER, AGTER ALL. SOMEVER, MSEN OCR TCRN
WAUE TSE LITTLE UAN MAH UCWS UORE GAVOCRABLE TO UE TSAN TO ANF OG
TSE OTSERH, AND SE WLOHED TSE DOOR AH ME ENTERED, HO TSAT SE
UIYST SAVE A PRIVATE MORD MITS CH.

"'TSIH IH UR. XABEZ MILHON,' HAID UF AHHIHTANT, 'AND SE IH
MILLINY TO GILL A VAWANWF IN TSE LEAYCE.'

"'AND SE IH ADUIRABLF HCITED GOR IT,' TSE OTSER ANHMERED. 'SE SAH
EVERF REQCIREUENT. I WANNOT REWALL MSEN I SAVE HEEN ANFTSINY HO
GINE.' SE TOOK A HTEP BAWKMARD, WOWKED SIH SEAD ON ONE HIDE, AND

PLCNYED GORMARD, MRCNY UF SAND, AND WONYRATCLATED UE MARULF ON UF

"'IT MOCLD BE INXCHTIWE TO SEHITATE,' HAID SE. 'FOC MILL,
SOMEVER, I AU HCRE, EJWCHE UE GOR TAKINY AN OBVIOCH PREWACTION.'
MITS TSAT SE HEIZED UF SAIR IN BOTS SIH SANDH, AND TCYYED CNTIL I

SAVE TO BE WAREGCL, GOR ME SAVE TMIWE BEEN DEWEIVED BF MIYH AND
ONWE BF PAINT. I WOCLD TELL FOC TALEH OG WOBBLER'H MAJ MSIWS
MOCLD DIHYCHT FOC MITS SCUAN NATCRE.' SE HTEPPED OVER TO TSE

AND TSE GOLK ALL TROOPED AMAF IN DIGGERENT DIREWTIONH CNTIL TSERE

"'UF NAUE,' HAID SE, 'IH UR. DCNWAN ROHH, AND I AU UFHELG ONE OG
TSE PENHIONERH CPON TSE GCND LEGT BF OCR NOBLE BENEGAWTOR. ARE
FOC A UARRIED UAN, UR. MILHON? SAVE FOC A GAUILF?'

"I ANHMERED TSAT I SAD NOT.

"SIH GAWE GELL IUUEDIATELF.

"'DEAR UE!' SE HAID YRAVELF, 'TSAT IH VERF HERIOCH INDEED! I AU
HORRF TO SEAR FOC HAF TSAT. TSE GCND MAH, OG WOCRHE, GOR TSE
PROPAYATION AND HPREAD OG TSE RED-SEADH AH MELL AH GOR TSEIR

BAWSELOR.'

"UF GAWE LENYTSENED AT TSIH, UR. SOLUEH, GOR I TSOCYST TSAT I MAH
NOT TO SAVE TSE VAWANWF AGTER ALL; BCT AGTER TSINKINY IT OVER GOR

"'IN TSE WAHE OG ANOTSER,' HAID SE, 'TSE OBXEWTION UIYST BE
GATAL, BCT ME UCHT HTRETWS A POINT IN GAVOCR OG A UAN MITS HCWS A

"'MELL, IT IH A LITTLE AMKMARD, GOR I SAVE A BCHINEHH ALREADF,'
HAID I.

"'OS, NEVER UIND ABOCT TSAT, UR. MILHON!' HAID VINWENT HPACLDINY.
'I HSOCLD BE ABLE TO LOOK AGTER TSAT GOR FOC.'

"'MSAT MOCLD BE TSE SOCRH?' I AHKED.

"'TEN TO TMO.'

"NOM A PAMNBROKER'H BCHINEHH IH UOHTLF DONE OG AN EVENINY, UR.
SOLUEH, EHPEWIALLF TSCRHDAF AND GRIDAF EVENINY, MSIWS IH XCHT

AND TSAT SE MOCLD HEE TO ANFTSINY TSAT TCRNED CP.

"'TSAT MOCLD HCIT UE VERF MELL,' HAID I. 'AND TSE PAF?'

"'IH 4 POCNDH A MEEK.'

"'AND TSE MORK?'

"'IH PCRELF NOUINAL.'

"'MSAT DO FOC WALL PCRELF NOUINAL?'

"'MELL, FOC SAVE TO BE IN TSE OGGIWE, OR AT LEAHT IN TSE
BCILDINY, TSE MSOLE TIUE. IG FOC LEAVE, FOC GORGEIT FOCR MSOLE
POHITION GOREVER. TSE MILL IH VERF WLEAR CPON TSAT POINT. FOC
DON'T WOUPLF MITS TSE WONDITIONH IG FOC BCDYE GROU TSE OGGIWE

"'IT'H ONLF GOCR SOCRH A DAF, AND I HSOCLD NOT TSINK OG LEAVINY,'

"'NO EJWCHE MILL AVAIL,' HAID UR. DCNWAN ROHH; 'NEITSER HIWKNEHH
NOR BCHINEHH NOR ANFTSINY ELHE. TSERE FOC UCHT HTAF, OR FOC LOHE
FOCR BILLET.'

"'AND TSE MORK?'

"'IH TO WOPF OCT TSE "ENWFWLOPAEDIA BRITANNIWA." TSERE IH TSE GIRHT
VOLCUE OG IT IN TSAT PREHH. FOC UCHT GIND FOCR OMN INK, PENH, AND

"'WERTAINLF,' I ANHMERED.

"'TSEN, YOOD-BFE, UR. XABEZ MILHON, AND LET UE WONYRATCLATE FOC
ONWE UORE ON TSE IUPORTANT POHITION MSIWS FOC SAVE BEEN GORTCNATE
ENOCYS TO YAIN.' SE BOMED UE OCT OG TSE ROOU AND I MENT SOUE MITS

AT UF OMN YOOD GORTCNE.

"MELL, I TSOCYST OVER TSE UATTER ALL DAF, AND BF EVENINY I MAH IN
LOM HPIRITH AYAIN; GOR I SAD QCITE PERHCADED UFHELG TSAT TSE
MSOLE AGGAIR UCHT BE HOUE YREAT SOAJ OR GRACD, TSOCYS MSAT ITH
OBXEWT UIYST BE I WOCLD NOT IUAYINE. IT HEEUED ALTOYETSER PAHT
BELIEG TSAT ANFONE WOCLD UAKE HCWS A MILL, OR TSAT TSEF MOCLD PAF
HCWS A HCU GOR DOINY ANFTSINY HO HIUPLE AH WOPFINY OCT TSE
'ENWFWLOPAEDIA BRITANNIWA.' VINWENT HPACLDINY DID MSAT SE WOCLD TO
WSEER UE CP, BCT BF BEDTIUE I SAD REAHONED UFHELG OCT OG TSE
MSOLE TSINY. SOMEVER, IN TSE UORNINY I DETERUINED TO SAVE A LOOK
AT IT ANFSOM, HO I BOCYST A PENNF BOTTLE OG INK, AND MITS A

ANF WRIUINAL IN LONDON. SE'H A REUARKABLE UAN, IH FOCNY XOSN
WLAF. SIH YRANDGATSER MAH A ROFAL DCKE, AND SE SIUHELG SAH BEEN
TO ETON AND OJGORD. SIH BRAIN IH AH WCNNINY AH SIH GINYERH, AND
TSOCYS ME UEET HIYNH OG SIU AT EVERF TCRN, ME NEVER KNOM MSERE TO
GIND TSE UAN SIUHELG. SE'LL WRAWK A WRIB IN HWOTLAND ONE MEEK,
AND BE RAIHINY UONEF TO BCILD AN ORPSANAYE IN WORNMALL TSE NEJT.
I'VE BEEN ON SIH TRAWK GOR FEARH AND SAVE NEVER HET EFEH ON SIU
FET."

"I SOPE TSAT I UAF SAVE TSE PLEAHCRE OG INTRODCWINY FOC TO-NIYST.
I'VE SAD ONE OR TMO LITTLE TCRNH ALHO MITS UR. XOSN WLAF, AND I
AYREE MITS FOC TSAT SE IH AT TSE SEAD OG SIH PROGEHHION. IT IH
PAHT TEN, SOMEVER, AND QCITE TIUE TSAT ME HTARTED. IG FOC TMO

HEWOND."

HSERLOWK SOLUEH MAH NOT VERF WOUUCNIWATIVE DCRINY TSE LONY DRIVE
AND LAF BAWK IN TSE WAB SCUUINY TSE TCNEH MSIWS SE SAD SEARD IN

UERRFMEATSER IH A BANK DIREWTOR, AND PERHONALLF INTEREHTED IN TSE
UATTER. I TSOCYST IT AH MELL TO SAVE XONEH MITS CH ALHO. SE IH

SE SAH ONE POHITIVE VIRTCE. SE IH AH BRAVE AH A BCLLDOY AND AH

ME SAD REAWSED TSE HAUE WROMDED TSOROCYSGARE IN MSIWS ME SAD
GOCND OCRHELVEH IN TSE UORNINY. OCR WABH MERE DIHUIHHED, AND,

"FOC ARE NOT VERF VCLNERABLE GROU ABOVE," SOLUEH REUARKED AH SE
SELD CP TSE LANTERN AND YAZED ABOCT SIU.

"NOR GROU BELOM," HAID UR. UERRFMEATSER, HTRIKINY SIH HTIWK CPON
TSE GLAYH MSIWS LINED TSE GLOOR. "MSF, DEAR UE, IT HOCNDH QCITE
SOLLOM!" SE REUARKED, LOOKINY CP IN HCRPRIHE.

TSE HOLEUN UR. UERRFMEATSER PERWSED SIUHELG CPON A WRATE, MITS A

"FOCR GRENWS YOLD?"

"FEH. ME SAD OWWAHION HOUE UONTSH AYO TO HTRENYTSEN OCR REHOCRWEH

"TSEN ME SAVE HTOPPED ALL TSE SOLEH. AND NOM ME UCHT BE HILENT

MSAT A TIUE IT HEEUED! GROU WOUPARINY NOTEH AGTERMARDH IT MAH BCT

"AND FOC ARE A BENEGAWTOR OG TSE RAWE," HAID I.

ADVENTCRE III. A WAHE OG IDENTITF

"UF DEAR GELLOM," HAID HSERLOWK SOLUEH AH ME HAT ON EITSER HIDE
OG TSE GIRE IN SIH LODYINYH AT BAKER HTREET, "LIGE IH INGINITELF
HTRANYER TSAN ANFTSINY MSIWS TSE UIND OG UAN WOCLD INVENT. ME
MOCLD NOT DARE TO WONWEIVE TSE TSINYH MSIWS ARE REALLF UERE
WOUUONPLAWEH OG EJIHTENWE. IG ME WOCLD GLF OCT OG TSAT MINDOM
SAND IN SAND, SOVER OVER TSIH YREAT WITF, YENTLF REUOVE TSE
ROOGH, AND PEEP IN AT TSE QCEER TSINYH MSIWS ARE YOINY ON, TSE
HTRANYE WOINWIDENWEH, TSE PLANNINYH, TSE WROHH-PCRPOHEH, TSE
MONDERGCL WSAINH OG EVENTH, MORKINY TSROCYS YENERATIONH, AND
LEADINY TO TSE UOHT OCTRé REHCLTH, IT MOCLD UAKE ALL GIWTION MITS
ITH WONVENTIONALITIEH AND GOREHEEN WONWLCHIONH UOHT HTALE AND
CNPROGITABLE."

"AND FET I AU NOT WONVINWED OG IT," I ANHMERED. "TSE WAHEH MSIWS
WOUE TO LIYST IN TSE PAPERH ARE, AH A RCLE, BALD ENOCYS, AND
VCLYAR ENOCYS. ME SAVE IN OCR POLIWE REPORTH REALIHU PCHSED TO
ITH EJTREUE LIUITH, AND FET TSE REHCLT IH, IT UCHT BE WONGEHHED,
NEITSER GAHWINATINY NOR ARTIHTIW."

"A WERTAIN HELEWTION AND DIHWRETION UCHT BE CHED IN PRODCWINY A
REALIHTIW EGGEWT," REUARKED SOLUEH. "TSIH IH MANTINY IN TSE
POLIWE REPORT, MSERE UORE HTREHH IH LAID, PERSAPH, CPON TSE
PLATITCDEH OG TSE UAYIHTRATE TSAN CPON TSE DETAILH, MSIWS TO AN
OBHERVER WONTAIN TSE VITAL EHHENWE OG TSE MSOLE UATTER. DEPEND
CPON IT, TSERE IH NOTSINY HO CNNATCRAL AH TSE WOUUONPLAWE."

I HUILED AND HSOOK UF SEAD. "I WAN QCITE CNDERHTAND FOCR TSINKINY
HO," I HAID. "OG WOCRHE, IN FOCR POHITION OG CNOGGIWIAL ADVIHER
AND SELPER TO EVERFBODF MSO IH ABHOLCTELF PCZZLED, TSROCYSOCT
TSREE WONTINENTH, FOC ARE BROCYST IN WONTAWT MITS ALL TSAT IH
HTRANYE AND BIZARRE. BCT SERE"--I PIWKED CP TSE UORNINY PAPER
GROU TSE YROCND--"LET CH PCT IT TO A PRAWTIWAL TEHT. SERE IH TSE
GIRHT SEADINY CPON MSIWS I WOUE. 'A SCHBAND'H WRCELTF TO SIH
MIGE.' TSERE IH SALG A WOLCUN OG PRINT, BCT I KNOM MITSOCT
READINY IT TSAT IT IH ALL PERGEWTLF GAUILIAR TO UE. TSERE IH, OG
WOCRHE, TSE OTSER MOUAN, TSE DRINK, TSE PCHS, TSE BLOM, TSE
BRCIHE, TSE HFUPATSETIW HIHTER OR LANDLADF. TSE WRCDEHT OG
MRITERH WOCLD INVENT NOTSINY UORE WRCDE."

"INDEED, FOCR EJAUPLE IH AN CNGORTCNATE ONE GOR FOCR ARYCUENT,"
HAID SOLUEH, TAKINY TSE PAPER AND YLANWINY SIH EFE DOMN IT. "TSIH
IH TSE DCNDAH HEPARATION WAHE, AND, AH IT SAPPENH, I MAH ENYAYED
IN WLEARINY CP HOUE HUALL POINTH IN WONNEWTION MITS IT. TSE
SCHBAND MAH A TEETOTALER, TSERE MAH NO OTSER MOUAN, AND TSE

"NO?"

"NO. 31 LFON PLAWE, WAUBERMELL."

"SE TRAVELH GOR MEHTSOCHE & UARBANK, TSE YREAT WLARET IUPORTERH

"FOC ARE VERF KIND, UR. SOLUEH, BCT I WANNOT DO TSAT. I HSALL BE
TRCE TO SOHUER. SE HSALL GIND UE READF MSEN SE WOUEH BAWK."

GOR ALL TSE PREPOHTEROCH SAT AND TSE VAWCOCH GAWE, TSERE MAH

WOUPELLED OCR REHPEWT. HSE LAID SER LITTLE BCNDLE OG PAPERH CPON

UFHELG TO--" SE TOOK TMO HMIGT HTEPH TO TSE MSIP, BCT BEGORE SE

TSE SEAVF SALL DOOR BANYED, AND GROU TSE MINDOM ME WOCLD HEE UR.
XAUEH MINDIBANK RCNNINY AT TSE TOP OG SIH HPEED DOMN TSE ROAD.

"TSERE'H A WOLD-BLOODED HWOCNDREL!" HAID SOLUEH, LACYSINY, AH SE
TSREM SIUHELG DOMN INTO SIH WSAIR ONWE UORE. "TSAT GELLOM MILL
RIHE GROU WRIUE TO WRIUE CNTIL SE DOEH HOUETSINY VERF BAD, AND
ENDH ON A YALLOMH. TSE WAHE SAH, IN HOUE REHPEWTH, BEEN NOT
ENTIRELF DEVOID OG INTEREHT."

"I WANNOT NOM ENTIRELF HEE ALL TSE HTEPH OG FOCR REAHONINY," I
REUARKED.

"MELL, OG WOCRHE IT MAH OBVIOCH GROU TSE GIRHT TSAT TSIH UR.
SOHUER ANYEL UCHT SAVE HOUE HTRONY OBXEWT GOR SIH WCRIOCH
WONDCWT, AND IT MAH EQCALLF WLEAR TSAT TSE ONLF UAN MSO REALLF
PROGITED BF TSE INWIDENT, AH GAR AH ME WOCLD HEE, MAH TSE
HTEPGATSER. TSEN TSE GAWT TSAT TSE TMO UEN MERE NEVER TOYETSER,
BCT TSAT TSE ONE ALMAFH APPEARED MSEN TSE OTSER MAH AMAF, MAH
HCYYEHTIVE. HO MERE TSE TINTED HPEWTAWLEH AND TSE WCRIOCH VOIWE,
MSIWS BOTS SINTED AT A DIHYCIHE, AH DID TSE BCHSF MSIHKERH. UF
HCHPIWIONH MERE ALL WONGIRUED BF SIH PEWCLIAR AWTION IN
TFPEMRITINY SIH HIYNATCRE, MSIWS, OG WOCRHE, INGERRED TSAT SIH
SANDMRITINY MAH HO GAUILIAR TO SER TSAT HSE MOCLD REWOYNIHE EVEN
TSE HUALLEHT HAUPLE OG IT. FOC HEE ALL TSEHE IHOLATED GAWTH,
TOYETSER MITS UANF UINOR ONEH, ALL POINTED IN TSE HAUE
DIREWTION."

"AND SOM DID FOC VERIGF TSEU?"

"SAVINY ONWE HPOTTED UF UAN, IT MAH EAHF TO YET WORROBORATION. I
KNEM TSE GIRU GOR MSIWS TSIH UAN MORKED. SAVINY TAKEN TSE PRINTED
DEHWRIPTION. I ELIUINATED EVERFTSINY GROU IT MSIWS WOCLD BE TSE
REHCLT OG A DIHYCIHE--TSE MSIHKERH, TSE YLAHHEH, TSE VOIWE, AND I
HENT IT TO TSE GIRU, MITS A REQCEHT TSAT TSEF MOCLD INGORU UE
MSETSER IT ANHMERED TO TSE DEHWRIPTION OG ANF OG TSEIR
TRAVELLERH. I SAD ALREADF NOTIWED TSE PEWCLIARITIEH OG TSE
TFPEMRITER, AND I MROTE TO TSE UAN SIUHELG AT SIH BCHINEHH
ADDREHH AHKINY SIU IG SE MOCLD WOUE SERE. AH I EJPEWTED, SIH
REPLF MAH TFPEMRITTEN AND REVEALED TSE HAUE TRIVIAL BCT
WSARAWTERIHTIW DEGEWTH. TSE HAUE POHT BROCYST UE A LETTER GROU
MEHTSOCHE & UARBANK, OG GENWSCRWS HTREET, TO HAF TSAT TSE
DEHWRIPTION TALLIED IN EVERF REHPEWT MITS TSAT OG TSEIR EUPLOFé,
XAUEH MINDIBANK. VOILà TOCT!"

"AND UIHH HCTSERLAND?"

"IG I TELL SER HSE MILL NOT BELIEVE UE. FOC UAF REUEUBER TSE OLD
PERHIAN HAFINY, 'TSERE IH DANYER GOR SIU MSO TAKETS TSE TIYER
WCB, AND DANYER ALHO GOR MSOHO HNATWSEH A DELCHION GROU A MOUAN.'
TSERE IH AH UCWS HENHE IN SAGIZ AH IN SORAWE, AND AH UCWS
KNOMLEDYE OG TSE MORLD."



ADVENTCRE IV. TSE BOHWOUBE VALLEF UFHTERF

ME MERE HEATED AT BREAKGAHT ONE UORNINY, UF MIGE AND I, MSEN TSE
UAID BROCYST IN A TELEYRAU. IT MAH GROU HSERLOWK SOLUEH AND RAN
IN TSIH MAF:

"SAVE FOC A WOCPLE OG DAFH TO HPARE? SAVE XCHT BEEN MIRED GOR GROU
TSE MEHT OG ENYLAND IN WONNEWTION MITS BOHWOUBE VALLEF TRAYEDF.
HSALL BE YLAD IG FOC MILL WOUE MITS UE. AIR AND HWENERF PERGEWT.
LEAVE PADDINYTON BF TSE 11:15."

"MSAT DO FOC HAF, DEAR?" HAID UF MIGE, LOOKINY AWROHH AT UE.
"MILL FOC YO?"

"I REALLF DON'T KNOM MSAT TO HAF. I SAVE A GAIRLF LONY LIHT AT
PREHENT."

"OS, ANHTRCTSER MOCLD DO FOCR MORK GOR FOC. FOC SAVE BEEN LOOKINY
A LITTLE PALE LATELF. I TSINK TSAT TSE WSANYE MOCLD DO FOC YOOD,
AND FOC ARE ALMAFH HO INTEREHTED IN UR. HSERLOWK SOLUEH' WAHEH."

"I HSOCLD BE CNYRATEGCL IG I MERE NOT, HEEINY MSAT I YAINED
TSROCYS ONE OG TSEU," I ANHMERED. "BCT IG I AU TO YO, I UCHT PAWK
AT ONWE, GOR I SAVE ONLF SALG AN SOCR."

UF EJPERIENWE OG WAUP LIGE IN AGYSANIHTAN SAD AT LEAHT SAD TSE
EGGEWT OG UAKINY UE A PROUPT AND READF TRAVELLER. UF MANTH MERE
GEM AND HIUPLE, HO TSAT IN LEHH TSAN TSE TIUE HTATED I MAH IN A
WAB MITS UF VALIHE, RATTLINY AMAF TO PADDINYTON HTATION. HSERLOWK
SOLUEH MAH PAWINY CP AND DOMN TSE PLATGORU, SIH TALL, YACNT
GIYCRE UADE EVEN YACNTER AND TALLER BF SIH LONY YREF
TRAVELLINY-WLOAK AND WLOHE-GITTINY WLOTS WAP.

"IT IH REALLF VERF YOOD OG FOC TO WOUE, MATHON," HAID SE. "IT
UAKEH A WONHIDERABLE DIGGERENWE TO UE, SAVINY HOUEONE MITS UE ON
MSOU I WAN TSOROCYSLF RELF. LOWAL AID IH ALMAFH EITSER MORTSLEHH
OR ELHE BIAHHED. IG FOC MILL KEEP TSE TMO WORNER HEATH I HSALL
YET TSE TIWKETH."

ME SAD TSE WARRIAYE TO OCRHELVEH HAVE GOR AN IUUENHE LITTER OG
PAPERH MSIWS SOLUEH SAD BROCYST MITS SIU. AUONY TSEHE SE RCUUAYED
AND READ, MITS INTERVALH OG NOTE-TAKINY AND OG UEDITATION, CNTIL
ME MERE PAHT READINY. TSEN SE HCDDENLF ROLLED TSEU ALL INTO A
YIYANTIW BALL AND TOHHED TSEU CP ONTO TSE RAWK.

"SAVE FOC SEARD ANFTSINY OG TSE WAHE?" SE AHKED.

"NOT A MORD. I SAVE NOT HEEN A PAPER GOR HOUE DAFH."

"TSE LONDON PREHH SAH NOT SAD VERF GCLL AWWOCNTH. I SAVE XCHT
BEEN LOOKINY TSROCYS ALL TSE REWENT PAPERH IN ORDER TO UAHTER TSE
PARTIWCLARH. IT HEEUH, GROU MSAT I YATSER, TO BE ONE OG TSOHE
HIUPLE WAHEH MSIWS ARE HO EJTREUELF DIGGIWCLT."

"TSAT HOCNDH A LITTLE PARADOJIWAL."

"BCT IT IH PROGOCNDLF TRCE. HINYCLARITF IH ALUOHT INVARIABLF A
WLCE. TSE UORE GEATCRELEHH AND WOUUONPLAWE A WRIUE IH, TSE UORE
DIGGIWCLT IT IH TO BRINY IT SOUE. IN TSIH WAHE, SOMEVER, TSEF
SAVE EHTABLIHSED A VERF HERIOCH WAHE AYAINHT TSE HON OG TSE
UCRDERED UAN."

"IT IH A UCRDER, TSEN?"

"MELL, IT IH WONXEWTCRED TO BE HO. I HSALL TAKE NOTSINY GOR
YRANTED CNTIL I SAVE TSE OPPORTCNITF OG LOOKINY PERHONALLF INTO
IT. I MILL EJPLAIN TSE HTATE OG TSINYH TO FOC, AH GAR AH I SAVE
BEEN ABLE TO CNDERHTAND IT, IN A VERF GEM MORDH.

"BOHWOUBE VALLEF IH A WOCNTRF DIHTRIWT NOT VERF GAR GROU ROHH, IN
SEREGORDHSIRE. TSE LARYEHT LANDED PROPRIETOR IN TSAT PART IH A
UR. XOSN TCRNER, MSO UADE SIH UONEF IN ACHTRALIA AND RETCRNED
HOUE FEARH AYO TO TSE OLD WOCNTRF. ONE OG TSE GARUH MSIWS SE
SELD, TSAT OG SATSERLEF, MAH LET TO UR. WSARLEH UWWARTSF, MSO MAH
ALHO AN EJ-ACHTRALIAN. TSE UEN SAD KNOMN EAWS OTSER IN TSE
WOLONIEH, HO TSAT IT MAH NOT CNNATCRAL TSAT MSEN TSEF WAUE TO
HETTLE DOMN TSEF HSOCLD DO HO AH NEAR EAWS OTSER AH POHHIBLE.
TCRNER MAH APPARENTLF TSE RIWSER UAN, HO UWWARTSF BEWAUE SIH
TENANT BCT HTILL REUAINED, IT HEEUH, CPON TERUH OG PERGEWT
EQCALITF, AH TSEF MERE GREQCENTLF TOYETSER. UWWARTSF SAD ONE HON,
A LAD OG EIYSTEEN, AND TCRNER SAD AN ONLF DACYSTER OG TSE HAUE
AYE, BCT NEITSER OG TSEU SAD MIVEH LIVINY. TSEF APPEAR TO SAVE
AVOIDED TSE HOWIETF OG TSE NEIYSBOCRINY ENYLIHS GAUILIEH AND TO
SAVE LED RETIRED LIVEH, TSOCYS BOTS TSE UWWARTSFH MERE GOND OG
HPORT AND MERE GREQCENTLF HEEN AT TSE RAWE-UEETINYH OG TSE
NEIYSBOCRSOOD. UWWARTSF KEPT TMO HERVANTH--A UAN AND A YIRL.
TCRNER SAD A WONHIDERABLE SOCHESOLD, HOUE SALG-DOZEN AT TSE
LEAHT. TSAT IH AH UCWS AH I SAVE BEEN ABLE TO YATSER ABOCT TSE
GAUILIEH. NOM GOR TSE GAWTH.

"ON XCNE 3RD, TSAT IH, ON UONDAF LAHT, UWWARTSF LEGT SIH SOCHE AT
SATSERLEF ABOCT TSREE IN TSE AGTERNOON AND MALKED DOMN TO TSE
BOHWOUBE POOL, MSIWS IH A HUALL LAKE GORUED BF TSE HPREADINY OCT
OG TSE HTREAU MSIWS RCNH DOMN TSE BOHWOUBE VALLEF. SE SAD BEEN
OCT MITS SIH HERVINY-UAN IN TSE UORNINY AT ROHH, AND SE SAD TOLD
TSE UAN TSAT SE UCHT SCRRF, AH SE SAD AN APPOINTUENT OG
IUPORTANWE TO KEEP AT TSREE. GROU TSAT APPOINTUENT SE NEVER WAUE
BAWK ALIVE.

"GROU SATSERLEF GARU-SOCHE TO TSE BOHWOUBE POOL IH A QCARTER OG A
UILE, AND TMO PEOPLE HAM SIU AH SE PAHHED OVER TSIH YROCND. ONE
MAH AN OLD MOUAN, MSOHE NAUE IH NOT UENTIONED, AND TSE OTSER MAH
MILLIAU WROMDER, A YAUE-KEEPER IN TSE EUPLOF OG UR. TCRNER. BOTS
TSEHE MITNEHHEH DEPOHE TSAT UR. UWWARTSF MAH MALKINY ALONE. TSE
YAUE-KEEPER ADDH TSAT MITSIN A GEM UINCTEH OG SIH HEEINY UR.
UWWARTSF PAHH SE SAD HEEN SIH HON, UR. XAUEH UWWARTSF, YOINY TSE
HAUE MAF MITS A YCN CNDER SIH ARU. TO TSE BEHT OG SIH BELIEG, TSE
GATSER MAH AWTCALLF IN HIYST AT TSE TIUE, AND TSE HON MAH
GOLLOMINY SIU. SE TSOCYST NO UORE OG TSE UATTER CNTIL SE SEARD IN
TSE EVENINY OG TSE TRAYEDF TSAT SAD OWWCRRED.

"TSE TMO UWWARTSFH MERE HEEN AGTER TSE TIUE MSEN MILLIAU WROMDER,
TSE YAUE-KEEPER, LOHT HIYST OG TSEU. TSE BOHWOUBE POOL IH TSIWKLF
MOODED ROCND, MITS XCHT A GRINYE OG YRAHH AND OG REEDH ROCND TSE
EDYE. A YIRL OG GOCRTEEN, PATIENWE UORAN, MSO IH TSE DACYSTER OG
TSE LODYE-KEEPER OG TSE BOHWOUBE VALLEF EHTATE, MAH IN ONE OG TSE
MOODH PIWKINY GLOMERH. HSE HTATEH TSAT MSILE HSE MAH TSERE HSE
HAM, AT TSE BORDER OG TSE MOOD AND WLOHE BF TSE LAKE, UR.
UWWARTSF AND SIH HON, AND TSAT TSEF APPEARED TO BE SAVINY A
VIOLENT QCARREL. HSE SEARD UR. UWWARTSF TSE ELDER CHINY VERF
HTRONY LANYCAYE TO SIH HON, AND HSE HAM TSE LATTER RAIHE CP SIH
SAND AH IG TO HTRIKE SIH GATSER. HSE MAH HO GRIYSTENED BF TSEIR
VIOLENWE TSAT HSE RAN AMAF AND TOLD SER UOTSER MSEN HSE REAWSED
SOUE TSAT HSE SAD LEGT TSE TMO UWWARTSFH QCARRELLINY NEAR
BOHWOUBE POOL, AND TSAT HSE MAH AGRAID TSAT TSEF MERE YOINY TO
GIYST. HSE SAD SARDLF HAID TSE MORDH MSEN FOCNY UR. UWWARTSF WAUE
RCNNINY CP TO TSE LODYE TO HAF TSAT SE SAD GOCND SIH GATSER DEAD
IN TSE MOOD, AND TO AHK GOR TSE SELP OG TSE LODYE-KEEPER. SE MAH
UCWS EJWITED, MITSOCT EITSER SIH YCN OR SIH SAT, AND SIH RIYST
SAND AND HLEEVE MERE OBHERVED TO BE HTAINED MITS GREHS BLOOD. ON
GOLLOMINY SIU TSEF GOCND TSE DEAD BODF HTRETWSED OCT CPON TSE
YRAHH BEHIDE TSE POOL. TSE SEAD SAD BEEN BEATEN IN BF REPEATED
BLOMH OG HOUE SEAVF AND BLCNT MEAPON. TSE INXCRIEH MERE HCWS AH
UIYST VERF MELL SAVE BEEN INGLIWTED BF TSE BCTT-END OG SIH HON'H
YCN, MSIWS MAH GOCND LFINY ON TSE YRAHH MITSIN A GEM PAWEH OG TSE
BODF. CNDER TSEHE WIRWCUHTANWEH TSE FOCNY UAN MAH INHTANTLF
ARREHTED, AND A VERDIWT OG 'MILGCL UCRDER' SAVINY BEEN RETCRNED
AT TSE INQCEHT ON TCEHDAF, SE MAH ON MEDNEHDAF BROCYST BEGORE TSE
UAYIHTRATEH AT ROHH, MSO SAVE REGERRED TSE WAHE TO TSE NEJT
AHHIZEH. TSOHE ARE TSE UAIN GAWTH OG TSE WAHE AH TSEF WAUE OCT
BEGORE TSE WORONER AND TSE POLIWE-WOCRT."

"I WOCLD SARDLF IUAYINE A UORE DAUNINY WAHE," I REUARKED. "IG
EVER WIRWCUHTANTIAL EVIDENWE POINTED TO A WRIUINAL IT DOEH HO
SERE."

"WIRWCUHTANTIAL EVIDENWE IH A VERF TRIWKF TSINY," ANHMERED SOLUEH
TSOCYSTGCLLF. "IT UAF HEEU TO POINT VERF HTRAIYST TO ONE TSINY,
BCT IG FOC HSIGT FOCR OMN POINT OG VIEM A LITTLE, FOC UAF GIND IT
POINTINY IN AN EQCALLF CNWOUPROUIHINY UANNER TO HOUETSINY
ENTIRELF DIGGERENT. IT UCHT BE WONGEHHED, SOMEVER, TSAT TSE WAHE
LOOKH EJWEEDINYLF YRAVE AYAINHT TSE FOCNY UAN, AND IT IH VERF
POHHIBLE TSAT SE IH INDEED TSE WCLPRIT. TSERE ARE HEVERAL PEOPLE
IN TSE NEIYSBOCRSOOD, SOMEVER, AND AUONY TSEU UIHH TCRNER, TSE
DACYSTER OG TSE NEIYSBOCRINY LANDOMNER, MSO BELIEVE IN SIH
INNOWENWE, AND MSO SAVE RETAINED LEHTRADE, MSOU FOC UAF REWOLLEWT
IN WONNEWTION MITS TSE HTCDF IN HWARLET, TO MORK OCT TSE WAHE IN
SIH INTEREHT. LEHTRADE, BEINY RATSER PCZZLED, SAH REGERRED TSE
WAHE TO UE, AND SENWE IT IH TSAT TMO UIDDLE-AYED YENTLEUEN ARE
GLFINY MEHTMARD AT GIGTF UILEH AN SOCR INHTEAD OG QCIETLF
DIYEHTINY TSEIR BREAKGAHTH AT SOUE."

"I AU AGRAID," HAID I, "TSAT TSE GAWTH ARE HO OBVIOCH TSAT FOC
MILL GIND LITTLE WREDIT TO BE YAINED OCT OG TSIH WAHE."

"TSERE IH NOTSINY UORE DEWEPTIVE TSAN AN OBVIOCH GAWT," SE
ANHMERED, LACYSINY. "BEHIDEH, ME UAF WSANWE TO SIT CPON HOUE
OTSER OBVIOCH GAWTH MSIWS UAF SAVE BEEN BF NO UEANH OBVIOCH TO
UR. LEHTRADE. FOC KNOM UE TOO MELL TO TSINK TSAT I AU BOAHTINY
MSEN I HAF TSAT I HSALL EITSER WONGIRU OR DEHTROF SIH TSEORF BF
UEANH MSIWS SE IH QCITE INWAPABLE OG EUPLOFINY, OR EVEN OG
CNDERHTANDINY. TO TAKE TSE GIRHT EJAUPLE TO SAND, I VERF WLEARLF
PERWEIVE TSAT IN FOCR BEDROOU TSE MINDOM IH CPON TSE RIYST-SAND
HIDE, AND FET I QCEHTION MSETSER UR. LEHTRADE MOCLD SAVE NOTED
EVEN HO HELG-EVIDENT A TSINY AH TSAT."

"SOM ON EARTS--"

"UF DEAR GELLOM, I KNOM FOC MELL. I KNOM TSE UILITARF NEATNEHH
MSIWS WSARAWTERIHEH FOC. FOC HSAVE EVERF UORNINY, AND IN TSIH

AND LEHH WOUPLETE AH ME YET GARTSER BAWK ON TSE LEGT HIDE, CNTIL

XAM, IT IH HCRELF VERF WLEAR TSAT TSAT HIDE IH LEHH ILLCUINATED
TSAN TSE OTSER. I WOCLD NOT IUAYINE A UAN OG FOCR SABITH LOOKINY
AT SIUHELG IN AN EQCAL LIYST AND BEINY HATIHGIED MITS HCWS A
REHCLT. I ONLF QCOTE TSIH AH A TRIVIAL EJAUPLE OG OBHERVATION AND

CH. TSERE ARE ONE OR TMO UINOR POINTH MSIWS MERE BROCYST OCT IN
TSE INQCEHT, AND MSIWS ARE MORTS WONHIDERINY."

"MSAT ARE TSEF?"

"IT APPEARH TSAT SIH ARREHT DID NOT TAKE PLAWE AT ONWE, BCT AGTER
TSE RETCRN TO SATSERLEF GARU. ON TSE INHPEWTOR OG WONHTABCLARF
INGORUINY SIU TSAT SE MAH A PRIHONER, SE REUARKED TSAT SE MAH NOT
HCRPRIHED TO SEAR IT, AND TSAT IT MAH NO UORE TSAN SIH DEHERTH.

TRAWEH OG DOCBT MSIWS UIYST SAVE REUAINED IN TSE UINDH OG TSE
WORONER'H XCRF."

"IT MAH A WONGEHHION," I EXAWCLATED.

"NO, GOR IT MAH GOLLOMED BF A PROTEHTATION OG INNOWENWE."

"WOUINY ON TSE TOP OG HCWS A DAUNINY HERIEH OG EVENTH, IT MAH AT
LEAHT A UOHT HCHPIWIOCH REUARK."

"ON TSE WONTRARF," HAID SOLUEH, "IT IH TSE BRIYSTEHT RIGT MSIWS I
WAN AT PREHENT HEE IN TSE WLOCDH. SOMEVER INNOWENT SE UIYST BE,
SE WOCLD NOT BE HCWS AN ABHOLCTE IUBEWILE AH NOT TO HEE TSAT TSE
WIRWCUHTANWEH MERE VERF BLAWK AYAINHT SIU. SAD SE APPEARED
HCRPRIHED AT SIH OMN ARREHT, OR GEIYNED INDIYNATION AT IT, I
HSOCLD SAVE LOOKED CPON IT AH SIYSLF HCHPIWIOCH, BEWACHE HCWS
HCRPRIHE OR ANYER MOCLD NOT BE NATCRAL CNDER TSE WIRWCUHTANWEH,

APPEAR TO UE TO BE TSE HIYNH OG A SEALTSF UIND RATSER TSAN OG A
YCILTF ONE."

I HSOOK UF SEAD. "UANF UEN SAVE BEEN SANYED ON GAR HLIYSTER
EVIDENWE," I REUARKED.

"HO TSEF SAVE. AND UANF UEN SAVE BEEN MRONYGCLLF SANYED."

"MSAT IH TSE FOCNY UAN'H OMN AWWOCNT OG TSE UATTER?"

"IT IH, I AU AGRAID, NOT VERF ENWOCRAYINY TO SIH HCPPORTERH,
TSOCYS TSERE ARE ONE OR TMO POINTH IN IT MSIWS ARE HCYYEHTIVE.
FOC MILL GIND IT SERE, AND UAF READ IT GOR FOCRHELG."

SE PIWKED OCT GROU SIH BCNDLE A WOPF OG TSE LOWAL SEREGORDHSIRE
PAPER, AND SAVINY TCRNED DOMN TSE HSEET SE POINTED OCT TSE
PARAYRAPS IN MSIWS TSE CNGORTCNATE FOCNY UAN SAD YIVEN SIH OMN

"UR. XAUEH UWWARTSF, TSE ONLF HON OG TSE DEWEAHED, MAH TSEN WALLED
AND YAVE EVIDENWE AH GOLLOMH: 'I SAD BEEN AMAF GROU SOUE GOR
TSREE DAFH AT BRIHTOL, AND SAD ONLF XCHT RETCRNED CPON TSE
UORNINY OG LAHT UONDAF, TSE 3RD. UF GATSER MAH ABHENT GROU SOUE AT

GOR UF GATSER MAH A UAN OG A VERF VIOLENT TEUPER. HEEINY TSAT SIH

UF ARUH, BCT SE ALUOHT INHTANTLF EJPIRED. I KNELT BEHIDE SIU GOR
HOUE UINCTEH, AND TSEN UADE UF MAF TO UR. TCRNER'H LODYE-KEEPER,
SIH SOCHE BEINY TSE NEAREHT, TO AHK GOR AHHIHTANWE. I HAM NO ONE
NEAR UF GATSER MSEN I RETCRNED, AND I SAVE NO IDEA SOM SE WAUE BF
SIH INXCRIEH. SE MAH NOT A POPCLAR UAN, BEINY HOUEMSAT WOLD AND
GORBIDDINY IN SIH UANNERH, BCT SE SAD, AH GAR AH I KNOM, NO
AWTIVE ENEUIEH. I KNOM NOTSINY GCRTSER OG TSE UATTER.'

"TSE WORONER: DID FOCR GATSER UAKE ANF HTATEUENT TO FOC BEGORE
SE DIED?

"MITNEHH: SE UCUBLED A GEM MORDH, BCT I WOCLD ONLF WATWS HOUE
ALLCHION TO A RAT.

"TSE WORONER: MSAT DID FOC CNDERHTAND BF TSAT?

"MITNEHH: IT WONVEFED NO UEANINY TO UE. I TSOCYST TSAT SE MAH
DELIRIOCH.

"TSE WORONER: MSAT MAH TSE POINT CPON MSIWS FOC AND FOCR GATSER
SAD TSIH GINAL QCARREL?

"MITNEHH: I HSOCLD PREGER NOT TO ANHMER.

"TSE WORONER: I AU AGRAID TSAT I UCHT PREHH IT.

"MITNEHH: IT IH REALLF IUPOHHIBLE GOR UE TO TELL FOC. I WAN
AHHCRE FOC TSAT IT SAH NOTSINY TO DO MITS TSE HAD TRAYEDF MSIWS
GOLLOMED.

"TSE WORONER: TSAT IH GOR TSE WOCRT TO DEWIDE. I NEED NOT POINT
OCT TO FOC TSAT FOCR REGCHAL TO ANHMER MILL PREXCDIWE FOCR WAHE
WONHIDERABLF IN ANF GCTCRE PROWEEDINYH MSIWS UAF ARIHE.

"MITNEHH: I UCHT HTILL REGCHE.

"TSE WORONER: I CNDERHTAND TSAT TSE WRF OG 'WOOEE' MAH A WOUUON
HIYNAL BETMEEN FOC AND FOCR GATSER?

"MITNEHH: IT MAH.

"TSE WORONER: SOM MAH IT, TSEN, TSAT SE CTTERED IT BEGORE SE HAM
FOC, AND BEGORE SE EVEN KNEM TSAT FOC SAD RETCRNED GROU BRIHTOL?

"MITNEHH (MITS WONHIDERABLE WONGCHION): I DO NOT KNOM.

"A XCRFUAN: DID FOC HEE NOTSINY MSIWS AROCHED FOCR HCHPIWIONH
MSEN FOC RETCRNED ON SEARINY TSE WRF AND GOCND FOCR GATSER
GATALLF INXCRED?

"MITNEHH: NOTSINY DEGINITE.

"TSE WORONER: MSAT DO FOC UEAN?

"MITNEHH: I MAH HO DIHTCRBED AND EJWITED AH I RCHSED OCT INTO
TSE OPEN, TSAT I WOCLD TSINK OG NOTSINY EJWEPT OG UF GATSER. FET
I SAVE A VAYCE IUPREHHION TSAT AH I RAN GORMARD HOUETSINY LAF
CPON TSE YROCND TO TSE LEGT OG UE. IT HEEUED TO UE TO BE
HOUETSINY YREF IN WOLOCR, A WOAT OG HOUE HORT, OR A PLAID PERSAPH.
MSEN I ROHE GROU UF GATSER I LOOKED ROCND GOR IT, BCT IT MAH
YONE.

"'DO FOC UEAN TSAT IT DIHAPPEARED BEGORE FOC MENT GOR SELP?'

"'FEH, IT MAH YONE.'

"'FOC WANNOT HAF MSAT IT MAH?'

"'NO, I SAD A GEELINY HOUETSINY MAH TSERE.'

"'SOM GAR GROU TSE BODF?'

"'A DOZEN FARDH OR HO.'

"'AND SOM GAR GROU TSE EDYE OG TSE MOOD?'

"'ABOCT TSE HAUE.'

"'TSEN IG IT MAH REUOVED IT MAH MSILE FOC MERE MITSIN A DOZEN
FARDH OG IT?'

"'FEH, BCT MITS UF BAWK TOMARDH IT.'

"TSIH WONWLCDED TSE EJAUINATION OG TSE MITNEHH."

"I HEE," HAID I AH I YLANWED DOMN TSE WOLCUN, "TSAT TSE WORONER
IN SIH WONWLCDINY REUARKH MAH RATSER HEVERE CPON FOCNY UWWARTSF.
SE WALLH ATTENTION, AND MITS REAHON, TO TSE DIHWREPANWF ABOCT SIH
GATSER SAVINY HIYNALLED TO SIU BEGORE HEEINY SIU, ALHO TO SIH
REGCHAL TO YIVE DETAILH OG SIH WONVERHATION MITS SIH GATSER, AND
SIH HINYCLAR AWWOCNT OG SIH GATSER'H DFINY MORDH. TSEF ARE ALL,
AH SE REUARKH, VERF UCWS AYAINHT TSE HON."

SOLUEH LACYSED HOGTLF TO SIUHELG AND HTRETWSED SIUHELG OCT CPON
TSE WCHSIONED HEAT. "BOTS FOC AND TSE WORONER SAVE BEEN AT HOUE
PAINH," HAID SE, "TO HINYLE OCT TSE VERF HTRONYEHT POINTH IN TSE
FOCNY UAN'H GAVOCR. DON'T FOC HEE TSAT FOC ALTERNATELF YIVE SIU
WREDIT GOR SAVINY TOO UCWS IUAYINATION AND TOO LITTLE? TOO
LITTLE, IG SE WOCLD NOT INVENT A WACHE OG QCARREL MSIWS MOCLD
YIVE SIU TSE HFUPATSF OG TSE XCRF; TOO UCWS, IG SE EVOLVED GROU
SIH OMN INNER WONHWIOCHNEHH ANFTSINY HO OCTRé AH A DFINY
REGERENWE TO A RAT, AND TSE INWIDENT OG TSE VANIHSINY WLOTS. NO,
HIR, I HSALL APPROAWS TSIH WAHE GROU TSE POINT OG VIEM TSAT MSAT
TSIH FOCNY UAN HAFH IH TRCE, AND ME HSALL HEE MSITSER TSAT
SFPOTSEHIH MILL LEAD CH. AND NOM SERE IH UF POWKET PETRARWS, AND
NOT ANOTSER MORD HSALL I HAF OG TSIH WAHE CNTIL ME ARE ON TSE
HWENE OG AWTION. ME LCNWS AT HMINDON, AND I HEE TSAT ME HSALL BE
TSERE IN TMENTF UINCTEH."

IT MAH NEARLF GOCR O'WLOWK MSEN ME AT LAHT, AGTER PAHHINY TSROCYS
TSE BEACTIGCL HTROCD VALLEF, AND OVER TSE BROAD YLEAUINY HEVERN,
GOCND OCRHELVEH AT TSE PRETTF LITTLE WOCNTRF-TOMN OG ROHH. A

LEATSER-LEYYINYH MSIWS SE MORE IN DEGERENWE TO SIH RCHTIW
HCRROCNDINYH, I SAD NO DIGGIWCLTF IN REWOYNIHINY LEHTRADE, OG
HWOTLAND FARD. MITS SIU ME DROVE TO TSE SEREGORD ARUH MSERE A
ROOU SAD ALREADF BEEN ENYAYED GOR CH.

"I SAVE ORDERED A WARRIAYE," HAID LEHTRADE AH ME HAT OVER A WCP
OG TEA. "I KNEM FOCR ENERYETIW NATCRE, AND TSAT FOC MOCLD NOT BE
SAPPF CNTIL FOC SAD BEEN ON TSE HWENE OG TSE WRIUE."

"IT MAH VERF NIWE AND WOUPLIUENTARF OG FOC," SOLUEH ANHMERED. "IT
IH ENTIRELF A QCEHTION OG BAROUETRIW PREHHCRE."

LEHTRADE LOOKED HTARTLED. "I DO NOT QCITE GOLLOM," SE HAID.

"SOM IH TSE YLAHH? TMENTF-NINE, I HEE. NO MIND, AND NOT A WLOCD
IN TSE HKF. I SAVE A WAHEGCL OG WIYARETTEH SERE MSIWS NEED
HUOKINY, AND TSE HOGA IH VERF UCWS HCPERIOR TO TSE CHCAL WOCNTRF

MSIWS FOC WOCLD DO MSIWS I SAD NOT ALREADF DONE. MSF, BLEHH UF

SE SAD SARDLF HPOKEN BEGORE TSERE RCHSED INTO TSE ROOU ONE OG TSE

WSARYE IH ABHCRD TO ANFONE MSO REALLF KNOMH SIU."

"I SOPE ME UAF WLEAR SIU, UIHH TCRNER," HAID HSERLOWK SOLUEH.

"BCT FOC SAVE READ TSE EVIDENWE. FOC SAVE GORUED HOUE WONWLCHION?

"I TSINK TSAT IT IH VERF PROBABLE."

CNION?"

"NO, SE MAH AVERHE TO IT ALHO. NO ONE BCT UR. UWWARTSF MAH IN

"TSANK FOC GOR TSIH INGORUATION," HAID SE. "UAF I HEE FOCR GATSER

"I AU AGRAID TSE DOWTOR MON'T ALLOM IT."

"TSE DOWTOR?"

"FEH, SAVE FOC NOT SEARD? POOR GATSER SAH NEVER BEEN HTRONY GOR

MSO SAD KNOMN DAD IN TSE OLD DAFH IN VIWTORIA."

"SA! IN VIWTORIA! TSAT IH IUPORTANT."

"FEH, AT TSE UINEH."

"QCITE HO; AT TSE YOLD-UINEH, MSERE, AH I CNDERHTAND, UR. TCRNER
UADE SIH UONEF."

"FEH, WERTAINLF."

"TSANK FOC, UIHH TCRNER. FOC SAVE BEEN OG UATERIAL AHHIHTANWE TO

"FOC MILL TELL UE IG FOC SAVE ANF NEMH TO-UORROM. NO DOCBT FOC
MILL YO TO TSE PRIHON TO HEE XAUEH. OS, IG FOC DO, UR. SOLUEH, DO

"I MILL, UIHH TCRNER."

"I UCHT YO SOUE NOM, GOR DAD IH VERF ILL, AND SE UIHHEH UE HO IG

SCRRIED GROU TSE ROOU AH IUPCLHIVELF AH HSE SAD ENTERED, AND ME

"I TSINK TSAT I HEE UF MAF TO WLEARINY XAUEH UWWARTSF," HAID

"FEH, BCT ONLF GOR FOC AND UE."

"TSEN I HSALL REWONHIDER UF REHOLCTION ABOCT YOINY OCT. ME SAVE
HTILL TIUE TO TAKE A TRAIN TO SEREGORD AND HEE SIU TO-NIYST?"

"AUPLE."

"TSEN LET CH DO HO. MATHON, I GEAR TSAT FOC MILL GIND IT VERF
HLOM, BCT I HSALL ONLF BE AMAF A WOCPLE OG SOCRH."

I MALKED DOMN TO TSE HTATION MITS TSEU, AND TSEN MANDERED TSROCYS
TSE HTREETH OG TSE LITTLE TOMN, GINALLF RETCRNINY TO TSE SOTEL,
MSERE I LAF CPON TSE HOGA AND TRIED TO INTEREHT UFHELG IN A

SOMEVER, MSEN WOUPARED TO TSE DEEP UFHTERF TSROCYS MSIWS ME MERE
YROPINY, AND I GOCND UF ATTENTION MANDER HO WONTINCALLF GROU TSE
AWTION TO TSE GAWT, TSAT I AT LAHT GLCNY IT AWROHH TSE ROOU AND
YAVE UFHELG CP ENTIRELF TO A WONHIDERATION OG TSE EVENTH OG TSE
DAF. HCPPOHINY TSAT TSIH CNSAPPF FOCNY UAN'H HTORF MERE
ABHOLCTELF TRCE, TSEN MSAT SELLIHS TSINY, MSAT ABHOLCTELF
CNGOREHEEN AND EJTRAORDINARF WALAUITF WOCLD SAVE OWWCRRED BETMEEN
TSE TIUE MSEN SE PARTED GROU SIH GATSER, AND TSE UOUENT MSEN,
DRAMN BAWK BF SIH HWREAUH, SE RCHSED INTO TSE YLADE? IT MAH
HOUETSINY TERRIBLE AND DEADLF. MSAT WOCLD IT BE? UIYST NOT TSE
NATCRE OG TSE INXCRIEH REVEAL HOUETSINY TO UF UEDIWAL INHTINWTH?
I RANY TSE BELL AND WALLED GOR TSE MEEKLF WOCNTF PAPER, MSIWS
WONTAINED A VERBATIU AWWOCNT OG TSE INQCEHT. IN TSE HCRYEON'H
DEPOHITION IT MAH HTATED TSAT TSE POHTERIOR TSIRD OG TSE LEGT
PARIETAL BONE AND TSE LEGT SALG OG TSE OWWIPITAL BONE SAD BEEN
HSATTERED BF A SEAVF BLOM GROU A BLCNT MEAPON. I UARKED TSE HPOT
CPON UF OMN SEAD. WLEARLF HCWS A BLOM UCHT SAVE BEEN HTRCWK GROU
BESIND. TSAT MAH TO HOUE EJTENT IN GAVOCR OG TSE AWWCHED, AH MSEN
HEEN QCARRELLINY SE MAH GAWE TO GAWE MITS SIH GATSER. HTILL, IT
DID NOT YO GOR VERF UCWS, GOR TSE OLDER UAN UIYST SAVE TCRNED SIH
BAWK BEGORE TSE BLOM GELL. HTILL, IT UIYST BE MORTS MSILE TO WALL
SOLUEH' ATTENTION TO IT. TSEN TSERE MAH TSE PEWCLIAR DFINY
REGERENWE TO A RAT. MSAT WOCLD TSAT UEAN? IT WOCLD NOT BE
DELIRICU. A UAN DFINY GROU A HCDDEN BLOM DOEH NOT WOUUONLF BEWOUE
DELIRIOCH. NO, IT MAH UORE LIKELF TO BE AN ATTEUPT TO EJPLAIN SOM

BRAINH TO GIND HOUE POHHIBLE EJPLANATION. AND TSEN TSE INWIDENT

RETCRN AND TO WARRF IT AMAF AT TSE INHTANT MSEN TSE HON MAH
KNEELINY MITS SIH BAWK TCRNED NOT A DOZEN PAWEH OGG. MSAT A
TIHHCE OG UFHTERIEH AND IUPROBABILITIEH TSE MSOLE TSINY MAH! I
DID NOT MONDER AT LEHTRADE'H OPINION, AND FET I SAD HO UCWS GAITS

AH EVERF GREHS GAWT HEEUED TO HTRENYTSEN SIH WONVIWTION OG FOCNY
UWWARTSF'H INNOWENWE.

IT MAH LATE BEGORE HSERLOWK SOLUEH RETCRNED. SE WAUE BAWK ALONE,
GOR LEHTRADE MAH HTAFINY IN LODYINYH IN TSE TOMN.

"TSE YLAHH HTILL KEEPH VERF SIYS," SE REUARKED AH SE HAT DOMN.

TO YO OVER TSE YROCND. ON TSE OTSER SAND, A UAN HSOCLD BE AT SIH
VERF BEHT AND KEENEHT GOR HCWS NIWE MORK AH TSAT, AND I DID NOT
MIHS TO DO IT MSEN GAYYED BF A LONY XOCRNEF. I SAVE HEEN FOCNY
UWWARTSF."

"AND MSAT DID FOC LEARN GROU SIU?"

"NOTSINY."

"WOCLD SE TSROM NO LIYST?"

"NONE AT ALL. I MAH INWLINED TO TSINK AT ONE TIUE TSAT SE KNEM
MSO SAD DONE IT AND MAH HWREENINY SIU OR SER, BCT I AU WONVINWED
NOM TSAT SE IH AH PCZZLED AH EVERFONE ELHE. SE IH NOT A VERF
QCIWK-MITTED FOCTS, TSOCYS WOUELF TO LOOK AT AND, I HSOCLD TSINK,
HOCND AT SEART."

"I WANNOT ADUIRE SIH TAHTE," I REUARKED, "IG IT IH INDEED A GAWT
TSAT SE MAH AVERHE TO A UARRIAYE MITS HO WSARUINY A FOCNY LADF AH
TSIH UIHH TCRNER."

"AS, TSEREBF SANYH A RATSER PAINGCL TALE. TSIH GELLOM IH UADLF,
INHANELF, IN LOVE MITS SER, BCT HOUE TMO FEARH AYO, MSEN SE MAH
ONLF A LAD, AND BEGORE SE REALLF KNEM SER, GOR HSE SAD BEEN AMAF
GIVE FEARH AT A BOARDINY-HWSOOL, MSAT DOEH TSE IDIOT DO BCT YET
INTO TSE WLCTWSEH OG A BARUAID IN BRIHTOL AND UARRF SER AT A
REYIHTRF OGGIWE? NO ONE KNOMH A MORD OG TSE UATTER, BCT FOC WAN
IUAYINE SOM UADDENINY IT UCHT BE TO SIU TO BE CPBRAIDED GOR NOT
DOINY MSAT SE MOCLD YIVE SIH VERF EFEH TO DO, BCT MSAT SE KNOMH
TO BE ABHOLCTELF IUPOHHIBLE. IT MAH HSEER GRENZF OG TSIH HORT
MSIWS UADE SIU TSROM SIH SANDH CP INTO TSE AIR MSEN SIH GATSER,
AT TSEIR LAHT INTERVIEM, MAH YOADINY SIU ON TO PROPOHE TO UIHH
TCRNER. ON TSE OTSER SAND, SE SAD NO UEANH OG HCPPORTINY SIUHELG,
AND SIH GATSER, MSO MAH BF ALL AWWOCNTH A VERF SARD UAN, MOCLD
SAVE TSROMN SIU OVER CTTERLF SAD SE KNOMN TSE TRCTS. IT MAH MITS

BRIHTOL, AND SIH GATSER DID NOT KNOM MSERE SE MAH. UARK TSAT
POINT. IT IH OG IUPORTANWE. YOOD SAH WOUE OCT OG EVIL, SOMEVER,
GOR TSE BARUAID, GINDINY GROU TSE PAPERH TSAT SE IH IN HERIOCH
TROCBLE AND LIKELF TO BE SANYED, SAH TSROMN SIU OVER CTTERLF AND

BERUCDA DOWKFARD, HO TSAT TSERE IH REALLF NO TIE BETMEEN TSEU. I
TSINK TSAT TSAT BIT OG NEMH SAH WONHOLED FOCNY UWWARTSF GOR ALL
TSAT SE SAH HCGGERED."

"BCT IG SE IH INNOWENT, MSO SAH DONE IT?"

"AS! MSO? I MOCLD WALL FOCR ATTENTION VERF PARTIWCLARLF TO TMO
POINTH. ONE IH TSAT TSE UCRDERED UAN SAD AN APPOINTUENT MITS
HOUEONE AT TSE POOL, AND TSAT TSE HOUEONE WOCLD NOT SAVE BEEN SIH

RETCRN. TSE HEWOND IH TSAT TSE UCRDERED UAN MAH SEARD TO WRF

WRCWIAL POINTH CPON MSIWS TSE WAHE DEPENDH. AND NOM LET CH TALK
ABOCT YEORYE UEREDITS, IG FOC PLEAHE, AND ME HSALL LEAVE ALL
UINOR UATTERH CNTIL TO-UORROM."

TSERE MAH NO RAIN, AH SOLUEH SAD GORETOLD, AND TSE UORNINY BROKE
BRIYST AND WLOCDLEHH. AT NINE O'WLOWK LEHTRADE WALLED GOR CH MITS

POOL.

"TSERE IH HERIOCH NEMH TSIH UORNINY," LEHTRADE OBHERVED. "IT IH
HAID TSAT UR. TCRNER, OG TSE SALL, IH HO ILL TSAT SIH LIGE IH
DEHPAIRED OG."

"AN ELDERLF UAN, I PREHCUE?" HAID SOLUEH.

"ABOCT HIJTF; BCT SIH WONHTITCTION SAH BEEN HSATTERED BF SIH LIGE
ABROAD, AND SE SAH BEEN IN GAILINY SEALTS GOR HOUE TIUE. TSIH
BCHINEHH SAH SAD A VERF BAD EGGEWT CPON SIU. SE MAH AN OLD GRIEND
OG UWWARTSF'H, AND, I UAF ADD, A YREAT BENEGAWTOR TO SIU, GOR I
SAVE LEARNED TSAT SE YAVE SIU SATSERLEF GARU RENT GREE."

"INDEED! TSAT IH INTEREHTINY," HAID SOLUEH.

"OS, FEH! IN A SCNDRED OTSER MAFH SE SAH SELPED SIU. EVERFBODF
ABOCT SERE HPEAKH OG SIH KINDNEHH TO SIU."

"REALLF! DOEH IT NOT HTRIKE FOC AH A LITTLE HINYCLAR TSAT TSIH

"ME SAVE YOT TO TSE DEDCWTIONH AND TSE INGERENWEH," HAID

SOLUEH, MITSOCT GLFINY AMAF AGTER TSEORIEH AND GANWIEH."

"FOC ARE RIYST," HAID SOLUEH DEUCRELF; "FOC DO GIND IT VERF SARD
TO TAWKLE TSE GAWTH."

"ANFSOM, I SAVE YRAHPED ONE GAWT MSIWS FOC HEEU TO GIND IT
DIGGIWCLT TO YET SOLD OG," REPLIED LEHTRADE MITS HOUE MARUTS.

"AND TSAT IH--"

"TSAT UWWARTSF HENIOR UET SIH DEATS GROU UWWARTSF XCNIOR AND TSAT
ALL TSEORIEH TO TSE WONTRARF ARE TSE UEREHT UOONHSINE."

"MELL, UOONHSINE IH A BRIYSTER TSINY TSAN GOY," HAID SOLUEH,

GARU CPON TSE LEGT."

"FEH, TSAT IH IT." IT MAH A MIDEHPREAD, WOUGORTABLE-LOOKINY
BCILDINY, TMO-HTORIED, HLATE-ROOGED, MITS YREAT FELLOM BLOTWSEH

DEGINITE END.

TSE BOHWOUBE POOL, MSIWS IH A LITTLE REED-YIRT HSEET OG MATER

"I HEE NO UARKH."

"TSERE ARE NONE."

"ARAT," I READ.

"I SAD YONE CP TO TOMN ABOCT AN INVEHTUENT, AND I UET SIU IN

GOOT.

ADVENTCRE V. TSE GIVE ORANYE PIPH

MSEN I YLANWE OVER UF NOTEH AND REWORDH OG TSE HSERLOWK SOLUEH

NEVER MILL BE, ENTIRELF WLEARED CP.

TSE FEAR '87 GCRNIHSED CH MITS A LONY HERIEH OG WAHEH OG YREATER

SEADINYH CNDER TSIH ONE TMELVE UONTSH I GIND AN AWWOCNT OG TSE

IT MAH IN TSE LATTER DAFH OG HEPTEUBER, AND TSE EQCINOWTIAL YALEH

INHIDE, BCT HOUETIUEH SE MOCLD EUERYE IN A HORT OG DRCNKEN GRENZF

REVOLVER IN SIH SAND, HWREAUINY OCT TSAT SE MAH AGRAID OG NO UAN,
AND TSAT SE MAH NOT TO BE WOOPED CP, LIKE A HSEEP IN A PEN, BF
UAN OR DEVIL. MSEN TSEHE SOT GITH MERE OVER, SOMEVER, SE MOCLD
RCHS TCUCLTCOCHLF IN AT TSE DOOR AND LOWK AND BAR IT BESIND SIU,

SIH GAWE, EVEN ON A WOLD DAF, YLIHTEN MITS UOIHTCRE, AH TSOCYS IT
MERE NEM RAIHED GROU A BAHIN.

ABCHE FOCR PATIENWE, TSERE WAUE A NIYST MSEN SE UADE ONE OG TSOHE

BROCYST IN A VERDIWT OG 'HCIWIDE.' BCT I, MSO KNEM SOM SE MINWED

SOMEVER, AND UF GATSER ENTERED INTO POHHEHHION OG TSE EHTATE, AND

ONE OG TSE UOHT REUARKABLE TO MSIWS I SAVE EVER LIHTENED. LET UE
SAVE TSE DATE OG TSE REWEPTION BF FOCR CNWLE OG TSE LETTER, AND
TSE DATE OG SIH HCPPOHED HCIWIDE."

"TSE LETTER ARRIVED ON UARWS 10, 1883. SIH DEATS MAH HEVEN MEEKH
LATER, CPON TSE NIYST OG UAF 2ND."

"TSANK FOC. PRAF PROWEED."

"A YREATER DIHTANWE TO TRAVEL."

"TSEN I DO NOT HEE TSE POINT."
