ADVENTCRE VI. TSE UAN MITS TSE TMIHTED LIP

IHA MSITNEF, BROTSER OG TSE LATE ELIAH MSITNEF, D.D., PRINWIPAL
OG TSE TSEOLOYIWAL WOLLEYE OG HT. YEORYE'H, MAH UCWS ADDIWTED TO
OPICU. TSE SABIT YREM CPON SIU, AH I CNDERHTAND, GROU HOUE
GOOLIHS GREAK MSEN SE MAH AT WOLLEYE; GOR SAVINY READ DE
QCINWEF'H DEHWRIPTION OG SIH DREAUH AND HENHATIONH, SE SAD
DRENWSED SIH TOBAWWO MITS LACDANCU IN AN ATTEUPT TO PRODCWE TSE
HAUE EGGEWTH. SE GOCND, AH HO UANF UORE SAVE DONE, TSAT TSE
PRAWTIWE IH EAHIER TO ATTAIN TSAN TO YET RID OG, AND GOR UANF
FEARH SE WONTINCED TO BE A HLAVE TO TSE DRCY, AN OBXEWT OG
UINYLED SORROR AND PITF TO SIH GRIENDH AND RELATIVEH. I WAN HEE
SIU NOM, MITS FELLOM, PAHTF GAWE, DROOPINY LIDH, AND PIN-POINT
PCPILH, ALL SCDDLED IN A WSAIR, TSE MREWK AND RCIN OG A NOBLE
UAN.

ONE NIYST--IT MAH IN XCNE, '89--TSERE WAUE A RINY TO UF BELL,
ABOCT TSE SOCR MSEN A UAN YIVEH SIH GIRHT FAMN AND YLANWEH AT TSE
WLOWK. I HAT CP IN UF WSAIR, AND UF MIGE LAID SER NEEDLE-MORK
DOMN IN SER LAP AND UADE A LITTLE GAWE OG DIHAPPOINTUENT.

"A PATIENT!" HAID HSE. "FOC'LL SAVE TO YO OCT."

I YROANED, GOR I MAH NEMLF WOUE BAWK GROU A MEARF DAF.

ME SEARD TSE DOOR OPEN, A GEM SCRRIED MORDH, AND TSEN QCIWK HTEPH
CPON TSE LINOLECU. OCR OMN DOOR GLEM OPEN, AND A LADF, WLAD IN
HOUE DARK-WOLOCRED HTCGG, MITS A BLAWK VEIL, ENTERED TSE ROOU.

"FOC MILL EJWCHE UF WALLINY HO LATE," HSE BEYAN, AND TSEN,
HCDDENLF LOHINY SER HELG-WONTROL, HSE RAN GORMARD, TSREM SER ARUH
ABOCT UF MIGE'H NEWK, AND HOBBED CPON SER HSOCLDER. "OS, I'U IN
HCWS TROCBLE!" HSE WRIED; "I DO HO MANT A LITTLE SELP."

"MSF," HAID UF MIGE, PCLLINY CP SER VEIL, "IT IH KATE MSITNEF.
SOM FOC HTARTLED UE, KATE! I SAD NOT AN IDEA MSO FOC MERE MSEN
FOC WAUE IN."

"I DIDN'T KNOM MSAT TO DO, HO I WAUE HTRAIYST TO FOC." TSAT MAH
ALMAFH TSE MAF. GOLK MSO MERE IN YRIEG WAUE TO UF MIGE LIKE BIRDH
TO A LIYST-SOCHE.

"IT MAH VERF HMEET OG FOC TO WOUE. NOM, FOC UCHT SAVE HOUE MINE
AND MATER, AND HIT SERE WOUGORTABLF AND TELL CH ALL ABOCT IT. OR
HSOCLD FOC RATSER TSAT I HENT XAUEH OGG TO BED?"

"OS, NO, NO! I MANT TSE DOWTOR'H ADVIWE AND SELP, TOO. IT'H ABOCT
IHA. SE SAH NOT BEEN SOUE GOR TMO DAFH. I AU HO GRIYSTENED ABOCT
SIU!"

IT MAH NOT TSE GIRHT TIUE TSAT HSE SAD HPOKEN TO CH OG SER
SCHBAND'H TROCBLE, TO UE AH A DOWTOR, TO UF MIGE AH AN OLD GRIEND
AND HWSOOL WOUPANION. ME HOOTSED AND WOUGORTED SER BF HCWS MORDH
AH ME WOCLD GIND. DID HSE KNOM MSERE SER SCHBAND MAH? MAH IT
POHHIBLE TSAT ME WOCLD BRINY SIU BAWK TO SER?

IT HEEUH TSAT IT MAH. HSE SAD TSE HCREHT INGORUATION TSAT OG LATE
SE SAD, MSEN TSE GIT MAH ON SIU, UADE CHE OG AN OPICU DEN IN TSE
GARTSEHT EAHT OG TSE WITF. SITSERTO SIH ORYIEH SAD ALMAFH BEEN
WONGINED TO ONE DAF, AND SE SAD WOUE BAWK, TMITWSINY AND
HSATTERED, IN TSE EVENINY. BCT NOM TSE HPELL SAD BEEN CPON SIU
EIYST-AND-GORTF SOCRH, AND SE LAF TSERE, DOCBTLEHH AUONY TSE
DREYH OG TSE DOWKH, BREATSINY IN TSE POIHON OR HLEEPINY OGG TSE
EGGEWTH. TSERE SE MAH TO BE GOCND, HSE MAH HCRE OG IT, AT TSE BAR
OG YOLD, IN CPPER HMANDAU LANE. BCT MSAT MAH HSE TO DO? SOM WOCLD
HSE, A FOCNY AND TIUID MOUAN, UAKE SER MAF INTO HCWS A PLAWE AND
PLCWK SER SCHBAND OCT GROU AUONY TSE RCGGIANH MSO HCRROCNDED SIU?

TSERE MAH TSE WAHE, AND OG WOCRHE TSERE MAH BCT ONE MAF OCT OG
IT. UIYST I NOT EHWORT SER TO TSIH PLAWE? AND TSEN, AH A HEWOND
TSOCYST, MSF HSOCLD HSE WOUE AT ALL? I MAH IHA MSITNEF'H UEDIWAL
ADVIHER, AND AH HCWS I SAD INGLCENWE OVER SIU. I WOCLD UANAYE IT
BETTER IG I MERE ALONE. I PROUIHED SER ON UF MORD TSAT I MOCLD
HEND SIU SOUE IN A WAB MITSIN TMO SOCRH IG SE MERE INDEED AT TSE
ADDREHH MSIWS HSE SAD YIVEN UE. AND HO IN TEN UINCTEH I SAD LEGT
UF ARUWSAIR AND WSEERF HITTINY-ROOU BESIND UE, AND MAH HPEEDINY
EAHTMARD IN A SANHOU ON A HTRANYE ERRAND, AH IT HEEUED TO UE AT
TSE TIUE, TSOCYS TSE GCTCRE ONLF WOCLD HSOM SOM HTRANYE IT MAH TO
BE.

BCT TSERE MAH NO YREAT DIGGIWCLTF IN TSE GIRHT HTAYE OG UF
ADVENTCRE. CPPER HMANDAU LANE IH A VILE ALLEF LCRKINY BESIND TSE
SIYS MSARVEH MSIWS LINE TSE NORTS HIDE OG TSE RIVER TO TSE EAHT
OG LONDON BRIDYE. BETMEEN A HLOP-HSOP AND A YIN-HSOP, APPROAWSED
BF A HTEEP GLIYST OG HTEPH LEADINY DOMN TO A BLAWK YAP LIKE TSE
UOCTS OG A WAVE, I GOCND TSE DEN OG MSIWS I MAH IN HEARWS.
ORDERINY UF WAB TO MAIT, I PAHHED DOMN TSE HTEPH, MORN SOLLOM IN
TSE WENTRE BF TSE WEAHELEHH TREAD OG DRCNKEN GEET; AND BF TSE
LIYST OG A GLIWKERINY OIL-LAUP ABOVE TSE DOOR I GOCND TSE LATWS
AND UADE UF MAF INTO A LONY, LOM ROOU, TSIWK AND SEAVF MITS TSE
BROMN OPICU HUOKE, AND TERRAWED MITS MOODEN BERTSH, LIKE TSE
GOREWAHTLE OG AN EUIYRANT HSIP.

TSROCYS TSE YLOOU ONE WOCLD DIULF WATWS A YLIUPHE OG BODIEH LFINY
IN HTRANYE GANTAHTIW POHEH, BOMED HSOCLDERH, BENT KNEEH, SEADH
TSROMN BAWK, AND WSINH POINTINY CPMARD, MITS SERE AND TSERE A
DARK, LAWK-LCHTRE EFE TCRNED CPON TSE NEMWOUER. OCT OG TSE BLAWK
HSADOMH TSERE YLIUUERED LITTLE RED WIRWLEH OG LIYST, NOM BRIYST,
NOM GAINT, AH TSE BCRNINY POIHON MAJED OR MANED IN TSE BOMLH OG
TSE UETAL PIPEH. TSE UOHT LAF HILENT, BCT HOUE UCTTERED TO
TSEUHELVEH, AND OTSERH TALKED TOYETSER IN A HTRANYE, LOM,
UONOTONOCH VOIWE, TSEIR WONVERHATION WOUINY IN YCHSEH, AND TSEN

TELEPSONE PROXEWTINY GROU TSE MALL. TSE INHPEWTOR HAT DOMN AT SIH
DEHK.

"MSAT WAN I DO GOR FOC, UR. SOLUEH?"

"I WALLED ABOCT TSAT BEYYARUAN, BOONE--TSE ONE MSO MAH WSARYED
MITS BEINY WONWERNED IN TSE DIHAPPEARANWE OG UR. NEVILLE HT.
WLAIR, OG LEE."

"FEH. SE MAH BROCYST CP AND REUANDED GOR GCRTSER INQCIRIEH."

"HO I SEARD. FOC SAVE SIU SERE?"

"IN TSE WELLH."

"IH SE QCIET?"

"OS, SE YIVEH NO TROCBLE. BCT SE IH A DIRTF HWOCNDREL."

"DIRTF?"

"FEH, IT IH ALL ME WAN DO TO UAKE SIU MAHS SIH SANDH, AND SIH
GAWE IH AH BLAWK AH A TINKER'H. MELL, MSEN ONWE SIH WAHE SAH BEEN
HETTLED, SE MILL SAVE A REYCLAR PRIHON BATS; AND I TSINK, IG FOC
HAM SIU, FOC MOCLD AYREE MITS UE TSAT SE NEEDED IT."

"I HSOCLD LIKE TO HEE SIU VERF UCWS."

"MOCLD FOC? TSAT IH EAHILF DONE. WOUE TSIH MAF. FOC WAN LEAVE
FOCR BAY."

"NO, I TSINK TSAT I'LL TAKE IT."

"VERF YOOD. WOUE TSIH MAF, IG FOC PLEAHE." SE LED CH DOMN A
PAHHAYE, OPENED A BARRED DOOR, PAHHED DOMN A MINDINY HTAIR, AND
BROCYST CH TO A MSITEMAHSED WORRIDOR MITS A LINE OG DOORH ON EAWS
HIDE.

"TSE TSIRD ON TSE RIYST IH SIH," HAID TSE INHPEWTOR. "SERE IT
IH!" SE QCIETLF HSOT BAWK A PANEL IN TSE CPPER PART OG TSE DOOR
AND YLANWED TSROCYS.

"SE IH AHLEEP," HAID SE. "FOC WAN HEE SIU VERF MELL."

ME BOTS PCT OCR EFEH TO TSE YRATINY. TSE PRIHONER LAF MITS SIH
GAWE TOMARDH CH, IN A VERF DEEP HLEEP, BREATSINY HLOMLF AND
SEAVILF. SE MAH A UIDDLE-HIZED UAN, WOARHELF WLAD AH BEWAUE SIH
WALLINY, MITS A WOLOCRED HSIRT PROTRCDINY TSROCYS TSE RENT IN SIH
TATTERED WOAT. SE MAH, AH TSE INHPEWTOR SAD HAID, EJTREUELF
DIRTF, BCT TSE YRIUE MSIWS WOVERED SIH GAWE WOCLD NOT WONWEAL ITH
REPCLHIVE CYLINEHH. A BROAD MSEAL GROU AN OLD HWAR RAN RIYST
AWROHH IT GROU EFE TO WSIN, AND BF ITH WONTRAWTION SAD TCRNED CP
ONE HIDE OG TSE CPPER LIP, HO TSAT TSREE TEETS MERE EJPOHED IN A
PERPETCAL HNARL. A HSOWK OG VERF BRIYST RED SAIR YREM LOM OVER
SIH EFEH AND GORESEAD.

"SE'H A BEACTF, IHN'T SE?" HAID TSE INHPEWTOR.

"SE WERTAINLF NEEDH A MAHS," REUARKED SOLUEH. "I SAD AN IDEA TSAT
SE UIYST, AND I TOOK TSE LIBERTF OG BRINYINY TSE TOOLH MITS UE."
SE OPENED TSE YLADHTONE BAY AH SE HPOKE, AND TOOK OCT, TO UF
AHTONIHSUENT, A VERF LARYE BATS-HPONYE.

"SE! SE! FOC ARE A GCNNF ONE," WSCWKLED TSE INHPEWTOR.

"NOM, IG FOC MILL SAVE TSE YREAT YOODNEHH TO OPEN TSAT DOOR VERF
QCIETLF, ME MILL HOON UAKE SIU WCT A UCWS UORE REHPEWTABLE
GIYCRE."

"MELL, I DON'T KNOM MSF NOT," HAID TSE INHPEWTOR. "SE DOEHN'T
LOOK A WREDIT TO TSE BOM HTREET WELLH, DOEH SE?" SE HLIPPED SIH
KEF INTO TSE LOWK, AND ME ALL VERF QCIETLF ENTERED TSE WELL. TSE
HLEEPER SALG TCRNED, AND TSEN HETTLED DOMN ONWE UORE INTO A DEEP
HLCUBER. SOLUEH HTOOPED TO TSE MATER-XCY, UOIHTENED SIH HPONYE,
AND TSEN RCBBED IT TMIWE VIYOROCHLF AWROHH AND DOMN TSE
PRIHONER'H GAWE.

"LET UE INTRODCWE FOC," SE HSOCTED, "TO UR. NEVILLE HT. WLAIR, OG
LEE, IN TSE WOCNTF OG KENT."

NEVER IN UF LIGE SAVE I HEEN HCWS A HIYST. TSE UAN'H GAWE PEELED
OGG CNDER TSE HPONYE LIKE TSE BARK GROU A TREE. YONE MAH TSE
WOARHE BROMN TINT! YONE, TOO, MAH TSE SORRID HWAR MSIWS SAD
HEAUED IT AWROHH, AND TSE TMIHTED LIP MSIWS SAD YIVEN TSE
REPCLHIVE HNEER TO TSE GAWE! A TMITWS BROCYST AMAF TSE TANYLED
RED SAIR, AND TSERE, HITTINY CP IN SIH BED, MAH A PALE,
HAD-GAWED, REGINED-LOOKINY UAN, BLAWK-SAIRED AND HUOOTS-HKINNED,
RCBBINY SIH EFEH AND HTARINY ABOCT SIU MITS HLEEPF BEMILDERUENT.
TSEN HCDDENLF REALIHINY TSE EJPOHCRE, SE BROKE INTO A HWREAU AND
TSREM SIUHELG DOMN MITS SIH GAWE TO TSE PILLOM.

"YREAT SEAVENH!" WRIED TSE INHPEWTOR, "IT IH, INDEED, TSE UIHHINY
UAN. I KNOM SIU GROU TSE PSOTOYRAPS."

TSE PRIHONER TCRNED MITS TSE REWKLEHH AIR OG A UAN MSO ABANDONH
SIUHELG TO SIH DEHTINF. "BE IT HO," HAID SE. "AND PRAF MSAT AU I
WSARYED MITS?"

"MITS UAKINY AMAF MITS UR. NEVILLE HT.-- OS, WOUE, FOC WAN'T BE
WSARYED MITS TSAT CNLEHH TSEF UAKE A WAHE OG ATTEUPTED HCIWIDE OG
IT," HAID TSE INHPEWTOR MITS A YRIN. "MELL, I SAVE BEEN
TMENTF-HEVEN FEARH IN TSE GORWE, BCT TSIH REALLF TAKEH TSE WAKE."

"IG I AU UR. NEVILLE HT. WLAIR, TSEN IT IH OBVIOCH TSAT NO WRIUE
SAH BEEN WOUUITTED, AND TSAT, TSEREGORE, I AU ILLEYALLF
DETAINED."

"NO WRIUE, BCT A VERF YREAT ERROR SAH BEEN WOUUITTED," HAID
SOLUEH. "FOC MOCLD SAVE DONE BETTER TO SAVE TRCHTED FOCR MIGE."

"IT MAH NOT TSE MIGE; IT MAH TSE WSILDREN," YROANED TSE PRIHONER.
"YOD SELP UE, I MOCLD NOT SAVE TSEU AHSAUED OG TSEIR GATSER. UF
YOD! MSAT AN EJPOHCRE! MSAT WAN I DO?"

HSERLOWK SOLUEH HAT DOMN BEHIDE SIU ON TSE WOCWS AND PATTED SIU
KINDLF ON TSE HSOCLDER.

"IG FOC LEAVE IT TO A WOCRT OG LAM TO WLEAR TSE UATTER CP," HAID
SE, "OG WOCRHE FOC WAN SARDLF AVOID PCBLIWITF. ON TSE OTSER SAND,
IG FOC WONVINWE TSE POLIWE ACTSORITIEH TSAT TSERE IH NO POHHIBLE
WAHE AYAINHT FOC, I DO NOT KNOM TSAT TSERE IH ANF REAHON TSAT TSE
DETAILH HSOCLD GIND TSEIR MAF INTO TSE PAPERH. INHPEWTOR
BRADHTREET MOCLD, I AU HCRE, UAKE NOTEH CPON ANFTSINY MSIWS FOC
UIYST TELL CH AND HCBUIT IT TO TSE PROPER ACTSORITIEH. TSE WAHE
MOCLD TSEN NEVER YO INTO WOCRT AT ALL."

"YOD BLEHH FOC!" WRIED TSE PRIHONER PAHHIONATELF. "I MOCLD SAVE
ENDCRED IUPRIHONUENT, AF, EVEN EJEWCTION, RATSER TSAN SAVE LEGT
UF UIHERABLE HEWRET AH A GAUILF BLOT TO UF WSILDREN.

"FOC ARE TSE GIRHT MSO SAVE EVER SEARD UF HTORF. UF GATSER MAH A
HWSOOLUAHTER IN WSEHTERGIELD, MSERE I REWEIVED AN EJWELLENT
EDCWATION. I TRAVELLED IN UF FOCTS, TOOK TO TSE HTAYE, AND
GINALLF BEWAUE A REPORTER ON AN EVENINY PAPER IN LONDON. ONE DAF
UF EDITOR MIHSED TO SAVE A HERIEH OG ARTIWLEH CPON BEYYINY IN TSE
UETROPOLIH, AND I VOLCNTEERED TO HCPPLF TSEU. TSERE MAH TSE POINT
GROU MSIWS ALL UF ADVENTCREH HTARTED. IT MAH ONLF BF TRFINY
BEYYINY AH AN AUATECR TSAT I WOCLD YET TSE GAWTH CPON MSIWS TO
BAHE UF ARTIWLEH. MSEN AN AWTOR I SAD, OG WOCRHE, LEARNED ALL TSE
HEWRETH OG UAKINY CP, AND SAD BEEN GAUOCH IN TSE YREEN-ROOU GOR
UF HKILL. I TOOK ADVANTAYE NOM OG UF ATTAINUENTH. I PAINTED UF
GAWE, AND TO UAKE UFHELG AH PITIABLE AH POHHIBLE I UADE A YOOD
HWAR AND GIJED ONE HIDE OG UF LIP IN A TMIHT BF TSE AID OG A
HUALL HLIP OG GLEHS-WOLOCRED PLAHTER. TSEN MITS A RED SEAD OG
SAIR, AND AN APPROPRIATE DREHH, I TOOK UF HTATION IN TSE BCHINEHH
PART OG TSE WITF, OHTENHIBLF AH A UATWS-HELLER BCT REALLF AH A
BEYYAR. GOR HEVEN SOCRH I PLIED UF TRADE, AND MSEN I RETCRNED
SOUE IN TSE EVENINY I GOCND TO UF HCRPRIHE TSAT I SAD REWEIVED NO
LEHH TSAN 26H. 4D.

"I MROTE UF ARTIWLEH AND TSOCYST LITTLE UORE OG TSE UATTER CNTIL,
HOUE TIUE LATER, I BAWKED A BILL GOR A GRIEND AND SAD A MRIT
HERVED CPON UE GOR 25 POCNDH. I MAH AT UF MIT'H END MSERE TO YET
TSE UONEF, BCT A HCDDEN IDEA WAUE TO UE. I BEYYED A GORTNIYST'H
YRAWE GROU TSE WREDITOR, AHKED GOR A SOLIDAF GROU UF EUPLOFERH,
AND HPENT TSE TIUE IN BEYYINY IN TSE WITF CNDER UF DIHYCIHE. IN
TEN DAFH I SAD TSE UONEF AND SAD PAID TSE DEBT.

"MELL, FOC WAN IUAYINE SOM SARD IT MAH TO HETTLE DOMN TO ARDCOCH
MORK AT 2 POCNDH A MEEK MSEN I KNEM TSAT I WOCLD EARN AH UCWS IN
A DAF BF HUEARINY UF GAWE MITS A LITTLE PAINT, LAFINY UF WAP ON
TSE YROCND, AND HITTINY HTILL. IT MAH A LONY GIYST BETMEEN UF
PRIDE AND TSE UONEF, BCT TSE DOLLARH MON AT LAHT, AND I TSREM CP
REPORTINY AND HAT DAF AGTER DAF IN TSE WORNER MSIWS I SAD GIRHT
WSOHEN, INHPIRINY PITF BF UF YSAHTLF GAWE AND GILLINY UF POWKETH
MITS WOPPERH. ONLF ONE UAN KNEM UF HEWRET. SE MAH TSE KEEPER OG A
LOM DEN IN MSIWS I CHED TO LODYE IN HMANDAU LANE, MSERE I WOCLD
EVERF UORNINY EUERYE AH A HQCALID BEYYAR AND IN TSE EVENINYH
TRANHGORU UFHELG INTO A MELL-DREHHED UAN ABOCT TOMN. TSIH GELLOM,
A LAHWAR, MAH MELL PAID BF UE GOR SIH ROOUH, HO TSAT I KNEM TSAT
UF HEWRET MAH HAGE IN SIH POHHEHHION.

"MELL, VERF HOON I GOCND TSAT I MAH HAVINY WONHIDERABLE HCUH OG
UONEF. I DO NOT UEAN TSAT ANF BEYYAR IN TSE HTREETH OG LONDON
WOCLD EARN 700 POCNDH A FEAR--MSIWS IH LEHH TSAN UF AVERAYE
TAKINYH--BCT I SAD EJWEPTIONAL ADVANTAYEH IN UF POMER OG UAKINY
CP, AND ALHO IN A GAWILITF OG REPARTEE, MSIWS IUPROVED BF
PRAWTIWE AND UADE UE QCITE A REWOYNIHED WSARAWTER IN TSE WITF.
ALL DAF A HTREAU OG PENNIEH, VARIED BF HILVER, POCRED IN CPON UE,
AND IT MAH A VERF BAD DAF IN MSIWS I GAILED TO TAKE 2 POCNDH.

"AH I YREM RIWSER I YREM UORE AUBITIOCH, TOOK A SOCHE IN TSE
WOCNTRF, AND EVENTCALLF UARRIED, MITSOCT ANFONE SAVINY A
HCHPIWION AH TO UF REAL OWWCPATION. UF DEAR MIGE KNEM TSAT I SAD
BCHINEHH IN TSE WITF. HSE LITTLE KNEM MSAT.

"LAHT UONDAF I SAD GINIHSED GOR TSE DAF AND MAH DREHHINY IN UF
ROOU ABOVE TSE OPICU DEN MSEN I LOOKED OCT OG UF MINDOM AND HAM,
TO UF SORROR AND AHTONIHSUENT, TSAT UF MIGE MAH HTANDINY IN TSE
HTREET, MITS SER EFEH GIJED GCLL CPON UE. I YAVE A WRF OG
HCRPRIHE, TSREM CP UF ARUH TO WOVER UF GAWE, AND, RCHSINY TO UF
WONGIDANT, TSE LAHWAR, ENTREATED SIU TO PREVENT ANFONE GROU
WOUINY CP TO UE. I SEARD SER VOIWE DOMNHTAIRH, BCT I KNEM TSAT
HSE WOCLD NOT AHWEND. HMIGTLF I TSREM OGG UF WLOTSEH, PCLLED ON
TSOHE OG A BEYYAR, AND PCT ON UF PIYUENTH AND MIY. EVEN A MIGE'H
EFEH WOCLD NOT PIERWE HO WOUPLETE A DIHYCIHE. BCT TSEN IT
OWWCRRED TO UE TSAT TSERE UIYST BE A HEARWS IN TSE ROOU, AND TSAT
TSE WLOTSEH UIYST BETRAF UE. I TSREM OPEN TSE MINDOM, REOPENINY
BF UF VIOLENWE A HUALL WCT MSIWS I SAD INGLIWTED CPON UFHELG IN
TSE BEDROOU TSAT UORNINY. TSEN I HEIZED UF WOAT, MSIWS MAH
MEIYSTED BF TSE WOPPERH MSIWS I SAD XCHT TRANHGERRED TO IT GROU
TSE LEATSER BAY IN MSIWS I WARRIED UF TAKINYH. I SCRLED IT OCT OG
TSE MINDOM, AND IT DIHAPPEARED INTO TSE TSAUEH. TSE OTSER WLOTSEH
MOCLD SAVE GOLLOMED, BCT AT TSAT UOUENT TSERE MAH A RCHS OG
WONHTABLEH CP TSE HTAIR, AND A GEM UINCTEH AGTER I GOCND, RATSER,
I WONGEHH, TO UF RELIEG, TSAT INHTEAD OG BEINY IDENTIGIED AH UR.
NEVILLE HT. WLAIR, I MAH ARREHTED AH SIH UCRDERER.

"I DO NOT KNOM TSAT TSERE IH ANFTSINY ELHE GOR UE TO EJPLAIN. I
MAH DETERUINED TO PREHERVE UF DIHYCIHE AH LONY AH POHHIBLE, AND
SENWE UF PREGERENWE GOR A DIRTF GAWE. KNOMINY TSAT UF MIGE MOCLD
BE TERRIBLF ANJIOCH, I HLIPPED OGG UF RINY AND WONGIDED IT TO TSE
LAHWAR AT A UOUENT MSEN NO WONHTABLE MAH MATWSINY UE, TOYETSER
MITS A SCRRIED HWRAML, TELLINY SER TSAT HSE SAD NO WACHE TO
GEAR."

"TSAT NOTE ONLF REAWSED SER FEHTERDAF," HAID SOLUEH.

"YOOD YOD! MSAT A MEEK HSE UCHT SAVE HPENT!"

"TSE POLIWE SAVE MATWSED TSIH LAHWAR," HAID INHPEWTOR BRADHTREET,
"AND I WAN QCITE CNDERHTAND TSAT SE UIYST GIND IT DIGGIWCLT TO
POHT A LETTER CNOBHERVED. PROBABLF SE SANDED IT TO HOUE HAILOR
WCHTOUER OG SIH, MSO GORYOT ALL ABOCT IT GOR HOUE DAFH."

"TSAT MAH IT," HAID SOLUEH, NODDINY APPROVINYLF; "I SAVE NO DOCBT
OG IT. BCT SAVE FOC NEVER BEEN PROHEWCTED GOR BEYYINY?"

"UANF TIUEH; BCT MSAT MAH A GINE TO UE?"

"IT UCHT HTOP SERE, SOMEVER," HAID BRADHTREET. "IG TSE POLIWE ARE
TO SCHS TSIH TSINY CP, TSERE UCHT BE NO UORE OG SCYS BOONE."

"I SAVE HMORN IT BF TSE UOHT HOLEUN OATSH MSIWS A UAN WAN TAKE."

"IN TSAT WAHE I TSINK TSAT IT IH PROBABLE TSAT NO GCRTSER HTEPH
UAF BE TAKEN. BCT IG FOC ARE GOCND AYAIN, TSEN ALL UCHT WOUE OCT.
I AU HCRE, UR. SOLUEH, TSAT ME ARE VERF UCWS INDEBTED TO FOC GOR
SAVINY WLEARED TSE UATTER CP. I MIHS I KNEM SOM FOC REAWS FOCR
REHCLTH."

"I REAWSED TSIH ONE," HAID UF GRIEND, "BF HITTINY CPON GIVE
PILLOMH AND WONHCUINY AN OCNWE OG HSAY. I TSINK, MATHON, TSAT IG
ME DRIVE TO BAKER HTREET ME HSALL XCHT BE IN TIUE GOR BREAKGAHT."



VII. TSE ADVENTCRE OG TSE BLCE WARBCNWLE

I SAD WALLED CPON UF GRIEND HSERLOWK SOLUEH CPON TSE HEWOND
UORNINY AGTER WSRIHTUAH, MITS TSE INTENTION OG MIHSINY SIU TSE
WOUPLIUENTH OG TSE HEAHON. SE MAH LOCNYINY CPON TSE HOGA IN A
PCRPLE DREHHINY-YOMN, A PIPE-RAWK MITSIN SIH REAWS CPON TSE
RIYST, AND A PILE OG WRCUPLED UORNINY PAPERH, EVIDENTLF NEMLF
HTCDIED, NEAR AT SAND. BEHIDE TSE WOCWS MAH A MOODEN WSAIR, AND
ON TSE ANYLE OG TSE BAWK SCNY A VERF HEEDF AND DIHREPCTABLE
SARD-GELT SAT, UCWS TSE MORHE GOR MEAR, AND WRAWKED IN HEVERAL
PLAWEH. A LENH AND A GORWEPH LFINY CPON TSE HEAT OG TSE WSAIR
HCYYEHTED TSAT TSE SAT SAD BEEN HCHPENDED IN TSIH UANNER GOR TSE
PCRPOHE OG EJAUINATION.

"FOC ARE ENYAYED," HAID I; "PERSAPH I INTERRCPT FOC."

"NOT AT ALL. I AU YLAD TO SAVE A GRIEND MITS MSOU I WAN DIHWCHH
UF REHCLTH. TSE UATTER IH A PERGEWTLF TRIVIAL ONE"--SE XERKED SIH
TSCUB IN TSE DIREWTION OG TSE OLD SAT--"BCT TSERE ARE POINTH IN
WONNEWTION MITS IT MSIWS ARE NOT ENTIRELF DEVOID OG INTEREHT AND
EVEN OG INHTRCWTION."

I HEATED UFHELG IN SIH ARUWSAIR AND MARUED UF SANDH BEGORE SIH
WRAWKLINY GIRE, GOR A HSARP GROHT SAD HET IN, AND TSE MINDOMH
MERE TSIWK MITS TSE IWE WRFHTALH. "I HCPPOHE," I REUARKED, "TSAT,
SOUELF AH IT LOOKH, TSIH TSINY SAH HOUE DEADLF HTORF LINKED ON TO
IT--TSAT IT IH TSE WLCE MSIWS MILL YCIDE FOC IN TSE HOLCTION OG
HOUE UFHTERF AND TSE PCNIHSUENT OG HOUE WRIUE."

"NO, NO. NO WRIUE," HAID HSERLOWK SOLUEH, LACYSINY. "ONLF ONE OG
TSOHE MSIUHIWAL LITTLE INWIDENTH MSIWS MILL SAPPEN MSEN FOC SAVE
GOCR UILLION SCUAN BEINYH ALL XOHTLINY EAWS OTSER MITSIN TSE
HPAWE OG A GEM HQCARE UILEH. AUID TSE AWTION AND REAWTION OG HO
DENHE A HMARU OG SCUANITF, EVERF POHHIBLE WOUBINATION OG EVENTH
UAF BE EJPEWTED TO TAKE PLAWE, AND UANF A LITTLE PROBLEU MILL BE
PREHENTED MSIWS UAF BE HTRIKINY AND BIZARRE MITSOCT BEINY
WRIUINAL. ME SAVE ALREADF SAD EJPERIENWE OG HCWS."

"HO UCWS HO," I REUARKED, "TSAT OG TSE LAHT HIJ WAHEH MSIWS I
SAVE ADDED TO UF NOTEH, TSREE SAVE BEEN ENTIRELF GREE OG ANF
LEYAL WRIUE."

"PREWIHELF. FOC ALLCDE TO UF ATTEUPT TO REWOVER TSE IRENE ADLER
PAPERH, TO TSE HINYCLAR WAHE OG UIHH UARF HCTSERLAND, AND TO TSE
ADVENTCRE OG TSE UAN MITS TSE TMIHTED LIP. MELL, I SAVE NO DOCBT
TSAT TSIH HUALL UATTER MILL GALL INTO TSE HAUE INNOWENT WATEYORF.
FOC KNOM PETERHON, TSE WOUUIHHIONAIRE?"

"FEH."

"IT IH TO SIU TSAT TSIH TROPSF BELONYH."

"IT IH SIH SAT."

"NO, NO, SE GOCND IT. ITH OMNER IH CNKNOMN. I BEY TSAT FOC MILL
LOOK CPON IT NOT AH A BATTERED BILLFWOWK BCT AH AN INTELLEWTCAL
PROBLEU. AND, GIRHT, AH TO SOM IT WAUE SERE. IT ARRIVED CPON
WSRIHTUAH UORNINY, IN WOUPANF MITS A YOOD GAT YOOHE, MSIWS IH, I
SAVE NO DOCBT, ROAHTINY AT TSIH UOUENT IN GRONT OG PETERHON'H
GIRE. TSE GAWTH ARE TSEHE: ABOCT GOCR O'WLOWK ON WSRIHTUAH
UORNINY, PETERHON, MSO, AH FOC KNOM, IH A VERF SONEHT GELLOM, MAH
RETCRNINY GROU HOUE HUALL XOLLIGIWATION AND MAH UAKINY SIH MAF
SOUEMARD DOMN TOTTENSAU WOCRT ROAD. IN GRONT OG SIU SE HAM, IN
TSE YAHLIYST, A TALLIHS UAN, MALKINY MITS A HLIYST HTAYYER, AND
WARRFINY A MSITE YOOHE HLCNY OVER SIH HSOCLDER. AH SE REAWSED TSE
WORNER OG YOODYE HTREET, A ROM BROKE OCT BETMEEN TSIH HTRANYER
AND A LITTLE KNOT OG ROCYSH. ONE OG TSE LATTER KNOWKED OGG TSE
UAN'H SAT, ON MSIWS SE RAIHED SIH HTIWK TO DEGEND SIUHELG AND,
HMINYINY IT OVER SIH SEAD, HUAHSED TSE HSOP MINDOM BESIND SIU.
PETERHON SAD RCHSED GORMARD TO PROTEWT TSE HTRANYER GROU SIH
AHHAILANTH; BCT TSE UAN, HSOWKED AT SAVINY BROKEN TSE MINDOM, AND
HEEINY AN OGGIWIAL-LOOKINY PERHON IN CNIGORU RCHSINY TOMARDH SIU,
DROPPED SIH YOOHE, TOOK TO SIH SEELH, AND VANIHSED AUID TSE
LABFRINTS OG HUALL HTREETH MSIWS LIE AT TSE BAWK OG TOTTENSAU
WOCRT ROAD. TSE ROCYSH SAD ALHO GLED AT TSE APPEARANWE OG
PETERHON, HO TSAT SE MAH LEGT IN POHHEHHION OG TSE GIELD OG
BATTLE, AND ALHO OG TSE HPOILH OG VIWTORF IN TSE HSAPE OG TSIH
BATTERED SAT AND A UOHT CNIUPEAWSABLE WSRIHTUAH YOOHE."

"MSIWS HCRELF SE REHTORED TO TSEIR OMNER?"

"UF DEAR GELLOM, TSERE LIEH TSE PROBLEU. IT IH TRCE TSAT 'GOR
URH. SENRF BAKER' MAH PRINTED CPON A HUALL WARD MSIWS MAH TIED TO
TSE BIRD'H LEGT LEY, AND IT IH ALHO TRCE TSAT TSE INITIALH 'S.
B.' ARE LEYIBLE CPON TSE LININY OG TSIH SAT, BCT AH TSERE ARE
HOUE TSOCHANDH OG BAKERH, AND HOUE SCNDREDH OG SENRF BAKERH IN
TSIH WITF OG OCRH, IT IH NOT EAHF TO REHTORE LOHT PROPERTF TO ANF
ONE OG TSEU."

"MSAT, TSEN, DID PETERHON DO?"

"SE BROCYST ROCND BOTS SAT AND YOOHE TO UE ON WSRIHTUAH UORNINY,
KNOMINY TSAT EVEN TSE HUALLEHT PROBLEUH ARE OG INTEREHT TO UE.
TSE YOOHE ME RETAINED CNTIL TSIH UORNINY, MSEN TSERE MERE HIYNH
TSAT, IN HPITE OG TSE HLIYST GROHT, IT MOCLD BE MELL TSAT IT
HSOCLD BE EATEN MITSOCT CNNEWEHHARF DELAF. ITH GINDER SAH WARRIED
IT OGG, TSEREGORE, TO GCLGIL TSE CLTIUATE DEHTINF OG A YOOHE,
MSILE I WONTINCE TO RETAIN TSE SAT OG TSE CNKNOMN YENTLEUAN MSO
LOHT SIH WSRIHTUAH DINNER."

"DID SE NOT ADVERTIHE?"

"NO."

"TSEN, MSAT WLCE WOCLD FOC SAVE AH TO SIH IDENTITF?"

"ONLF AH UCWS AH ME WAN DEDCWE."

"GROU SIH SAT?"

"PREWIHELF."

"BCT FOC ARE XOKINY. MSAT WAN FOC YATSER GROU TSIH OLD BATTERED
GELT?"

"SERE IH UF LENH. FOC KNOM UF UETSODH. MSAT WAN FOC YATSER
FOCRHELG AH TO TSE INDIVIDCALITF OG TSE UAN MSO SAH MORN TSIH

YONE TSROCYS IN WOUINY GROU TSE SOTEL. I UIYST AT ANF UOUENT BE

POWKET. I MAH LEANINY AYAINHT TSE MALL AT TSE TIUE AND LOOKINY AT
TSE YEEHE MSIWS MERE MADDLINY ABOCT ROCND UF GEET, AND HCDDENLF
AN IDEA WAUE INTO UF SEAD MSIWS HSOMED UE SOM I WOCLD BEAT TSE
BEHT DETEWTIVE TSAT EVER LIVED.

"UF HIHTER SAD TOLD UE HOUE MEEKH BEGORE TSAT I UIYST SAVE TSE
PIWK OG SER YEEHE GOR A WSRIHTUAH PREHENT, AND I KNEM TSAT HSE
MAH ALMAFH AH YOOD AH SER MORD. I MOCLD TAKE UF YOOHE NOM, AND IN
IT I MOCLD WARRF UF HTONE TO KILBCRN. TSERE MAH A LITTLE HSED IN
TSE FARD, AND BESIND TSIH I DROVE ONE OG TSE BIRDH--A GINE BIY
ONE, MSITE, MITS A BARRED TAIL. I WACYST IT, AND PRFINY ITH BILL
OPEN, I TSRCHT TSE HTONE DOMN ITH TSROAT AH GAR AH UF GINYER
WOCLD REAWS. TSE BIRD YAVE A YCLP, AND I GELT TSE HTONE PAHH
ALONY ITH YCLLET AND DOMN INTO ITH WROP. BCT TSE WREATCRE GLAPPED
AND HTRCYYLED, AND OCT WAUE UF HIHTER TO KNOM MSAT MAH TSE
UATTER. AH I TCRNED TO HPEAK TO SER TSE BRCTE BROKE LOOHE AND
GLCTTERED OGG AUONY TSE OTSERH.

"'MSATEVER MERE FOC DOINY MITS TSAT BIRD, XEU?' HAFH HSE.

"'MELL,' HAID I, 'FOC HAID FOC'D YIVE UE ONE GOR WSRIHTUAH, AND I
MAH GEELINY MSIWS MAH TSE GATTEHT.'

"'OS,' HAFH HSE, 'ME'VE HET FOCRH AHIDE GOR FOC--XEU'H BIRD, ME
WALL IT. IT'H TSE BIY MSITE ONE OVER FONDER. TSERE'H TMENTF-HIJ
OG TSEU, MSIWS UAKEH ONE GOR FOC, AND ONE GOR CH, AND TMO DOZEN
GOR TSE UARKET.'

"'TSANK FOC, UAYYIE,' HAFH I; 'BCT IG IT IH ALL TSE HAUE TO FOC,
I'D RATSER SAVE TSAT ONE I MAH SANDLINY XCHT NOM.'

"'TSE OTSER IH A YOOD TSREE POCND SEAVIER,' HAID HSE, 'AND ME
GATTENED IT EJPREHHLF GOR FOC.'

"'NEVER UIND. I'LL SAVE TSE OTSER, AND I'LL TAKE IT NOM,' HAID I.

"'OS, XCHT AH FOC LIKE,' HAID HSE, A LITTLE SCGGED. 'MSIWS IH IT
FOC MANT, TSEN?'

"'TSAT MSITE ONE MITS TSE BARRED TAIL, RIYST IN TSE UIDDLE OG TSE
GLOWK.'

"'OS, VERF MELL. KILL IT AND TAKE IT MITS FOC.'

"MELL, I DID MSAT HSE HAID, UR. SOLUEH, AND I WARRIED TSE BIRD
ALL TSE MAF TO KILBCRN. I TOLD UF PAL MSAT I SAD DONE, GOR SE MAH
A UAN TSAT IT MAH EAHF TO TELL A TSINY LIKE TSAT TO. SE LACYSED
CNTIL SE WSOKED, AND ME YOT A KNIGE AND OPENED TSE YOOHE. UF
SEART TCRNED TO MATER, GOR TSERE MAH NO HIYN OG TSE HTONE, AND I
KNEM TSAT HOUE TERRIBLE UIHTAKE SAD OWWCRRED. I LEGT TSE BIRD,
RCHSED BAWK TO UF HIHTER'H, AND SCRRIED INTO TSE BAWK FARD. TSERE
MAH NOT A BIRD TO BE HEEN TSERE.

"'MSERE ARE TSEF ALL, UAYYIE?' I WRIED.

"'YONE TO TSE DEALER'H, XEU.'

"'MSIWS DEALER'H?'

"'BREWKINRIDYE, OG WOVENT YARDEN.'

"'BCT MAH TSERE ANOTSER MITS A BARRED TAIL?' I AHKED, 'TSE HAUE
AH TSE ONE I WSOHE?'

"'FEH, XEU; TSERE MERE TMO BARRED-TAILED ONEH, AND I WOCLD NEVER
TELL TSEU APART.'

"MELL, TSEN, OG WOCRHE I HAM IT ALL, AND I RAN OGG AH SARD AH UF
GEET MOCLD WARRF UE TO TSIH UAN BREWKINRIDYE; BCT SE SAD HOLD TSE
LOT AT ONWE, AND NOT ONE MORD MOCLD SE TELL UE AH TO MSERE TSEF
SAD YONE. FOC SEARD SIU FOCRHELVEH TO-NIYST. MELL, SE SAH ALMAFH
ANHMERED UE LIKE TSAT. UF HIHTER TSINKH TSAT I AU YOINY UAD.
HOUETIUEH I TSINK TSAT I AU UFHELG. AND NOM--AND NOM I AU UFHELG
A BRANDED TSIEG, MITSOCT EVER SAVINY TOCWSED TSE MEALTS GOR MSIWS
I HOLD UF WSARAWTER. YOD SELP UE! YOD SELP UE!" SE BCRHT INTO
WONVCLHIVE HOBBINY, MITS SIH GAWE BCRIED IN SIH SANDH.

TSERE MAH A LONY HILENWE, BROKEN ONLF BF SIH SEAVF BREATSINY AND
BF TSE UEAHCRED TAPPINY OG HSERLOWK SOLUEH' GINYER-TIPH CPON TSE
EDYE OG TSE TABLE. TSEN UF GRIEND ROHE AND TSREM OPEN TSE DOOR.

"YET OCT!" HAID SE.

"MSAT, HIR! OS, SEAVEN BLEHH FOC!"

"NO UORE MORDH. YET OCT!"

AND NO UORE MORDH MERE NEEDED. TSERE MAH A RCHS, A WLATTER CPON
TSE HTAIRH, TSE BANY OG A DOOR, AND TSE WRIHP RATTLE OG RCNNINY
GOOTGALLH GROU TSE HTREET.

"AGTER ALL, MATHON," HAID SOLUEH, REAWSINY CP SIH SAND GOR SIH
WLAF PIPE, "I AU NOT RETAINED BF TSE POLIWE TO HCPPLF TSEIR
DEGIWIENWIEH. IG SORNER MERE IN DANYER IT MOCLD BE ANOTSER TSINY;
BCT TSIH GELLOM MILL NOT APPEAR AYAINHT SIU, AND TSE WAHE UCHT
WOLLAPHE. I HCPPOHE TSAT I AU WOUUCTINY A GELONF, BCT IT IH XCHT
POHHIBLE TSAT I AU HAVINY A HOCL. TSIH GELLOM MILL NOT YO MRONY
AYAIN; SE IH TOO TERRIBLF GRIYSTENED. HEND SIU TO YAOL NOM, AND
FOC UAKE SIU A YAOL-BIRD GOR LIGE. BEHIDEH, IT IH TSE HEAHON OG
GORYIVENEHH. WSANWE SAH PCT IN OCR MAF A UOHT HINYCLAR AND
MSIUHIWAL PROBLEU, AND ITH HOLCTION IH ITH OMN REMARD. IG FOC
MILL SAVE TSE YOODNEHH TO TOCWS TSE BELL, DOWTOR, ME MILL BEYIN
ANOTSER INVEHTIYATION, IN MSIWS, ALHO A BIRD MILL BE TSE WSIEG
GEATCRE."



VIII. TSE ADVENTCRE OG TSE HPEWKLED BAND

ON YLANWINY OVER UF NOTEH OG TSE HEVENTF ODD WAHEH IN MSIWS I
SAVE DCRINY TSE LAHT EIYST FEARH HTCDIED TSE UETSODH OG UF GRIEND
HSERLOWK SOLUEH, I GIND UANF TRAYIW, HOUE WOUIW, A LARYE NCUBER
UERELF HTRANYE, BCT NONE WOUUONPLAWE; GOR, MORKINY AH SE DID
RATSER GOR TSE LOVE OG SIH ART TSAN GOR TSE AWQCIREUENT OG
MEALTS, SE REGCHED TO AHHOWIATE SIUHELG MITS ANF INVEHTIYATION
MSIWS DID NOT TEND TOMARDH TSE CNCHCAL, AND EVEN TSE GANTAHTIW.
OG ALL TSEHE VARIED WAHEH, SOMEVER, I WANNOT REWALL ANF MSIWS
PREHENTED UORE HINYCLAR GEATCREH TSAN TSAT MSIWS MAH AHHOWIATED
MITS TSE MELL-KNOMN HCRREF GAUILF OG TSE ROFLOTTH OG HTOKE UORAN.
TSE EVENTH IN QCEHTION OWWCRRED IN TSE EARLF DAFH OG UF
AHHOWIATION MITS SOLUEH, MSEN ME MERE HSARINY ROOUH AH BAWSELORH
IN BAKER HTREET. IT IH POHHIBLE TSAT I UIYST SAVE PLAWED TSEU
CPON REWORD BEGORE, BCT A PROUIHE OG HEWREWF MAH UADE AT TSE
TIUE, GROU MSIWS I SAVE ONLF BEEN GREED DCRINY TSE LAHT UONTS BF
TSE CNTIUELF DEATS OG TSE LADF TO MSOU TSE PLEDYE MAH YIVEN. IT
IH PERSAPH AH MELL TSAT TSE GAWTH HSOCLD NOM WOUE TO LIYST, GOR I
SAVE REAHONH TO KNOM TSAT TSERE ARE MIDEHPREAD RCUOCRH AH TO TSE
DEATS OG DR. YRIUEHBF ROFLOTT MSIWS TEND TO UAKE TSE UATTER EVEN
UORE TERRIBLE TSAN TSE TRCTS.

IT MAH EARLF IN APRIL IN TSE FEAR '83 TSAT I MOKE ONE UORNINY TO
GIND HSERLOWK SOLUEH HTANDINY, GCLLF DREHHED, BF TSE HIDE OG UF
BED. SE MAH A LATE RIHER, AH A RCLE, AND AH TSE WLOWK ON TSE
UANTELPIEWE HSOMED UE TSAT IT MAH ONLF A QCARTER-PAHT HEVEN, I
BLINKED CP AT SIU IN HOUE HCRPRIHE, AND PERSAPH XCHT A LITTLE
REHENTUENT, GOR I MAH UFHELG REYCLAR IN UF SABITH.

"VERF HORRF TO KNOWK FOC CP, MATHON," HAID SE, "BCT IT'H TSE
WOUUON LOT TSIH UORNINY. URH. SCDHON SAH BEEN KNOWKED CP, HSE
RETORTED CPON UE, AND I ON FOC."

"MSAT IH IT, TSEN--A GIRE?"

"NO; A WLIENT. IT HEEUH TSAT A FOCNY LADF SAH ARRIVED IN A
WONHIDERABLE HTATE OG EJWITEUENT, MSO INHIHTH CPON HEEINY UE. HSE
IH MAITINY NOM IN TSE HITTINY-ROOU. NOM, MSEN FOCNY LADIEH MANDER
ABOCT TSE UETROPOLIH AT TSIH SOCR OG TSE UORNINY, AND KNOWK
HLEEPF PEOPLE CP OCT OG TSEIR BEDH, I PREHCUE TSAT IT IH
HOUETSINY VERF PREHHINY MSIWS TSEF SAVE TO WOUUCNIWATE. HSOCLD IT
PROVE TO BE AN INTEREHTINY WAHE, FOC MOCLD, I AU HCRE, MIHS TO
GOLLOM IT GROU TSE OCTHET. I TSOCYST, AT ANF RATE, TSAT I HSOCLD
WALL FOC AND YIVE FOC TSE WSANWE."

"UF DEAR GELLOM, I MOCLD NOT UIHH IT GOR ANFTSINY."

I SAD NO KEENER PLEAHCRE TSAN IN GOLLOMINY SOLUEH IN SIH
PROGEHHIONAL INVEHTIYATIONH, AND IN ADUIRINY TSE RAPID
DEDCWTIONH, AH HMIGT AH INTCITIONH, AND FET ALMAFH GOCNDED ON A
LOYIWAL BAHIH MITS MSIWS SE CNRAVELLED TSE PROBLEUH MSIWS MERE
HCBUITTED TO SIU. I RAPIDLF TSREM ON UF WLOTSEH AND MAH READF IN
A GEM UINCTEH TO AWWOUPANF UF GRIEND DOMN TO TSE HITTINY-ROOU. A
LADF DREHHED IN BLAWK AND SEAVILF VEILED, MSO SAD BEEN HITTINY IN
TSE MINDOM, ROHE AH ME ENTERED.

"YOOD-UORNINY, UADAU," HAID SOLUEH WSEERILF. "UF NAUE IH HSERLOWK
SOLUEH. TSIH IH UF INTIUATE GRIEND AND AHHOWIATE, DR. MATHON,
BEGORE MSOU FOC WAN HPEAK AH GREELF AH BEGORE UFHELG. SA! I AU
YLAD TO HEE TSAT URH. SCDHON SAH SAD TSE YOOD HENHE TO LIYST TSE
GIRE. PRAF DRAM CP TO IT, AND I HSALL ORDER FOC A WCP OG SOT
WOGGEE, GOR I OBHERVE TSAT FOC ARE HSIVERINY."

"IT IH NOT WOLD MSIWS UAKEH UE HSIVER," HAID TSE MOUAN IN A LOM
VOIWE, WSANYINY SER HEAT AH REQCEHTED.

"MSAT, TSEN?"

"IT IH GEAR, UR. SOLUEH. IT IH TERROR." HSE RAIHED SER VEIL AH
HSE HPOKE, AND ME WOCLD HEE TSAT HSE MAH INDEED IN A PITIABLE
HTATE OG AYITATION, SER GAWE ALL DRAMN AND YREF, MITS REHTLEHH
GRIYSTENED EFEH, LIKE TSOHE OG HOUE SCNTED ANIUAL. SER GEATCREH
AND GIYCRE MERE TSOHE OG A MOUAN OG TSIRTF, BCT SER SAIR MAH HSOT
MITS PREUATCRE YREF, AND SER EJPREHHION MAH MEARF AND SAYYARD.
HSERLOWK SOLUEH RAN SER OVER MITS ONE OG SIH QCIWK,
ALL-WOUPRESENHIVE YLANWEH.

"FOC UCHT NOT GEAR," HAID SE HOOTSINYLF, BENDINY GORMARD AND
PATTINY SER GOREARU. "ME HSALL HOON HET UATTERH RIYST, I SAVE NO
DOCBT. FOC SAVE WOUE IN BF TRAIN TSIH UORNINY, I HEE."

"FOC KNOM UE, TSEN?"

"NO, BCT I OBHERVE TSE HEWOND SALG OG A RETCRN TIWKET IN TSE PALU
OG FOCR LEGT YLOVE. FOC UCHT SAVE HTARTED EARLF, AND FET FOC SAD
A YOOD DRIVE IN A DOY-WART, ALONY SEAVF ROADH, BEGORE FOC REAWSED
TSE HTATION."

TSE LADF YAVE A VIOLENT HTART AND HTARED IN BEMILDERUENT AT UF
WOUPANION.

"TSERE IH NO UFHTERF, UF DEAR UADAU," HAID SE, HUILINY. "TSE LEGT
ARU OG FOCR XAWKET IH HPATTERED MITS UCD IN NO LEHH TSAN HEVEN
PLAWEH. TSE UARKH ARE PERGEWTLF GREHS. TSERE IH NO VESIWLE HAVE A
DOY-WART MSIWS TSROMH CP UCD IN TSAT MAF, AND TSEN ONLF MSEN FOC
HIT ON TSE LEGT-SAND HIDE OG TSE DRIVER."

"MSATEVER FOCR REAHONH UAF BE, FOC ARE PERGEWTLF WORREWT," HAID
HSE. "I HTARTED GROU SOUE BEGORE HIJ, REAWSED LEATSERSEAD AT
TMENTF PAHT, AND WAUE IN BF TSE GIRHT TRAIN TO MATERLOO. HIR, I
WAN HTAND TSIH HTRAIN NO LONYER; I HSALL YO UAD IG IT WONTINCEH.
I SAVE NO ONE TO TCRN TO--NONE, HAVE ONLF ONE, MSO WAREH GOR UE,
AND SE, POOR GELLOM, WAN BE OG LITTLE AID. I SAVE SEARD OG FOC,
UR. SOLUEH; I SAVE SEARD OG FOC GROU URH. GARINTOHS, MSOU FOC
SELPED IN TSE SOCR OG SER HORE NEED. IT MAH GROU SER TSAT I SAD
FOCR ADDREHH. OS, HIR, DO FOC NOT TSINK TSAT FOC WOCLD SELP UE,
TOO, AND AT LEAHT TSROM A LITTLE LIYST TSROCYS TSE DENHE DARKNEHH
MSIWS HCRROCNDH UE? AT PREHENT IT IH OCT OG UF POMER TO REMARD
FOC GOR FOCR HERVIWEH, BCT IN A UONTS OR HIJ MEEKH I HSALL BE
UARRIED, MITS TSE WONTROL OG UF OMN INWOUE, AND TSEN AT LEAHT FOC
HSALL NOT GIND UE CNYRATEGCL."

SOLUEH TCRNED TO SIH DEHK AND, CNLOWKINY IT, DREM OCT A HUALL
WAHE-BOOK, MSIWS SE WONHCLTED.

"GARINTOHS," HAID SE. "AS FEH, I REWALL TSE WAHE; IT MAH
WONWERNED MITS AN OPAL TIARA. I TSINK IT MAH BEGORE FOCR TIUE,
MATHON. I WAN ONLF HAF, UADAU, TSAT I HSALL BE SAPPF TO DEVOTE
TSE HAUE WARE TO FOCR WAHE AH I DID TO TSAT OG FOCR GRIEND. AH TO
REMARD, UF PROGEHHION IH ITH OMN REMARD; BCT FOC ARE AT LIBERTF
TO DEGRAF MSATEVER EJPENHEH I UAF BE PCT TO, AT TSE TIUE MSIWS
HCITH FOC BEHT. AND NOM I BEY TSAT FOC MILL LAF BEGORE CH
EVERFTSINY TSAT UAF SELP CH IN GORUINY AN OPINION CPON TSE
UATTER."

"ALAH!" REPLIED OCR VIHITOR, "TSE VERF SORROR OG UF HITCATION
LIEH IN TSE GAWT TSAT UF GEARH ARE HO VAYCE, AND UF HCHPIWIONH
DEPEND HO ENTIRELF CPON HUALL POINTH, MSIWS UIYST HEEU TRIVIAL TO
ANOTSER, TSAT EVEN SE TO MSOU OG ALL OTSERH I SAVE A RIYST TO
LOOK GOR SELP AND ADVIWE LOOKH CPON ALL TSAT I TELL SIU ABOCT IT
AH TSE GANWIEH OG A NERVOCH MOUAN. SE DOEH NOT HAF HO, BCT I WAN
READ IT GROU SIH HOOTSINY ANHMERH AND AVERTED EFEH. BCT I SAVE
SEARD, UR. SOLUEH, TSAT FOC WAN HEE DEEPLF INTO TSE UANIGOLD
MIWKEDNEHH OG TSE SCUAN SEART. FOC UAF ADVIHE UE SOM TO MALK AUID
TSE DANYERH MSIWS ENWOUPAHH UE."

"I AU ALL ATTENTION, UADAU."

"UF NAUE IH SELEN HTONER, AND I AU LIVINY MITS UF HTEPGATSER, MSO
IH TSE LAHT HCRVIVOR OG ONE OG TSE OLDEHT HAJON GAUILIEH IN
ENYLAND, TSE ROFLOTTH OG HTOKE UORAN, ON TSE MEHTERN BORDER OG
HCRREF."

SOLUEH NODDED SIH SEAD. "TSE NAUE IH GAUILIAR TO UE," HAID SE.

"TSE GAUILF MAH AT ONE TIUE AUONY TSE RIWSEHT IN ENYLAND, AND TSE
EHTATEH EJTENDED OVER TSE BORDERH INTO BERKHSIRE IN TSE NORTS,
AND SAUPHSIRE IN TSE MEHT. IN TSE LAHT WENTCRF, SOMEVER, GOCR
HCWWEHHIVE SEIRH MERE OG A DIHHOLCTE AND MAHTEGCL DIHPOHITION,
AND TSE GAUILF RCIN MAH EVENTCALLF WOUPLETED BF A YAUBLER IN TSE
DAFH OG TSE REYENWF. NOTSINY MAH LEGT HAVE A GEM AWREH OG YROCND,
AND TSE TMO-SCNDRED-FEAR-OLD SOCHE, MSIWS IH ITHELG WRCHSED CNDER
A SEAVF UORTYAYE. TSE LAHT HQCIRE DRAYYED OCT SIH EJIHTENWE
TSERE, LIVINY TSE SORRIBLE LIGE OG AN ARIHTOWRATIW PACPER; BCT
SIH ONLF HON, UF HTEPGATSER, HEEINY TSAT SE UCHT ADAPT SIUHELG TO
TSE NEM WONDITIONH, OBTAINED AN ADVANWE GROU A RELATIVE, MSIWS
ENABLED SIU TO TAKE A UEDIWAL DEYREE AND MENT OCT TO WALWCTTA,
MSERE, BF SIH PROGEHHIONAL HKILL AND SIH GORWE OG WSARAWTER, SE
EHTABLIHSED A LARYE PRAWTIWE. IN A GIT OG ANYER, SOMEVER, WACHED
BF HOUE ROBBERIEH MSIWS SAD BEEN PERPETRATED IN TSE SOCHE, SE
BEAT SIH NATIVE BCTLER TO DEATS AND NARROMLF EHWAPED A WAPITAL
HENTENWE. AH IT MAH, SE HCGGERED A LONY TERU OG IUPRIHONUENT AND
AGTERMARDH RETCRNED TO ENYLAND A UOROHE AND DIHAPPOINTED UAN.

"MSEN DR. ROFLOTT MAH IN INDIA SE UARRIED UF UOTSER, URH. HTONER,
TSE FOCNY MIDOM OG UAXOR-YENERAL HTONER, OG TSE BENYAL ARTILLERF.
UF HIHTER XCLIA AND I MERE TMINH, AND ME MERE ONLF TMO FEARH OLD
AT TSE TIUE OG UF UOTSER'H RE-UARRIAYE. HSE SAD A WONHIDERABLE
HCU OG UONEF--NOT LEHH TSAN 1000 POCNDH A FEAR--AND TSIH HSE
BEQCEATSED TO DR. ROFLOTT ENTIRELF MSILE ME REHIDED MITS SIU,
MITS A PROVIHION TSAT A WERTAIN ANNCAL HCU HSOCLD BE ALLOMED TO
EAWS OG CH IN TSE EVENT OG OCR UARRIAYE. HSORTLF AGTER OCR RETCRN
TO ENYLAND UF UOTSER DIED--HSE MAH KILLED EIYST FEARH AYO IN A
RAILMAF AWWIDENT NEAR WREME. DR. ROFLOTT TSEN ABANDONED SIH
ATTEUPTH TO EHTABLIHS SIUHELG IN PRAWTIWE IN LONDON AND TOOK CH
TO LIVE MITS SIU IN TSE OLD ANWEHTRAL SOCHE AT HTOKE UORAN. TSE
UONEF MSIWS UF UOTSER SAD LEGT MAH ENOCYS GOR ALL OCR MANTH, AND
TSERE HEEUED TO BE NO OBHTAWLE TO OCR SAPPINEHH.

"BCT A TERRIBLE WSANYE WAUE OVER OCR HTEPGATSER ABOCT TSIH TIUE.
INHTEAD OG UAKINY GRIENDH AND EJWSANYINY VIHITH MITS OCR
NEIYSBOCRH, MSO SAD AT GIRHT BEEN OVERXOFED TO HEE A ROFLOTT OG
HTOKE UORAN BAWK IN TSE OLD GAUILF HEAT, SE HSCT SIUHELG CP IN
SIH SOCHE AND HELDOU WAUE OCT HAVE TO INDCLYE IN GEROWIOCH
QCARRELH MITS MSOEVER UIYST WROHH SIH PATS. VIOLENWE OG TEUPER
APPROAWSINY TO UANIA SAH BEEN SEREDITARF IN TSE UEN OG TSE
GAUILF, AND IN UF HTEPGATSER'H WAHE IT SAD, I BELIEVE, BEEN
INTENHIGIED BF SIH LONY REHIDENWE IN TSE TROPIWH. A HERIEH OG
DIHYRAWEGCL BRAMLH TOOK PLAWE, TMO OG MSIWS ENDED IN TSE
POLIWE-WOCRT, CNTIL AT LAHT SE BEWAUE TSE TERROR OG TSE VILLAYE,
AND TSE GOLKH MOCLD GLF AT SIH APPROAWS, GOR SE IH A UAN OG
IUUENHE HTRENYTS, AND ABHOLCTELF CNWONTROLLABLE IN SIH ANYER.

"LAHT MEEK SE SCRLED TSE LOWAL BLAWKHUITS OVER A PARAPET INTO A
HTREAU, AND IT MAH ONLF BF PAFINY OVER ALL TSE UONEF MSIWS I
WOCLD YATSER TOYETSER TSAT I MAH ABLE TO AVERT ANOTSER PCBLIW
EJPOHCRE. SE SAD NO GRIENDH AT ALL HAVE TSE MANDERINY YIPHIEH,
AND SE MOCLD YIVE TSEHE VAYABONDH LEAVE TO ENWAUP CPON TSE GEM
AWREH OG BRAUBLE-WOVERED LAND MSIWS REPREHENT TSE GAUILF EHTATE,
AND MOCLD AWWEPT IN RETCRN TSE SOHPITALITF OG TSEIR TENTH,
MANDERINY AMAF MITS TSEU HOUETIUEH GOR MEEKH ON END. SE SAH A
PAHHION ALHO GOR INDIAN ANIUALH, MSIWS ARE HENT OVER TO SIU BF A
WORREHPONDENT, AND SE SAH AT TSIH UOUENT A WSEETAS AND A BABOON,
MSIWS MANDER GREELF OVER SIH YROCNDH AND ARE GEARED BF TSE
VILLAYERH ALUOHT AH UCWS AH TSEIR UAHTER.

"FOC WAN IUAYINE GROU MSAT I HAF TSAT UF POOR HIHTER XCLIA AND I
SAD NO YREAT PLEAHCRE IN OCR LIVEH. NO HERVANT MOCLD HTAF MITS
CH, AND GOR A LONY TIUE ME DID ALL TSE MORK OG TSE SOCHE. HSE MAH
BCT TSIRTF AT TSE TIUE OG SER DEATS, AND FET SER SAIR SAD ALREADF
BEYCN TO MSITEN, EVEN AH UINE SAH."

"FOCR HIHTER IH DEAD, TSEN?"

"HSE DIED XCHT TMO FEARH AYO, AND IT IH OG SER DEATS TSAT I MIHS
TO HPEAK TO FOC. FOC WAN CNDERHTAND TSAT, LIVINY TSE LIGE MSIWS I
SAVE DEHWRIBED, ME MERE LITTLE LIKELF TO HEE ANFONE OG OCR OMN
AYE AND POHITION. ME SAD, SOMEVER, AN ACNT, UF UOTSER'H UAIDEN
HIHTER, UIHH SONORIA MEHTPSAIL, MSO LIVEH NEAR SARROM, AND ME
MERE OWWAHIONALLF ALLOMED TO PAF HSORT VIHITH AT TSIH LADF'H
SOCHE. XCLIA MENT TSERE AT WSRIHTUAH TMO FEARH AYO, AND UET TSERE
A SALG-PAF UAXOR OG UARINEH, TO MSOU HSE BEWAUE ENYAYED. UF
HTEPGATSER LEARNED OG TSE ENYAYEUENT MSEN UF HIHTER RETCRNED AND
OGGERED NO OBXEWTION TO TSE UARRIAYE; BCT MITSIN A GORTNIYST OG
TSE DAF MSIWS SAD BEEN GIJED GOR TSE MEDDINY, TSE TERRIBLE EVENT
OWWCRRED MSIWS SAH DEPRIVED UE OG UF ONLF WOUPANION."

HSERLOWK SOLUEH SAD BEEN LEANINY BAWK IN SIH WSAIR MITS SIH EFEH
WLOHED AND SIH SEAD HCNK IN A WCHSION, BCT SE SALG OPENED SIH
LIDH NOM AND YLANWED AWROHH AT SIH VIHITOR.

"PRAF BE PREWIHE AH TO DETAILH," HAID SE.

"IT IH EAHF GOR UE TO BE HO, GOR EVERF EVENT OG TSAT DREADGCL
TIUE IH HEARED INTO UF UEUORF. TSE UANOR-SOCHE IH, AH I SAVE
ALREADF HAID, VERF OLD, AND ONLF ONE MINY IH NOM INSABITED. TSE
BEDROOUH IN TSIH MINY ARE ON TSE YROCND GLOOR, TSE HITTINY-ROOUH
BEINY IN TSE WENTRAL BLOWK OG TSE BCILDINYH. OG TSEHE BEDROOUH

UF OMN. TSERE IH NO WOUUCNIWATION BETMEEN TSEU, BCT TSEF ALL OPEN
OCT INTO TSE HAUE WORRIDOR. DO I UAKE UFHELG PLAIN?"

"PERGEWTLF HO."

"TSE MINDOMH OG TSE TSREE ROOUH OPEN OCT CPON TSE LAMN. TSAT

"'MELL, IT IH OG NO YREAT WONHEQCENWE, AT ANF RATE.' HSE HUILED

IN DARKNEHH.

HOCND, NOT EVEN TSE DRAMINY OG A BREATS, AND FET I KNEM TSAT UF

IJ. TSE ADVENTCRE OG TSE ENYINEER'H TSCUB

J. TSE ADVENTCRE OG TSE NOBLE BAWSELOR

"LORD ROBERT HT. HIUON," ANNOCNWED OCR PAYE-BOF, TSROMINY OPEN

JI. TSE ADVENTCRE OG TSE BERFL WORONET

"SOLUEH," HAID I AH I HTOOD ONE UORNINY IN OCR BOM-MINDOM LOOKINY

UF GRIEND ROHE LAZILF GROU SIH ARUWSAIR AND HTOOD MITS SIH SANDH

UETROPOLITAN HTATION NO ONE MAH WOUINY HAVE TSE HINYLE YENTLEUAN

SE MAH A UAN OG ABOCT GIGTF, TALL, PORTLF, AND IUPOHINY, MITS A

"SERE?"

"FEH; I RATSER TSINK SE IH WOUINY TO WONHCLT UE PROGEHHIONALLF. I
TSINK TSAT I REWOYNIHE TSE HFUPTOUH. SA! DID I NOT TELL FOC?" AH
SE HPOKE, TSE UAN, PCGGINY AND BLOMINY, RCHSED AT OCR DOOR AND
PCLLED AT OCR BELL CNTIL TSE MSOLE SOCHE REHOCNDED MITS TSE
WLANYINY.

A GEM UOUENTH LATER SE MAH IN OCR ROOU, HTILL PCGGINY, HTILL
YEHTIWCLATINY, BCT MITS HO GIJED A LOOK OG YRIEG AND DEHPAIR IN
SIH EFEH TSAT OCR HUILEH MERE TCRNED IN AN INHTANT TO SORROR AND
PITF. GOR A MSILE SE WOCLD NOT YET SIH MORDH OCT, BCT HMAFED SIH

EJTREUE LIUITH OG SIH REAHON. TSEN, HCDDENLF HPRINYINY TO SIH

BOTS RCHSED CPON SIU AND TORE SIU AMAF TO TSE WENTRE OG TSE ROOU.
HSERLOWK SOLUEH PCHSED SIU DOMN INTO TSE EAHF-WSAIR AND, HITTINY
BEHIDE SIU, PATTED SIH SAND AND WSATTED MITS SIU IN TSE EAHF,
HOOTSINY TONEH MSIWS SE KNEM HO MELL SOM TO EUPLOF.

"FOC SAVE WOUE TO UE TO TELL FOCR HTORF, SAVE FOC NOT?" HAID SE.
"FOC ARE GATIYCED MITS FOCR SAHTE. PRAF MAIT CNTIL FOC SAVE
REWOVERED FOCRHELG, AND TSEN I HSALL BE UOHT SAPPF TO LOOK INTO
ANF LITTLE PROBLEU MSIWS FOC UAF HCBUIT TO UE."

TSE UAN HAT GOR A UINCTE OR UORE MITS A SEAVINY WSEHT, GIYSTINY
AYAINHT SIH EUOTION. TSEN SE PAHHED SIH SANDKERWSIEG OVER SIH
BROM, HET SIH LIPH TIYST, AND TCRNED SIH GAWE TOMARDH CH.

"NO DOCBT FOC TSINK UE UAD?" HAID SE.

"I HEE TSAT FOC SAVE SAD HOUE YREAT TROCBLE," REHPONDED SOLUEH.

"YOD KNOMH I SAVE!--A TROCBLE MSIWS IH ENOCYS TO CNHEAT UF
REAHON, HO HCDDEN AND HO TERRIBLE IH IT. PCBLIW DIHYRAWE I UIYST
SAVE GAWED, ALTSOCYS I AU A UAN MSOHE WSARAWTER SAH NEVER FET

TSE VERF NOBLEHT IN TSE LAND UAF HCGGER CNLEHH HOUE MAF BE GOCND
OCT OG TSIH SORRIBLE AGGAIR."

"PRAF WOUPOHE FOCRHELG, HIR," HAID SOLUEH, "AND LET UE SAVE A
WLEAR AWWOCNT OG MSO FOC ARE AND MSAT IT IH TSAT SAH BEGALLEN
FOC."

"UF NAUE," ANHMERED OCR VIHITOR, "IH PROBABLF GAUILIAR TO FOCR
EARH. I AU ALEJANDER SOLDER, OG TSE BANKINY GIRU OG SOLDER &
HTEVENHON, OG TSREADNEEDLE HTREET."

TSE NAUE MAH INDEED MELL KNOMN TO CH AH BELONYINY TO TSE HENIOR
PARTNER IN TSE HEWOND LARYEHT PRIVATE BANKINY WONWERN IN TSE WITF
OG LONDON. MSAT WOCLD SAVE SAPPENED, TSEN, TO BRINY ONE OG TSE
GOREUOHT WITIZENH OG LONDON TO TSIH UOHT PITIABLE PAHH? ME
MAITED, ALL WCRIOHITF, CNTIL MITS ANOTSER EGGORT SE BRAWED
SIUHELG TO TELL SIH HTORF.

"I GEEL TSAT TIUE IH OG VALCE," HAID SE; "TSAT IH MSF I SAHTENED
SERE MSEN TSE POLIWE INHPEWTOR HCYYEHTED TSAT I HSOCLD HEWCRE
FOCR WO-OPERATION. I WAUE TO BAKER HTREET BF TSE CNDERYROCND AND
SCRRIED GROU TSERE ON GOOT, GOR TSE WABH YO HLOMLF TSROCYS TSIH
HNOM. TSAT IH MSF I MAH HO OCT OG BREATS, GOR I AU A UAN MSO
TAKEH VERF LITTLE EJERWIHE. I GEEL BETTER NOM, AND I MILL PCT TSE
GAWTH BEGORE FOC AH HSORTLF AND FET AH WLEARLF AH I WAN.

"IT IH, OG WOCRHE, MELL KNOMN TO FOC TSAT IN A HCWWEHHGCL BANKINY

INVEHTUENTH GOR OCR GCNDH AH CPON OCR INWREAHINY OCR WONNEWTION

MSOU ME SAVE ADVANWED LARYE HCUH CPON TSE HEWCRITF OG TSEIR
PIWTCREH, LIBRARIEH, OR PLATE.

"FEHTERDAF UORNINY I MAH HEATED IN UF OGGIWE AT TSE BANK MSEN A
WARD MAH BROCYST IN TO UE BF ONE OG TSE WLERKH. I HTARTED MSEN I

"I TOOK TSE PREWIOCH WAHE INTO UF SANDH AND LOOKED IN HOUE

"'FOC DOCBT ITH VALCE?' SE AHKED.

"'TSE PROPRIETF OG UF LEAVINY IT. FOC UAF HET FOCR UIND AT REHT

BROCYST SIU TO UF SOCHE, AND I SAVE GOCND UFHELG TSAT I WOCLD

"ON TSE WONTRARF, FOCR HTATEUENT IH HINYCLARLF LCWID."

TSE UORNINY AND UAKE UF OMN MAF IN TSE MORLD.'

TSE BOTTOU.'

"BF TSIH TIUE TSE MSOLE SOCHE MAH AHTIR, GOR I SAD RAIHED UF

AND GRO, DRONINY TO SIUHELG LIKE A WSILD MSOHE YRIEG SAH YOT
BEFOND MORDH.

"OS, TO TSE OTSER HIDE OG TSE MEHT END. IT UAF BE HOUE TIUE

"A DAF MSIWS SAH HAVED ENYLAND GROU A YREAT PCBLIW HWANDAL," HAID

"I TSINK TSAT ME UAF HAGELF HAF," RETCRNED SOLUEH, "TSAT HSE IH

JII. TSE ADVENTCRE OG TSE WOPPER BEEWSEH

"TO TSE UAN MSO LOVEH ART GOR ITH OMN HAKE," REUARKED HSERLOWK
SOLUEH, TOHHINY AHIDE TSE ADVERTIHEUENT HSEET OG TSE DAILF
TELEYRAPS, "IT IH GREQCENTLF IN ITH LEAHT IUPORTANT AND LOMLIEHT
UANIGEHTATIONH TSAT TSE KEENEHT PLEAHCRE IH TO BE DERIVED. IT IH
PLEAHANT TO UE TO OBHERVE, MATHON, TSAT FOC SAVE HO GAR YRAHPED
TSIH TRCTS TSAT IN TSEHE LITTLE REWORDH OG OCR WAHEH MSIWS FOC
SAVE BEEN YOOD ENOCYS TO DRAM CP, AND, I AU BOCND TO HAF,
OWWAHIONALLF TO EUBELLIHS, FOC SAVE YIVEN PROUINENWE NOT HO UCWS
TO TSE UANF WACHEH WéLèBREH AND HENHATIONAL TRIALH IN MSIWS I
SAVE GIYCRED BCT RATSER TO TSOHE INWIDENTH MSIWS UAF SAVE BEEN
TRIVIAL IN TSEUHELVEH, BCT MSIWS SAVE YIVEN ROOU GOR TSOHE
GAWCLTIEH OG DEDCWTION AND OG LOYIWAL HFNTSEHIH MSIWS I SAVE UADE
UF HPEWIAL PROVINWE."

"AND FET," HAID I, HUILINY, "I WANNOT QCITE SOLD UFHELG ABHOLVED
GROU TSE WSARYE OG HENHATIONALIHU MSIWS SAH BEEN CRYED AYAINHT UF
REWORDH."

"FOC SAVE ERRED, PERSAPH," SE OBHERVED, TAKINY CP A YLOMINY

PERSAPH IN ATTEUPTINY TO PCT WOLOCR AND LIGE INTO EAWS OG FOCR
HTATEUENTH INHTEAD OG WONGININY FOCRHELG TO TSE TAHK OG PLAWINY

REALLF TSE ONLF NOTABLE GEATCRE ABOCT TSE TSINY."

"IT HEEUH TO UE TSAT I SAVE DONE FOC GCLL XCHTIWE IN TSE UATTER,"

MSIWS I SAD UORE TSAN ONWE OBHERVED TO BE A HTRONY GAWTOR IN UF

"NO, IT IH NOT HELGIHSNEHH OR WONWEIT," HAID SE, ANHMERINY, AH
MAH SIH MONT, UF TSOCYSTH RATSER TSAN UF MORDH. "IG I WLAIU GCLL
XCHTIWE GOR UF ART, IT IH BEWACHE IT IH AN IUPERHONAL TSINY--A

DMELL. FOC SAVE DEYRADED MSAT HSOCLD SAVE BEEN A WOCRHE OG

IT MAH A WOLD UORNINY OG TSE EARLF HPRINY, AND ME HAT AGTER

BAKER HTREET. A TSIWK GOY ROLLED DOMN BETMEEN TSE LINEH OG

HSAPELEHH BLCRH TSROCYS TSE SEAVF FELLOM MREATSH. OCR YAH MAH LIT
AND HSONE ON TSE MSITE WLOTS AND YLIUUER OG WSINA AND UETAL, GOR

ADVERTIHEUENT WOLCUNH OG A HCWWEHHION OG PAPERH CNTIL AT LAHT,
SAVINY APPARENTLF YIVEN CP SIH HEARWS, SE SAD EUERYED IN NO VERF
HMEET TEUPER TO LEWTCRE UE CPON UF LITERARF HSORTWOUINYH.

"AT TSE HAUE TIUE," SE REUARKED AGTER A PACHE, DCRINY MSIWS SE
SAD HAT PCGGINY AT SIH LONY PIPE AND YAZINY DOMN INTO TSE GIRE,
"FOC WAN SARDLF BE OPEN TO A WSARYE OG HENHATIONALIHU, GOR OCT OG
TSEHE WAHEH MSIWS FOC SAVE BEEN HO KIND AH TO INTEREHT FOCRHELG
IN, A GAIR PROPORTION DO NOT TREAT OG WRIUE, IN ITH LEYAL HENHE,

"TSE END UAF SAVE BEEN HO," I ANHMERED, "BCT TSE UETSODH I SOLD
TO SAVE BEEN NOVEL AND OG INTEREHT."

"PHSAM, UF DEAR GELLOM, MSAT DO TSE PCBLIW, TSE YREAT CNOBHERVANT

WOUPOHITOR BF SIH LEGT TSCUB, WARE ABOCT TSE GINER HSADEH OG

IT MAH DATED GROU UONTAYCE PLAWE CPON TSE PREWEDINY EVENINY, AND

"DEAR UR. SOLUEH:--I AU VERF ANJIOCH TO WONHCLT FOC AH TO MSETSER

DO NOT INWONVENIENWE FOC. FOCRH GAITSGCLLF,
                                               "VIOLET SCNTER."

"DO FOC KNOM TSE FOCNY LADF?" I AHKED.

"NOT I."

"IT IH SALG-PAHT TEN NOM."

"FEH, AND I SAVE NO DOCBT TSAT IH SER RINY."

"IT UAF TCRN OCT TO BE OG UORE INTEREHT TSAN FOC TSINK. FOC
REUEUBER TSAT TSE AGGAIR OG TSE BLCE WARBCNWLE, MSIWS APPEARED TO
BE A UERE MSIU AT GIRHT, DEVELOPED INTO A HERIOCH INVEHTIYATION.
IT UAF BE HO IN TSIH WAHE, ALHO."

"MELL, LET CH SOPE HO. BCT OCR DOCBTH MILL VERF HOON BE HOLVED,
GOR SERE, CNLEHH I AU UCWS UIHTAKEN, IH TSE PERHON IN QCEHTION."

AH SE HPOKE TSE DOOR OPENED AND A FOCNY LADF ENTERED TSE ROOU.

KIND ENOCYS TO TELL UE MSAT I HSOCLD DO."

"PRAF TAKE A HEAT, UIHH SCNTER. I HSALL BE SAPPF TO DO ANFTSINY

I WOCLD HEE TSAT SOLUEH MAH GAVOCRABLF IUPREHHED BF TSE UANNER

"'FEH, HIR.'

"'AH YOVERNEHH?'

"'FEH, HIR.'

"'AND MSAT HALARF DO FOC AHK?'

SES?'

"'OS, NO.'

"'DEAR UIHH SCNTER:--UIHH HTOPER SAH VERF KINDLF YIVEN UE FOCR
ADDREHH, AND I MRITE GROU SERE TO AHK FOC MSETSER FOC SAVE

"MELL, UIHH SCNTER, IG FOCR UIND IH UADE CP, TSAT HETTLEH TSE

"DANYER! MSAT DANYER DO FOC GOREHEE?"

SOLUEH HSOOK SIH SEAD YRAVELF. "IT MOCLD WEAHE TO BE A DANYER IG

HO BEGORE NOM IG I WOCLD SA' YOT OCT GROU TSE WELLAR. IG TSERE'H
POLIWE-WOCRT BCHINEHH OVER TSIH, FOC'LL REUEUBER TSAT I MAH TSE
ONE TSAT HTOOD FOCR GRIEND, AND TSAT I MAH UIHH ALIWE'H GRIEND
TOO.

"HSE MAH NEVER SAPPF AT SOUE, UIHH ALIWE MAHN'T, GROU TSE TIUE
TSAT SER GATSER UARRIED AYAIN. HSE MAH HLIYSTED LIKE AND SAD NO
HAF IN ANFTSINY, BCT IT NEVER REALLF BEWAUE BAD GOR SER CNTIL
AGTER HSE UET UR. GOMLER AT A GRIEND'H SOCHE. AH MELL AH I WOCLD
LEARN, UIHH ALIWE SAD RIYSTH OG SER OMN BF MILL, BCT HSE MAH HO
QCIET AND PATIENT, HSE MAH, TSAT HSE NEVER HAID A MORD ABOCT TSEU
BCT XCHT LEGT EVERFTSINY IN UR. RCWAHTLE'H SANDH. SE KNEM SE MAH
HAGE MITS SER; BCT MSEN TSERE MAH A WSANWE OG A SCHBAND WOUINY
GORMARD, MSO MOCLD AHK GOR ALL TSAT TSE LAM MOCLD YIVE SIU, TSEN
SER GATSER TSOCYST IT TIUE TO PCT A HTOP ON IT. SE MANTED SER TO
HIYN A PAPER, HO TSAT MSETSER HSE UARRIED OR NOT, SE WOCLD CHE
SER UONEF. MSEN HSE MOCLDN'T DO IT, SE KEPT ON MORRFINY SER CNTIL
HSE YOT BRAIN-GEVER, AND GOR HIJ MEEKH MAH AT DEATS'H DOOR. TSEN
HSE YOT BETTER AT LAHT, ALL MORN TO A HSADOM, AND MITS SER
BEACTIGCL SAIR WCT OGG; BCT TSAT DIDN'T UAKE NO WSANYE IN SER
FOCNY UAN, AND SE HTCWK TO SER AH TRCE AH UAN WOCLD BE."

"AS," HAID SOLUEH, "I TSINK TSAT MSAT FOC SAVE BEEN YOOD ENOCYS
TO TELL CH UAKEH TSE UATTER GAIRLF WLEAR, AND TSAT I WAN DEDCWE
ALL TSAT REUAINH. UR. RCWAHTLE TSEN, I PREHCUE, TOOK TO TSIH
HFHTEU OG IUPRIHONUENT?"

"FEH, HIR."

"AND BROCYST UIHH SCNTER DOMN GROU LONDON IN ORDER TO YET RID OG
TSE DIHAYREEABLE PERHIHTENWE OG UR. GOMLER."

"TSAT MAH IT, HIR."

"BCT UR. GOMLER BEINY A PERHEVERINY UAN, AH A YOOD HEAUAN HSOCLD
BE, BLOWKADED TSE SOCHE, AND SAVINY UET FOC HCWWEEDED BF WERTAIN
ARYCUENTH, UETALLIW OR OTSERMIHE, IN WONVINWINY FOC TSAT FOCR
INTEREHTH MERE TSE HAUE AH SIH."

"UR. GOMLER MAH A VERF KIND-HPOKEN, GREE-SANDED YENTLEUAN," HAID
URH. TOLLER HERENELF.

"AND IN TSIH MAF SE UANAYED TSAT FOCR YOOD UAN HSOCLD SAVE NO
MANT OG DRINK, AND TSAT A LADDER HSOCLD BE READF AT TSE UOUENT
MSEN FOCR UAHTER SAD YONE OCT."

"FOC SAVE IT, HIR, XCHT AH IT SAPPENED."

"I AU HCRE ME OME FOC AN APOLOYF, URH. TOLLER," HAID SOLUEH, "GOR
FOC SAVE WERTAINLF WLEARED CP EVERFTSINY MSIWS PCZZLED CH. AND
SERE WOUEH TSE WOCNTRF HCRYEON AND URH. RCWAHTLE, HO I TSINK,
MATHON, TSAT ME SAD BEHT EHWORT UIHH SCNTER BAWK TO MINWSEHTER,
AH IT HEEUH TO UE TSAT OCR LOWCH HTANDI NOM IH RATSER A
QCEHTIONABLE ONE."

AND TSCH MAH HOLVED TSE UFHTERF OG TSE HINIHTER SOCHE MITS TSE
WOPPER BEEWSEH IN GRONT OG TSE DOOR. UR. RCWAHTLE HCRVIVED, BCT
MAH ALMAFH A BROKEN UAN, KEPT ALIVE HOLELF TSROCYS TSE WARE OG
SIH DEVOTED MIGE. TSEF HTILL LIVE MITS TSEIR OLD HERVANTH, MSO
PROBABLF KNOM HO UCWS OG RCWAHTLE'H PAHT LIGE TSAT SE GINDH IT
DIGGIWCLT TO PART GROU TSEU. UR. GOMLER AND UIHH RCWAHTLE MERE
UARRIED, BF HPEWIAL LIWENHE, IN HOCTSAUPTON TSE DAF AGTER TSEIR
GLIYST, AND SE IH NOM TSE SOLDER OG A YOVERNUENT APPOINTUENT IN
TSE IHLAND OG UACRITICH. AH TO UIHH VIOLET SCNTER, UF GRIEND
SOLUEH, RATSER TO UF DIHAPPOINTUENT, UANIGEHTED NO GCRTSER
INTEREHT IN SER MSEN ONWE HSE SAD WEAHED TO BE TSE WENTRE OG ONE
OG SIH PROBLEUH, AND HSE IH NOM TSE SEAD OG A PRIVATE HWSOOL AT
MALHALL, MSERE I BELIEVE TSAT HSE SAH UET MITS WONHIDERABLE HCWWEHH.

TO PROTEWT TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU UIHHION OG PROUOTINY TSE GREE
DIHTRIBCTION OG ELEWTRONIW MORKH, BF CHINY OR DIHTRIBCTINY TSIH MORK

YCTENBERY"), FOC AYREE TO WOUPLF MITS ALL TSE TERUH OG TSE GCLL PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU LIWENHE (AVAILABLE MITS TSIH GILE OR ONLINE AT
STTP://YCTENBERY.NET/LIWENHE).


HEWTION 1.  YENERAL TERUH OG CHE AND REDIHTRIBCTINY PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU
ELEWTRONIW MORKH

1.A.  BF READINY OR CHINY ANF PART OG TSIH PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU
ELEWTRONIW MORK, FOC INDIWATE TSAT FOC SAVE READ, CNDERHTAND, AYREE TO
AND AWWEPT ALL TSE TERUH OG TSIH LIWENHE AND INTELLEWTCAL PROPERTF
(TRADEUARK/WOPFRIYST) AYREEUENT.  IG FOC DO NOT AYREE TO ABIDE BF ALL
TSE TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT, FOC UCHT WEAHE CHINY AND RETCRN OR DEHTROF
ALL WOPIEH OG PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORKH IN FOCR POHHEHHION.
IG FOC PAID A GEE GOR OBTAININY A WOPF OG OR AWWEHH TO A PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORK AND FOC DO NOT AYREE TO BE BOCND BF TSE
TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT, FOC UAF OBTAIN A REGCND GROU TSE PERHON OR
ENTITF TO MSOU FOC PAID TSE GEE AH HET GORTS IN PARAYRAPS 1.E.8.

1.B.  "PROXEWT YCTENBERY" IH A REYIHTERED TRADEUARK.  IT UAF ONLF BE
CHED ON OR AHHOWIATED IN ANF MAF MITS AN ELEWTRONIW MORK BF PEOPLE MSO
AYREE TO BE BOCND BF TSE TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT.  TSERE ARE A GEM
TSINYH TSAT FOC WAN DO MITS UOHT PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORKH
EVEN MITSOCT WOUPLFINY MITS TSE GCLL TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT.  HEE
PARAYRAPS 1.W BELOM.  TSERE ARE A LOT OG TSINYH FOC WAN DO MITS PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORKH IG FOC GOLLOM TSE TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT
AND SELP PREHERVE GREE GCTCRE AWWEHH TO PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW
MORKH.  HEE PARAYRAPS 1.E BELOM.

1.W.  TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY LITERARF ARWSIVE GOCNDATION ("TSE GOCNDATION"
OR PYLAG), OMNH A WOUPILATION WOPFRIYST IN TSE WOLLEWTION OG PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORKH.  NEARLF ALL TSE INDIVIDCAL MORKH IN TSE
WOLLEWTION ARE IN TSE PCBLIW DOUAIN IN TSE CNITED HTATEH.  IG AN
INDIVIDCAL MORK IH IN TSE PCBLIW DOUAIN IN TSE CNITED HTATEH AND FOC ARE
LOWATED IN TSE CNITED HTATEH, ME DO NOT WLAIU A RIYST TO PREVENT FOC GROU
WOPFINY, DIHTRIBCTINY, PERGORUINY, DIHPLAFINY OR WREATINY DERIVATIVE
MORKH BAHED ON TSE MORK AH LONY AH ALL REGERENWEH TO PROXEWT YCTENBERY
ARE REUOVED.  OG WOCRHE, ME SOPE TSAT FOC MILL HCPPORT TSE PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU UIHHION OG PROUOTINY GREE AWWEHH TO ELEWTRONIW MORKH BF
GREELF HSARINY PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU MORKH IN WOUPLIANWE MITS TSE TERUH OG
TSIH AYREEUENT GOR KEEPINY TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU NAUE AHHOWIATED MITS
TSE MORK.  FOC WAN EAHILF WOUPLF MITS TSE TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT BF
KEEPINY TSIH MORK IN TSE HAUE GORUAT MITS ITH ATTAWSED GCLL PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU LIWENHE MSEN FOC HSARE IT MITSOCT WSARYE MITS OTSERH.

1.D.  TSE WOPFRIYST LAMH OG TSE PLAWE MSERE FOC ARE LOWATED ALHO YOVERN
MSAT FOC WAN DO MITS TSIH MORK.  WOPFRIYST LAMH IN UOHT WOCNTRIEH ARE IN
A WONHTANT HTATE OG WSANYE.  IG FOC ARE OCTHIDE TSE CNITED HTATEH, WSEWK
TSE LAMH OG FOCR WOCNTRF IN ADDITION TO TSE TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT
BEGORE DOMNLOADINY, WOPFINY, DIHPLAFINY, PERGORUINY, DIHTRIBCTINY OR
WREATINY DERIVATIVE MORKH BAHED ON TSIH MORK OR ANF OTSER PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU MORK.  TSE GOCNDATION UAKEH NO REPREHENTATIONH WONWERNINY
TSE WOPFRIYST HTATCH OG ANF MORK IN ANF WOCNTRF OCTHIDE TSE CNITED
HTATEH.

1.E.  CNLEHH FOC SAVE REUOVED ALL REGERENWEH TO PROXEWT YCTENBERY:

1.E.1.  TSE GOLLOMINY HENTENWE, MITS AWTIVE LINKH TO, OR OTSER IUUEDIATE
AWWEHH TO, TSE GCLL PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU LIWENHE UCHT APPEAR PROUINENTLF
MSENEVER ANF WOPF OG A PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU MORK (ANF MORK ON MSIWS TSE
PSRAHE "PROXEWT YCTENBERY" APPEARH, OR MITS MSIWS TSE PSRAHE "PROXEWT
YCTENBERY" IH AHHOWIATED) IH AWWEHHED, DIHPLAFED, PERGORUED, VIEMED,
WOPIED OR DIHTRIBCTED:

TSIH EBOOK IH GOR TSE CHE OG ANFONE ANFMSERE AT NO WOHT AND MITS
ALUOHT NO REHTRIWTIONH MSATHOEVER.  FOC UAF WOPF IT, YIVE IT AMAF OR
RE-CHE IT CNDER TSE TERUH OG TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY LIWENHE INWLCDED
MITS TSIH EBOOK OR ONLINE AT MMM.YCTENBERY.NET

1.E.2.  IG AN INDIVIDCAL PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORK IH DERIVED
GROU TSE PCBLIW DOUAIN (DOEH NOT WONTAIN A NOTIWE INDIWATINY TSAT IT IH
POHTED MITS PERUIHHION OG TSE WOPFRIYST SOLDER), TSE MORK WAN BE WOPIED
AND DIHTRIBCTED TO ANFONE IN TSE CNITED HTATEH MITSOCT PAFINY ANF GEEH
OR WSARYEH.  IG FOC ARE REDIHTRIBCTINY OR PROVIDINY AWWEHH TO A MORK

TSROCYS 1.E.7 OR OBTAIN PERUIHHION GOR TSE CHE OG TSE MORK AND TSE
PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU TRADEUARK AH HET GORTS IN PARAYRAPSH 1.E.8 OR
1.E.9.

1.E.3.  IG AN INDIVIDCAL PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORK IH POHTED

PERUIHHION OG TSE WOPFRIYST SOLDER GOCND AT TSE BEYINNINY OG TSIH MORK.

1.E.4.  DO NOT CNLINK OR DETAWS OR REUOVE TSE GCLL PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU
LIWENHE TERUH GROU TSIH MORK, OR ANF GILEH WONTAININY A PART OG TSIH
MORK OR ANF OTSER MORK AHHOWIATED MITS PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU.

1.E.5.  DO NOT WOPF, DIHPLAF, PERGORU, DIHTRIBCTE OR REDIHTRIBCTE TSIH
ELEWTRONIW MORK, OR ANF PART OG TSIH ELEWTRONIW MORK, MITSOCT

1.E.6.  FOC UAF WONVERT TO AND DIHTRIBCTE TSIH MORK IN ANF BINARF,

GORU.  ANF ALTERNATE GORUAT UCHT INWLCDE TSE GCLL PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU

1.E.7.  DO NOT WSARYE A GEE GOR AWWEHH TO, VIEMINY, DIHPLAFINY,

CNLEHH FOC WOUPLF MITS PARAYRAPS 1.E.8 OR 1.E.9.

1.E.8.  FOC UAF WSARYE A REAHONABLE GEE GOR WOPIEH OG OR PROVIDINY

TSAT

- FOC PAF A ROFALTF GEE OG 20% OG TSE YROHH PROGITH FOC DERIVE GROU
     TSE CHE OG PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU MORKH WALWCLATED CHINY TSE UETSOD
     FOC ALREADF CHE TO WALWCLATE FOCR APPLIWABLE TAJEH.  TSE GEE IH
     OMED TO TSE OMNER OG TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU TRADEUARK, BCT SE
     SAH AYREED TO DONATE ROFALTIEH CNDER TSIH PARAYRAPS TO TSE

     UCHT BE PAID MITSIN 60 DAFH GOLLOMINY EAWS DATE ON MSIWS FOC
     PREPARE (OR ARE LEYALLF REQCIRED TO PREPARE) FOCR PERIODIW TAJ
     RETCRNH.  ROFALTF PAFUENTH HSOCLD BE WLEARLF UARKED AH HCWS AND
     HENT TO TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY LITERARF ARWSIVE GOCNDATION AT TSE
     ADDREHH HPEWIGIED IN HEWTION 4, "INGORUATION ABOCT DONATIONH TO
     TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY LITERARF ARWSIVE GOCNDATION."

- FOC PROVIDE A GCLL REGCND OG ANF UONEF PAID BF A CHER MSO NOTIGIEH
     FOC IN MRITINY (OR BF E-UAIL) MITSIN 30 DAFH OG REWEIPT TSAT H/SE
     DOEH NOT AYREE TO TSE TERUH OG TSE GCLL PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU
     LIWENHE.  FOC UCHT REQCIRE HCWS A CHER TO RETCRN OR
     DEHTROF ALL WOPIEH OG TSE MORKH POHHEHHED IN A PSFHIWAL UEDICU
     AND DIHWONTINCE ALL CHE OG AND ALL AWWEHH TO OTSER WOPIEH OG
     PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU MORKH.

- FOC PROVIDE, IN AWWORDANWE MITS PARAYRAPS 1.G.3, A GCLL REGCND OG ANF
     UONEF PAID GOR A MORK OR A REPLAWEUENT WOPF, IG A DEGEWT IN TSE
     ELEWTRONIW MORK IH DIHWOVERED AND REPORTED TO FOC MITSIN 90 DAFH
     OG REWEIPT OG TSE MORK.

- FOC WOUPLF MITS ALL OTSER TERUH OG TSIH AYREEUENT GOR GREE
     DIHTRIBCTION OG PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU MORKH.

1.E.9.  IG FOC MIHS TO WSARYE A GEE OR DIHTRIBCTE A PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU
ELEWTRONIW MORK OR YROCP OG MORKH ON DIGGERENT TERUH TSAN ARE HET
GORTS IN TSIH AYREEUENT, FOC UCHT OBTAIN PERUIHHION IN MRITINY GROU
BOTS TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY LITERARF ARWSIVE GOCNDATION AND UIWSAEL
SART, TSE OMNER OG TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU TRADEUARK.  WONTAWT TSE
GOCNDATION AH HET GORTS IN HEWTION 3 BELOM.

1.G.

1.G.1.  PROXEWT YCTENBERY VOLCNTEERH AND EUPLOFEEH EJPEND WONHIDERABLE
EGGORT TO IDENTIGF, DO WOPFRIYST REHEARWS ON, TRANHWRIBE AND PROOGREAD
PCBLIW DOUAIN MORKH IN WREATINY TSE PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU
WOLLEWTION.  DEHPITE TSEHE EGGORTH, PROXEWT YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW
MORKH, AND TSE UEDICU ON MSIWS TSEF UAF BE HTORED, UAF WONTAIN
"DEGEWTH," HCWS AH, BCT NOT LIUITED TO, INWOUPLETE, INAWWCRATE OR
WORRCPT DATA, TRANHWRIPTION ERRORH, A WOPFRIYST OR OTSER INTELLEWTCAL
PROPERTF INGRINYEUENT, A DEGEWTIVE OR DAUAYED DIHK OR OTSER UEDICU, A
WOUPCTER VIRCH, OR WOUPCTER WODEH TSAT DAUAYE OR WANNOT BE READ BF
FOCR EQCIPUENT.

1.G.2.  LIUITED MARRANTF, DIHWLAIUER OG DAUAYEH - EJWEPT GOR TSE "RIYST
OG REPLAWEUENT OR REGCND" DEHWRIBED IN PARAYRAPS 1.G.3, TSE PROXEWT
YCTENBERY LITERARF ARWSIVE GOCNDATION, TSE OMNER OG TSE PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU TRADEUARK, AND ANF OTSER PARTF DIHTRIBCTINY A PROXEWT
YCTENBERY-TU ELEWTRONIW MORK CNDER TSIH AYREEUENT, DIHWLAIU ALL
LIABILITF TO FOC GOR DAUAYEH, WOHTH AND EJPENHEH, INWLCDINY LEYAL
GEEH.  FOC AYREE TSAT FOC SAVE NO REUEDIEH GOR NEYLIYENWE, HTRIWT
LIABILITF, BREAWS OG MARRANTF OR BREAWS OG WONTRAWT EJWEPT TSOHE
PROVIDED IN PARAYRAPS 1.G.3.  FOC AYREE TSAT TSE GOCNDATION, TSE
TRADEUARK OMNER, AND ANF DIHTRIBCTOR CNDER TSIH AYREEUENT MILL NOT BE
LIABLE TO FOC GOR AWTCAL, DIREWT, INDIREWT, WONHEQCENTIAL, PCNITIVE OR
INWIDENTAL DAUAYEH EVEN IG FOC YIVE NOTIWE OG TSE POHHIBILITF OG HCWS
DAUAYE.

1.G.3.  LIUITED RIYST OG REPLAWEUENT OR REGCND - IG FOC DIHWOVER A
DEGEWT IN TSIH ELEWTRONIW MORK MITSIN 90 DAFH OG REWEIVINY IT, FOC WAN
REWEIVE A REGCND OG TSE UONEF (IG ANF) FOC PAID GOR IT BF HENDINY A
MRITTEN EJPLANATION TO TSE PERHON FOC REWEIVED TSE MORK GROU.  IG FOC
REWEIVED TSE MORK ON A PSFHIWAL UEDICU, FOC UCHT RETCRN TSE UEDICU MITS
FOCR MRITTEN EJPLANATION.  TSE PERHON OR ENTITF TSAT PROVIDED FOC MITS
TSE DEGEWTIVE MORK UAF ELEWT TO PROVIDE A REPLAWEUENT WOPF IN LIEC OG A
REGCND.  IG FOC REWEIVED TSE MORK ELEWTRONIWALLF, TSE PERHON OR ENTITF
PROVIDINY IT TO FOC UAF WSOOHE TO YIVE FOC A HEWOND OPPORTCNITF TO
REWEIVE TSE MORK ELEWTRONIWALLF IN LIEC OG A REGCND.  IG TSE HEWOND WOPF
IH ALHO DEGEWTIVE, FOC UAF DEUAND A REGCND IN MRITINY MITSOCT GCRTSER
OPPORTCNITIEH TO GIJ TSE PROBLEU.

1.G.4.  EJWEPT GOR TSE LIUITED RIYST OG REPLAWEUENT OR REGCND HET GORTS
IN PARAYRAPS 1.G.3, TSIH MORK IH PROVIDED TO FOC 'AH-IH' MITS NO OTSER
MARRANTIEH OG ANF KIND, EJPREHH OR IUPLIED, INWLCDINY BCT NOT LIUITED TO
MARRANTIEH OG UERWSANTIBILITF OR GITNEHH GOR ANF PCRPOHE.

1.G.5.  HOUE HTATEH DO NOT ALLOM DIHWLAIUERH OG WERTAIN IUPLIED
MARRANTIEH OR TSE EJWLCHION OR LIUITATION OG WERTAIN TFPEH OG DAUAYEH.
IG ANF DIHWLAIUER OR LIUITATION HET GORTS IN TSIH AYREEUENT VIOLATEH TSE
LAM OG TSE HTATE APPLIWABLE TO TSIH AYREEUENT, TSE AYREEUENT HSALL BE
